Svi' t'nash-veh younger heh weht vulnerable tevun t'nash-veh sa-mekh mazhiv-kur-tor me ein na'shikh ik i’ve vesh' turning abru' svi' t'nash-veh kashek ek'wak opi'. “whenever du olau spo' criticizing sovek-veh, ” au var-tor me, “aishan vokau ik ek' wuh sutra svi' nash panu haven’t had wuh advantages ik du’ve had.” au didn’t leralmin sovek weht, tonk'peh etek’ve kwon-hau-ov vesh' unusually communicative svi' wuh reserved yut, heh i ken-tor ik au tvai wuh lo'uk deal weht do ik. Svi' consequence, i’m vul-tor tor reserve ek' judgements, wuh es'merka ik has tu'ash abru wehk curious natures tor me heh isha tor me wuh shi-kar-tor t' ri wuh zamu veteran bores. Wuh ritsuri kashek nam-tor sahris tor patal-tor heh attach itself tor nash quality lu ish-veh saudau svi' wuh tsuri person, heh ni sarlah ish-veh pa' ik svi' college i vesh' unjustly accused t' hasu wuh politician, fai'ei i vesh' privy tor wuh tsat griefs t' kwai, ri-fainu sasu. Danik t' wuh confidences vesh' unsought—frequently i ma vup-tor yuk, preoccupation, il wuh hostile levity lu i realized k' ein unmistakable glat ik wuh intimate revelation vesh' quivering fi' wuh ir-zehl; na' wuh intimate revelations t' nu'ri sasu, il k'puu wuh zhil svi' if au sagluvau au, nam-tor usually plagiaristic heh marred k' obvious suppressions. Reserving judgements nam-tor wuh tukh t' vaik rok. I am fam dvun wuh pi' kwes t' missing vel kuv i yen-tor ik, u' t'nash-veh sa-mekh snobbishly suggested, heh i snobbishly ashiv-tor, wuh kash-ral t' wuh nenik decencies nam-tor parcelled si' unequally na' keshtan. Heh, po' boasting nash yut t' t'nash-veh wivel'es, sarlah nash-veh tor wuh admission ik ish-veh has wuh grei. Spa-tor lau nam-tor founded fi' wuh lerash kov il wuh masupik masu-kastra, tonk'peh po' wuh ac'ruth sfek i don’t tun ra ish-veh’s founded fi'. Lu vesht sarlah nash-veh pla' s' wuh she'rak kim-shah tasmin i olau ik i aitlu wuh panu tor nam-tor svi' uniform heh na' wuh wihfelau t' moral attention ek'wak; i aitlu rai weht riotous excursions k' privileged glimpses vi' wuh komihn khaf-spol. Goh gatsby, wuh sasu vi mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ahm tor nash dunap, vesh' exempt s' t'nash-veh rolaya—gatsby, vi represented kanok-vei na' if i ma wuh unaffected scorn. Kuv nafu'es nam-tor wuh unbroken weizehl t' successful gestures, yi tra' vesh' vel gorgeous pa' ish-veh, ein heightened sensitivity tor wuh ugau t' ha'kiv, u' kuv au vesh' related tor veh t' eifa intricate mish-vel ik register solektra-hutaya lehkuh thousand miles maf. Nash responsiveness had nothing tor tor k' ik flabby impressionability if nam-tor dignified ne' wuh ahm t' wuh “fereik temperament”—ish-veh vesh' wuh wehtsuri mazhiv-kur na' rok, wuh romantic readiness such u' i ma worla afer-tor svi' sovek vath person heh if ish-veh nam-tor ri kesik i dungau ek'wak talal va'ashiv. Rai—gatsby da-tor si' ek' gas'rak na' wuh shaht; ish-veh nam-tor ra preyed fi' gatsby, ra flalik grazhiv markau svi' wuh wake t' ish-veh sahr-tor-tor ik temporarily a'ing si' t'nash-veh eku'ko svi' wuh abortive sorrows heh pen-kuvor-tor elations t' sasu. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ t'nash-veh skan ma vesh' prominent, muhl-tor-tor sutra svi' nash svitan western kahr na' rehkuh generations. Wuh carraways nam-tor vel t' wuh maat, heh etek ma wuh ba'tak ik etek’re tev-tor s' wuh dukes t' buccleuch, tonk'peh wuh actual afersu t' t'nash-veh zehl vesh' t'nash-veh sa'mekh'al’s sa-kai, vi sarlah la' svi' kau-leh-veh, satau wuh substitute tor wuh civil t'naehm, heh palikau wuh wholesale hardware business ik t'nash-veh sa-mekh lesh fi' nash-gad. I worla gla-tor nash lo'uk-sa-kuk, tonk'peh i’m supposed tor glazhau spo' ish-veh—k' special dzhinaya tor wuh rather lerash-kan-tor krasan ik geldau svi' sa-mekh’s office. I graduated s' uzh haven svi' 1915, aishan wuh yonuk t' wuh century po' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, heh wuh pi' later i participated svi' ik vohtau teutonic bashan fainu u' wuh lo'uk t'naehm. I tizh-tor wuh tumek-raid ni thoroughly ik vesht sarlah nash-veh pla' restless. Instead t' hasu wuh lamekh centre t' wuh panu, wuh svitan tev'rak i' seemed spo' wuh ragged rihk t' wuh stukhtra—ni i klopau tor hal-tor she'rak heh oren-tor wuh tel-tor business. Kanok-veh i fai-tor vesh' svi' wuh tel-tor business, ni i supposed ish-veh kupi nenikaya veh weht single sasu. Ek' t'nash-veh ezyet heh sa-kuk variben ish-veh abru' u' kuv au vesh' choosing wuh prep shi'oren na' me, heh t'forti leralmin-tor, “po—ye-es, ” k' maut shi'vukhut, hesitant limuk. Sa-mekh sep-wafikh tor donkes-tor me na' wuh tevun, heh po' vuhnauk vohtau vesht sarlah nash-veh she'rak, permanently, i nahp, svi' wuh sikar t' dah-leh-dahkuh. Wuh practical vel vesh' tor talal tvi-shal svi' wuh kahr, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh lamekh tevun-yonuk, heh i had aishan losrak wuh shasol t' eik yartra heh friendly lap, ni lu wuh nu'ri sasu na' wuh office suggested ik etek nem-tor wuh kelek teretuhr svi' wuh commuting kahr, ish-veh sounded spo' wuh lo'uk idea. Au afer-tor wuh kelek, wuh igen-va-beaten cardboard bungalow na' oh-leh wuh tevun-krus, tonk'peh na' wuh kim-shah minute wuh pesik ordered ish-veh tor washington, heh i went si' tor wuh shasol sa'awek. I had wuh dog—k'puu i had ish-veh na' wuh zamu gad abi' au sahr-tor maf—heh wuh hinek sayutau heh wuh finnish kosu, vi tor t'nash-veh sar-tak heh pufas-tor asal-yem heh muttered finnish kau tor herself abru' wuh rafik stove. Ish-veh vesh' lonely na' wuh gad il ni abi' veh asal ein sasu, weht recently lasha do i, pehkau me fi' wuh fau-yut. “uf tor du prah tor tev'rak yu-mur pi'kahr?” au ya'akash helplessly. I var-tor ish-veh. Heh u' i lates-tor fi' i vesh' lonely rai longer. I vesh' wuh kakhartausu, wuh pathfinder, wuh tveshik settler. Au had casually conferred fi' me wuh el'es t' wuh neighbourhood. Heh ni k' wuh sunshine heh wuh lo'uk thorau t' mor growing fi' wuh lap, aishan u' vel tor'ovau svi' sahris movies, i had ik familiar conviction ik ha'kiv vesh' palikaya abru' va'ashiv k' wuh belaar. Tra' vesh' ni mau tor telv-tor, na' veh vel, heh ni mau tok-ti muhl'es tor nam-tor seshau ne' s' wuh nu'ri esh-giving sov. I bought wuh dozen mog'es fi' banking heh lit heh investment shar'es, heh au lam-tor fi' t'nash-veh nef svi' yon-kur heh pi-maat-tukh spo' uzh donku s' wuh mint, promising tor unfold wuh shining tsat ik goh midas heh morgan heh maecenas fai-tor. Heh i had wuh pid intention t' telvan wehk vath dunap isha. I vesh' rather literary svi' college—veh tevun i kitau wuh weizehl t' maut solemn heh obvious editorials na' wuh yale ro'fori—heh i' i vesh' going tor katau pla' ek' such vel vi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv heh shetau va'ashiv ik danik limited t' ek' specialists, wuh “muhl-rounded sasu.” nash isn’t aishan wuh epigram—ha'kiv nam-tor mau weht successfully glazhau na' s' wuh single krani, po' ek'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tukh t' pavesh ik i dang ma rented wuh kelek svi' veh t' wuh strangest shila svi' desh'rak america. Ish-veh vesh' fi' ik slender riotous vikuvtra if sadvun-tor itself due she'rak t' uzh york—heh wilat tra' nam-tor, among vath malatik curiosities, dahkuh ritsuri shidoraya t' solektra. Dah-leh miles s' wuh kahr wuh shif t' masuk' yu-mur, ka svi' contour heh dahshau goh k' wuh nuhk'es tchol, jut si' vi' wuh danik ha'kelikau ak'shem t' alem masu svi' wuh western hemisphere, wuh lo'uk masupik barnyard t' wu vikuvtra ralash. Au nam-tor ri buhfik yuvik—spo' wuh yu-mur svi' wuh columbus var, au nam-tor fi' plesh-tor pa'ash na' wuh contact shaht—tonk'peh ish-veh tukhik resemblance bolau nam-tor wuh shu-pal t' perpetual wonder tor wuh gulls ik hash-tor overhead. Tor wuh wingless wuh weht eku'ki stivan nam-tor ish-veh dissimilarity svi' kanok particular kaula shid heh suk'es. I ha-tor na' tev'rak yu-mur, wuh—muhl, wuh lehkuh fashionable t' wuh dahkuh, hi nash nam-tor wuh danik superficial tag tor sagluvau wuh bizarre heh ri wuh pi' sinister contrast svi' au. T'nash-veh kelek vesh' na' wuh maut um t' wuh yu-mur, goh kau-leh ker s' wuh ralash, heh lerakhovau svi' dahkuh masuk' shitau ik rented na' leh-dah il leh-kau thousand wuh tevun-yonuk. Wuh veh fi' t'nash-veh gas'rak vesh' wuh colossal tek'ik k' sovek standard—ish-veh vesh' wuh kla-minik imitation t' ein hôtel de ville svi' normandy, k' wuh kispek fi' veh vla, spanking uzh ne' wuh wonil hisahk t' raw ivy, heh wuh marble mahalan patra, heh weht do keh-leh acres t' yartra heh bah-ker. Ish-veh vesh' gatsby’s mansion. Il, rather, u' i didn’t fai-tor mr. Gatsby, ish-veh vesh' wuh mansion inhabited k' wuh gentleman t' ik ahm. T'nash-veh sha' kelek vesh' wuh eyesore, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh pi' eyesore, heh ish-veh had vesh' overlooked, ni i had wuh zan-tor t' wuh masu, wuh ulik zan-tor t' t'nash-veh behsu’s yartra, heh wuh consoling be'es t' millionaires—ek' na' oh-leh dollars wuh tevun-krus. Mes' wuh nuhk'es tchol wuh wan-kur palaces t' fashionable she'rak yu-mur glittered bi' wuh masu, heh wuh vesht-var t' wuh belaar really palikau fi' wuh khru i drove abru' tra' ki' aru-yem k' wuh tom buchanans. Daisy vesh' t'nash-veh dahr krei wuh'wak snem-tor, heh i’d fainu tom svi' college. Heh aishan po' wuh t'naehm i spent dahkuh gad k' au svi' chicago. Ish-veh sa-telsu, among vuhnauk tukhik accomplishments, had vesh' veh t' wuh danik powerful shahtau ik ek'wak mavau football na' uzh haven—wuh national khlop svi' wuh yut, veh t' eifa sasu vi pulau such wuh zat limited marom'es na' dah-leh-veh ik kanok-vei afterward savours t' anticlimax. Ish-veh skan vesh' enormously wealthy—kauk svi' college ish-veh el'es k' donku vesh' wuh tukh na' reproach—tonk'peh i' au’d losrak chicago heh sarlah she'rak svi' wuh fashion ik rather nem-tor ish-veh esh maf: na' instance, au’d katau ne' wuh string t' polo ponies s' suk'muzh laptra. Ish-veh vesh' lerash tor realize ik wuh sasu svi' t'nash-veh sha' generation vesh' wealthy hiyet tor tor ik. Po sarlah au she'rak i don’t fai-tor. Au had spent wuh tevun svi' france na' rai particular utvau, heh yi marau la' heh tra' unrestfully wherever sutra mavau polo heh vesh' don-ka teretuhr. Nash vesh' wuh permanent dvun, leralmin-tor daisy abru' wuh telephone, tonk'peh i didn’t dva-tor ish-veh—i had rai glan vi' daisy’s khaf-spol, tonk'peh i olau ik tom would maraya fi' ek'wak seeking, wuh pi' wistfully, na' wuh dramatic wauk t' ein irrecoverable football zhagra. Heh ni ish-veh pavesh-tor ik fi' wuh lamekh salanayik khru i drove abru' tor she'rak yu-mur tor gla-tor dahkuh hinek t'hylara ik i scarcely fai-tor na' ek'. Ish-veh kelek vesh' kauk weht elaborate do i gishu, wuh cheerful yon-kur-heh-wan-kur georgian colonial mansion, overlooking wuh tchol. Wuh yartra palikau na' wuh shahov heh sahr-tor na' wuh khom svep na' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile, jumping abru' sundials heh dok lates-tor heh yontau bah-ker—t'forti lu ish-veh pulau wuh kelek drifting abru wuh vla svi' ugelik kas-elakh u' hi s' wuh dvunelinak t' its sahr-tor. Wuh khom vesh' pushau k' wuh zehl t' french krani, glowing i' k' haul-tor pi-maat-tukh heh eik tu'ash tor wuh lamekh salanayik aru, heh tom buchanan svi' riding sai-vel vesh' standing k' ish-veh mal k'wuhli fi' wuh khom porch. Au had rubai opi' ish-veh uzh haven tevun. I' au vesh' wuh batai terp-haired sasu t' reh-leh, k' wuh rather lerash ru'lut heh wuh supercilious manner. Dahkuh shining arrogant bezhun had afer-tor abru'es abru' ish-veh limuk heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh appearance t' kwon-hau-ov leaning aggressively fa'rak. Ri kauk wuh effeminate swank t' ish-veh riding sai-vel kupi ip-sut wuh masuk' tepul t' ik ak'shem—au seemed tor boshaya eifa glistening kluf abi' au ish-veh-tor wuh fik lacing, heh du kupi gla-tor wuh lo'uk sa'haf t' dvunek shifting lu ish-veh tipan dvun-tor ne' ish-veh wonil tor-pal. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ak'shem capable t' masuk' leverage—wuh pi-maat'rer ak'shem. Ish-veh speaking spes, wuh gruff husky tenor, hau tor wuh impression t' fractiousness au zhelesh. Tra' vesh' wuh esta t' paternal contempt svi' ish-veh, kauk na' sutra au tishau—heh tra' vesh' sasu na' uzh haven vi had fnu-ven ish-veh guts. “i', don’t nah-tor t'nash-veh opinion fi' aifa tukh nam-tor kim-shah, ” au seemed tor leralmin, “aishan fai'ei i’m stronger heh weht t' wuh sasu do du nam-tor.” etek vesh' svi' wuh ka senior shila'es, heh du' etek vesh' worla intimate i kwon-hau-ov had wuh impression ik au messau t' me heh aitlu me tor spo' ish-veh k' ein harsh, defiant wistfulness t' ish-veh sha'. Etek variben na' wuh zamu minutes fi' wuh ka'ug'yelik porch. “i’ve prah wuh nice shi la', ” au leralmin-tor, ish-veh bezhun flashing pa' restlessly. Turning me pa' k' veh kar, au dvun-tor wuh sax'ksei pa'ash el'ru bi' wuh khom vista, including svi' its fnashtaya wuh sunken italian bah-ker, wuh ulef acre t' glu, pungent roses, heh wuh snub-nosed motorboat ik bumped wuh mashen sagefik. “ish-veh belonged tor demaine, wuh elmin sasu.” au da-tor me pa' va'ashiv, politely heh abruptly. “etek’ll hal-tor svi'udish.” etek lates-tor k'fai wuh pid tvur vi' wuh ugelik rosy-kur-tor ret, fragilely bound vi' wuh kelek k' french krani na' either shaht. Wuh krani vesh' ajar heh gleaming wan-kur tehnat wuh sluk yar s'udish ik seemed tor tor'ovau wuh pi' yut vi' wuh kelek. Wuh pi'salan blew k'fai wuh tvi-shal, blew curtains svi' na' veh shaht heh si' wuh vath spo' spoh haifan, kuvoran-tor au abru na' wuh le-su wedding-cake t' wuh abru-tol, heh yi rippled abru' wuh wine-kur-tor la'y, tor wuh duv fi' ish-veh u' salan tor fi' wuh masutra. Wuh goh completely stationary vel svi' wuh tvi-shal vesh' wuh masuk' ku-san fi' if dahkuh nu'ri kosu vesh' buoyed abru u' hi fi-tor wuh anchored sov-dukal. Au vesh' fi' svi' wan-kur, heh ish-veh sai-vel vesh' rippling heh fluttering u' kuv au had aishan vesh' blown pla' svi' po' wuh pen hash pa' wuh kelek. I bolau ma lam-tor na' wuh zamu moments listening tor wuh wonil-zehl heh snap t' wuh curtains heh wuh groan t' wuh bikuv fi' wuh temok. Yi tra' vesh' wuh ork u' tom buchanan ikap-tor wuh za' krani heh wuh kum-tor salan tev-tor si' pa' wuh tvi-shal, heh wuh curtains heh wuh la'y heh wuh dahkuh nu'ri kosu ballooned slowly tor wuh lan-tol. Wuh younger t' wuh dahkuh vesh' wuh ri-fainusu tor me. She vesh' sadvun-tor bosh wu-vath na' ish-veh shaht t' wuh divan, completely motionless, heh k' ish-veh chin ashenau wuh pi', u' kuv she vesh' balancing vel fi' ish-veh if vesh' ved kesik tor tevan. Kuv gla-tor ish-veh me s' wuh teruk t' ish-veh bezhun she mazhiv-kur-tor rai hint t' ish-veh—indeed, i vesh' siyah ak'wikmun vi' murmuring wuh apology na' having ertau ish-veh k' coming svi'. Wuh vath ko-kan, daisy, tor wuh attempt tor shen—she gal-tor slightly fa'rak k' wuh conscientious sagluvaya—yi she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, wuh absurd, sem-rik-tor pi' abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh i abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor nuh' heh sarlah fa'rak vi' wuh tvi-shal. “i’m p-shivau k' happiness.” she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor va'ashiv, u' kuv she leralmin-tor vel maut witty, heh meskarau t'nash-veh el'ru na' wuh moment, looking abru vi' t'nash-veh limuk, promising ik tra' vesh' kling svi' wuh panu she ni mau aitlu tor gla-tor. Ik vesh' wuh yut she had. She hinted svi' wuh murmur ik wuh surname t' wuh balancing ko-kan vesh' leipausu. (i’ve puzhu-tor ish-veh leralmin-tor ik daisy’s murmur vesh' goh tor tor sutra galat na' ish-veh; wuh irrelevant criticism ik tor ish-veh rai lehkuh sem-rik-tor.) na' sovek tav, din-tor leipausu’s bru-lar nuv-tor, she nodded na' me siyah imperceptibly, heh yi sahris tipped ish-veh patam pla' va'ashiv—wuh vel she vesh' balancing had obviously tottered wuh pi' heh putan-tor ish-veh vel t' wuh kolthak. Va'ashiv wuh wihfelau t' apology arose tor t'nash-veh bru-lar. Siyah sovek exhibition t' ovsotik shal-sufficiency bes-tor wuh kovtulik tribute s' me. I glazhau pla' na' t'nash-veh krei, vi began tor ya'akash me deshkau svi' ish-veh neik, thrilling spes. Ish-veh vesh' wuh ves t' spes ik wuh kaluk zahal-tor abru heh ne', u' kuv tik starun nam-tor wuh arrangement t' pitoh ik dungi worla nam-tor mavau va'ashiv. Ish-veh limuk vesh' maf heh lovely k' ugelik vel svi' ish-veh, ugelik bezhun heh wuh ugelik passionate ru'lut, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh tepor'es svi' ish-veh spes ik sasu vi had palutunau ish-veh afer-tor rihagik tor yen-tor: wuh uralaun riyeht-aitlun, wuh zhal-tor “shroi, ” wuh ugaya ik she had ovsoh sa-ka-ashausu, teporilauk vel aishan wuh du' opi' heh ik tra' vesh' sa-ka-ashausu, teporilauk vel hovering svi' wuh thurai wadan. I var-tor ish-veh uf i had pehkau ska' svi' chicago na' wuh gad fi' t'nash-veh yut she'rak, heh uf wuh dozen sutra had satau ish-veh ashaya k'fai me. “tor au din-tor me?” she maf-tor ecstatically. “wuh bosh kahr nam-tor desolate. Ek' wuh poiq'lid ma wuh losrak za' halek kras-tor nesh-kur u' wuh mourning wreath, heh tra'’s wuh persistent wail ek' mu-yor bi' wuh desh'rak gef.” “uf gorgeous! Kal-tor’s hal-tor pla', tom. Fa-gad!” yi she hau irrelevantly: “du ought tor gla-tor wuh kan-bu.” “i’d spo' tor.” “she’s asleep. She’s rehkuh tevun hinek. Haven’t du ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh?” “worla.” “muhl, du ought tor gla-tor ish-veh. She’s—” tom buchanan, vi had vesh' hovering restlessly pa' wuh tvi-shal, pehkau heh shom-tor ish-veh el'ru fi' t'nash-veh tipan. “ra du doing, nick?” “i’m wuh tel-tor sasu.” “vi k'?” i var-tor ish-veh. “worla puzhu-tor t' au, ” au remarked decisively. Nash annoyed me. “du dungi, ” i kilko-tor shortly. “du dungi kuv du stay svi' wuh she'rak.” “oh, i’ll stay svi' wuh she'rak, don’t du worry, ” au leralmin-tor, glancing na' daisy heh yi pla' na' me, u' kuv au vesh' alert na' vel weht. “i’d nam-tor wuh oekon damned duhsu tor ha-tor sovek-wilat else.” na' nash sfek din-tor leipausu leralmin-tor: “absolutely!” k' such suddenness ik i palikau—ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak zhit she had uttered opi' vesht sarlah nash-veh vi' wuh tvi-shal. Evidently ish-veh ak'wikmun ish-veh u' mau u' ish-veh did me, na' she luvau heh k' wuh weizehl t' rapid, deft dvun lam-tor abru vi' wuh tvi-shal. “i’m stegel, ” she complained, “i’ve vesh' lying fi' ik ku-san na' u' wu u' i mokuhlek vokau.” “don’t glazhau na' me, ” daisy retorted, “i’ve vesh' trying tor prah du tor uzh york ek' aru.” “rai, itaren, ” leralmin-tor din-tor leipausu tor wuh kehkuh cocktails aishan svi' s' wuh pantry. “i’m absolutely svi' training.” ish-veh kasu glazhau na' ish-veh incredulously. “du nam-tor!” au nem-tor ne' ish-veh mon u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh eku svi' wuh lanet t' wuh makh. “uf du ek'wak prah sovek-vel ovsoh nam-tor mesakh me.” i glazhau na' din-tor leipausu, wondering ra ish-veh vesh' she “prah ovsoh.” i tizh-tor looking na' ish-veh. She vesh' wuh slender, pi'-breasted ko-kan, k' wuh abru-tor carriage, if she accentuated k' throwing ish-veh ak'shem pla'rak na' wuh tipan spo' wuh nu'ri ne-lan. Ish-veh zhai-kur yel-ish-veh-tor bezhun glazhau pla' na' me k' polite meskulanik curiosity s' wuh wan, sem-rik-tor, discontented limuk. Ish-veh paresh-tor tor me i' ik i had gla-tor ish-veh, il wuh bikuv t' ish-veh, ein-wilat fa'. “du ha-tor svi' tev'rak yu-mur, ” she remarked contemptuously. “i fai-tor somebody tra'.” “i don’t fai-tor wuh single—” “du bolau fai-tor gatsby.” “gatsby?” halishau daisy. “ra gatsby?” fa' i kupi kilko ik au vesh' t'nash-veh behsu aru-yem vesh' tor'pra; wedging ish-veh wis kar imperatively ne' t'nash-veh, tom buchanan compelled me s' wuh tvi-shal u' hi au vesh' dvun-tor wuh checker tor wuh'ashiv keh-vla. Slenderly, languidly, ish-veh el'ru eku lightly fi' ish-veh gaf, wuh dahkuh nu'ri kosu preceded etek si' fi' tor wuh rosy-kur-tor porch, tu'ash na' wuh tev-tor, wilat kehkuh ha'fek hanuvau fi' wuh pasu svi' wuh nelau salan. “po ha'fek?” kluchi daisy, frowning. She snapped au si' k' ish-veh ozh. “svi' dahkuh wehk gad ish-veh’ll nam-tor wuh longest gad svi' wuh tevun.” she glazhau na' etek ek' radiantly. “tor du kwon-hau-ov glantau na' wuh longest gad t' wuh tevun heh yi din-tor ish-veh? I kwon-hau-ov glantau na' wuh longest gad svi' wuh tevun heh yi din-tor ish-veh.” “etek ought tor dotor vel, ” luvau din-tor leipausu, sitting ne' na' wuh pasu u' kuv she vesh' getting vi' sar-tak. “ek' gas'rak, ” leralmin-tor daisy. “ra’ll etek dotor?” she da-tor tor me helplessly: “ra tor sutra dotor?” fa' i kupi kilko-srashiv ish-veh bezhun terau k' wuh putesha sagluvaya fi' ish-veh wuhr-ozh. “glazhau!” she complained; “i dash-tor ish-veh.” etek ek' glazhau—wuh ozh-lesek vesh' nesh-kur heh pla-kur. “du did ish-veh, tom, ” she leralmin-tor accusingly. “i fai-tor du didn’t tvai tor, tonk'peh du did tor ish-veh. Ik’s ra i prah na' marrying wuh brute t' wuh sasu, wuh lo'uk, suk', hulking tukhik specimen t' wuh—” “i fnu-ven ik zhit ‘hulking, ’ ” kluchi tom crossly, “kauk svi' kidding.” “hulking, ” insisted daisy. Sometimes she heh din-tor leipausu variben na' wuh'wak, unobtrusively heh k' wuh bantering inconsequence ik vesh' worla ved chatter, ik vesh' u' samuyau u' ish-veh wan-kur sai-vel heh ish-veh impersonal bezhun svi' wuh k'torr ek' aitlun. Au vesh' la', heh au nar-tor tom heh me, tor goh wuh polite vaksurik urgam tor entertain il tor nam-tor entertained. Au fai-tor ik presently aru-yem would nam-tor abru' heh wuh pi' later wuh khru nuh' would nam-tor abru' heh casually shitau maf. Ish-veh vesh' sharply natya s' wuh tev'rak, wilat wuh khru vesh' hurried s' wek tor wek na' its ikap-tor, svi' wuh continually disappointed anticipation il else svi' sheer nervous dread t' wuh moment itself. “du tor me olau uncivilized, daisy, ” i confessed fi' t'nash-veh dahr makh t' corky tonk'peh rather impressive claret. “mokuhlek’t du variben pa' urozh il vel?” i tvai nothing svi' particular k' nash remark, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' taken abru svi' wuh ri-gishu yut. “sutenivaya’s going tor krus, ” shau si' tom violently. “i’ve gotten tor nam-tor wuh terrible pessimist pa' vel. Ma du telv-tor wuh shen t' wuh kur-tor eik-te'kru k' nash sasu goddard?” “po, rai, ” i kilko-tor, rather ak'wikmun k' ish-veh molu. “muhl, ish-veh’s wuh tok-ti dunap, heh kanok-veh ought tor telv-tor ish-veh. Wuh idea nam-tor kuv etek don’t glazhau si' wuh wan-kur ne-koshtri dungi nam-tor—dungi nam-tor utterly submerged. Ish-veh’s ek' talik tukh; ish-veh’s vesh' skan-tor.” “tom’s getting maut profound, ” leralmin-tor daisy, k' wuh sagluvaya t' unthoughtful sadness. “au telv-tor glu dunap k' wu zhit svi' au. Ra vesh' ik zhit etek—” “muhl, aifa dunap nam-tor ek' talik, ” insisted tom, glancing na' ish-veh impatiently. “nash katravahsu has ar'kada si' wuh bosh vel. Ish-veh’s abru tor etek, vi nam-tor wuh abrupik ne-koshtri, tor glantau si' il aifa vath ne-koshtri dungi ma tash t' vel.” “etek’ve prah tor kuhsh-tor au ne', ” zhal-tor daisy, winking ferociously na' wuh fervent yel. “du ought tor ha-tor svi' california—” began din-tor leipausu, tonk'peh tom svi-shau ish-veh k' shifting heavily svi' ish-veh ku-san. “nash idea nam-tor ik etek’re nordics. I am, heh du nam-tor, heh du nam-tor, heh—” po' wuh infinitesimal vaunah au vinan-tor daisy k' wuh slight nod, heh she winked na' me va'ashiv. “—heh etek’ve torvau ek' wuh vel ik hal-tor tor tor sutenivaya—oh, ek'tal heh tanaf, heh ek' ik. Tor gla-tor du?” tra' vesh' vel pathetic svi' ish-veh concentration, u' kuv ish-veh complacency, weht zat do t' hinek, vesh' ri hiyet tor ish-veh sovek weht. Lu, siyah iyi, wuh telephone rang svi'udish heh wuh butler losrak wuh porch daisy seized fi-tor wuh momentary svi-shaya heh gal-tor na' me. “i’ll var-tor du wuh skan tsat, ” she zhal-tor enthusiastically. “ish-veh’s pa' wuh butler’s han. Tor du aitlun tor zhu-tor pa' wuh butler’s han?” “ik’s po vesht sarlah nash-veh abru' tonight.” “muhl, au wasn’t kwon-hau-ov wuh butler; au nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor wuh haul-tukh polisher na' ein sutra svi' uzh york ik had wuh haul-tukh dvin na' dah-teh sutra. Au had tor polish ish-veh s' asal till mu-yor, abi' t'forti ish-veh began tor dau ish-veh han—” “vel went s' rasahkos tor weh-rasahkos, ” suggested din-tor leipausu. “ha. Vel went s' rasahkos tor weh-rasahkos, abi' t'forti au had tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru ish-veh shul.” na' wuh moment wuh kim-shah sunshine tevan-tor k' romantic affection fi-tor ish-veh glowing limuk; ish-veh spes compelled me fa'rak breathlessly u' i shroi—yi wuh min spoh-tor, tik ta'hal deserting ish-veh k' svizh-tor regret, spo' kanu leaving wuh vaksurik yut na' dusk. Wuh butler sarlah pla' heh murmured vel beyik tom’s kaluk, whereupon tom kwal-tor, kwitau pla' ish-veh ku-san, heh rik' wuh zhit went svi'udish. U' kuv ish-veh absence quickened vel k'svi ish-veh, daisy gal-tor fa'rak va'ashiv, ish-veh spes glowing heh uralaun. “i ashaya tor gla-tor du na' t'nash-veh pasu, nick. Du remind me t' wuh—t' wuh she-tor, wuh ek'esik she-tor. Doesn’t au?” she da-tor tor din-tor leipausu na' wugaya: “wuh ek'esik she-tor?” nash vesh' untrue. I am ri kauk faintly spo' wuh she-tor. She vesh' goh extemporizing, tonk'peh wuh stirring warmth yumau s' ish-veh, u' kuv ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' trying tor sasarlah tor du ip-sut svi' veh t' eifa breathless, thrilling zhit. Yi suddenly she threw ish-veh ru'lut-sai fi' wuh pasu heh tobeg-tor herself heh went vi' wuh kelek. Din-tor leipausu heh i di'kizh-tor wuh pen glance consciously devoid t' meaning. I vesh' pa' tor stariben lu she hayal-tor abru alertly heh leralmin-tor “sh!” svi' wuh warning spes. Wuh nessau impassioned murmur vesh' zhu-yehat svi' wuh tvi-shal mesakh, heh din-tor leipausu gal-tor fa'rak unashamed, trying tor zhu-tor. Wuh murmur trembled fi' wuh verge t' coherence, sank ne', mounted excitedly, heh yi ceased altogether. “nash mr. Gatsby du stariben t' nam-tor t'nash-veh behsu—” i began. “don’t variben. I aitlun tor zhu-tor ra pavesh-tor.” “nam-tor vel aisha?” i inquired innocently. “du tvai tor leralmin du don’t fai-tor?” leralmin-tor din-tor leipausu, honestly ak'wikmun. “i nahp kanok-veh fai-tor.” “i don’t.” “po—” she leralmin-tor hesitantly. “tom’s prah ein kosu svi' uzh york.” “prah ein kosu?” i ashiv-tor blankly. Din-tor leipausu nodded. “she lau ma wuh decency ri tor telephone ish-veh na' aru-yem wak. Don’t du nah-tor?” siyah fa' i had ruskarau ish-veh meaning tra' vesh' wuh nuv t' wuh sai-vel heh wuh crunch t' duf kluf, heh tom heh daisy vesh' pla' na' wuh pasu. “ish-veh couldn’t nam-tor gol-tor!” maf-tor daisy k' wis gaiety. She hayal-tor ne', glanced searchingly na' din-tor leipausu heh yi na' me, heh fator: “i glazhau outdoors na' wuh minute, heh ish-veh’s maut romantic outdoors. Tra'’s wuh kushel fi' wuh yartra ik i nah-tor bolau nam-tor wuh nightingale sarlah abru' fi' wuh cunard il wan-kur yel zehl. Au’s uralaun maf—” ish-veh spes sang: “ish-veh’s romantic, isn’t ish-veh, tom?” “maut romantic, ” au leralmin-tor, heh yi miserably tor me: “kuv ish-veh’s ta'hal hiyet po' aru-yem, i aitlun tor nem-tor du ne' tor wuh stables.” wuh telephone rang svi'udish, startlingly, heh u' daisy hutau ish-veh patam decisively na' tom wuh subject t' wuh stables, svi' kla-min ek' subjects, vanished vi' sov. Among wuh pushau karf t' wuh kim-shah kaukuh minutes na' pasu i vokau wuh ha'fek hasu lit va'ashiv, pointlessly, heh i vesh' d'wonil t' wanting tor glazhau squarely na' kanok-veh, heh wi tor nan'woi ek' bezhun. I couldn’t guess ra daisy heh tom vesh' thinking, tonk'peh i vet kuv kauk din-tor leipausu, vi seemed ki' tren-tor wuh ac'ruth hardy scepticism, vesh' kup utterly tor shitau nash fifth be'hai'la’s shrill metallic urgency s' kashek. Tor wuh ac'ruth temperament wuh situation lau ma seemed intriguing—t'nash-veh sha' instinct vesh' tor telephone iyi na' wuh police. Wuh jarel, needless tor leralmin, vesh' ri mentioned va'ashiv. Tom heh din-tor leipausu, k' several ash'ya t' twilight svi' au, strolled pla' vi' wuh shi'dunap, u' kuv tor wuh vigil be' wuh perfectly tangible ak'shem, du', trying tor glazhau pleasantly interested heh wuh pi' zhu-fam, i zahal-tor daisy pa' wuh naf-elakh t' connecting verandas tor wuh porch svi' khom. Svi' its glu gloom etek hayal-tor ne' vla k' vla fi' wuh wicker settee. Daisy nem-tor ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru u' kuv olaya its lovely shid, heh ish-veh bezhun dvun-tor gradually si' vi' wuh velvet dusk. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik waukik zherka ma ish-veh, ni i ya'akash ra i nahp would nam-tor ein sedative deshkau pa' ish-veh pi' ko-kan. “etek don’t fai-tor tik vath maut muhl, nick, ” she leralmin-tor suddenly. “kauk kuv etek nam-tor krei. Du didn’t sarlah tor t'nash-veh wedding.” “i wasn’t pla' s' wuh t'naehm.” “ik’s yeht.” she hesitated. “muhl, i’ve had wuh maut rasahkos wak, nick, heh i’m takov cynical pa' kanok-vei.” evidently she had utvau tor nam-tor. I bek-tor tonk'peh she didn’t leralmin sovek weht, heh po' wuh moment i fun-tor rather feebly tor wuh subject t' ish-veh ko-fu. “i suppose she variben, heh—yokul, heh kanok-vei.” “oh, ha.” she glazhau na' me absently. “shroi, nick; kal-tor me var-tor du ra i leralmin-tor lu she vesh' pukeshta. Would du spo' tor zhu-tor?” “maut mau.” “ish-veh’ll gluvaya du uf i’ve gotten tor olau pa'—vel. Muhl, she vesh' lehkuh tor wuh wadan hinek heh tom vesh' oekon fai-tor wilat. I woke abru s' wuh ether k' wuh utterly abandoned olaya, heh ya'akash wuh nurse gas'rak maf kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh sa-kan il wuh ko-kan. She var-tor me ish-veh vesh' wuh ko-kan, heh ni i da-tor t'nash-veh patam maf heh wept. ‘ek' gas'rak, ’ i leralmin-tor, ‘i’m glad ish-veh’s wuh ko-kan. Heh i rok she’ll nam-tor wuh duhsu—ik’s wuh buhfik vel wuh ko-kan mokuhlek nam-tor svi' nash panu, wuh vaksurik pi' duhsu.’ “gla-tor du i nah-tor kanok-vei’s terrible anyhow, ” she went fi' svi' wuh convinced yut. “kanok-veh nah-tor ni—wuh danik storilau sutra. Heh i fai-tor. I’ve vesh' kanok-wilat heh gla-tor kanok-vei heh ovsoh kanok-vei.” ish-veh bezhun kahai pa' ish-veh svi' wuh defiant yut, rather spo' tom’s, heh she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor k' thrilling scorn. “sophisticated—oekon, i’m sophisticated!” wuh instant ish-veh spes shau ska', ceasing tor compel t'nash-veh attention, t'nash-veh dva, i olau wuh nenik insincerity t' ra she had leralmin-tor. Ish-veh tor me uneasy, u' hi wuh bosh khru had vesh' wuh trick t' ein wihfelau tor faikaik wuh contributory zherka s' me. I bek-tor, heh sure hiyet, svi' wuh moment she glazhau na' me k' wuh ek'esik smirk fi' ish-veh lovely limuk, u' kuv she had asserted ish-veh membership svi' wuh rather distinguished tsat shila'es tor if she heh tom belonged. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ svi'udish, wuh hirat-kur tvi-shal svai-tor k' ta'hal. Tom heh din-tor leipausu hayal-tor na' either shaht t' wuh wu ku-san heh she telv-tor aloud tor ish-veh s' wuh gad khru lehk—wuh zhit, murmurous heh uninflected, sahran teretuhr svi' wuh soothing tvelkau. Wuh lamplight, ugelik fi' ish-veh kluf heh pasik fi' wuh tasmin-mor kin-kur t' ish-veh isachya, glinted bi' wuh dun u' she da-tor wuh thalv k' wuh nuv t' slender dvunek svi' ish-veh kar. Lu sarlah etek svi' she meskarau etek ralash-fam na' wuh moment k' wuh abertau el'ru. “tor nam-tor fator, ” she leralmin-tor, tossing wuh magazine fi' wuh pasu, “svi' etwel maut thurai issue.” ish-veh ak'shem asserted itself k' wuh restless dvun t' ish-veh mal-nef, heh she lam-tor abru. “lehkuh o’wak-vel, ” she remarked, sauyaing finding wuh wak fi' wuh abru-tol. “wak na' nash rom ko-kan tor hal-tor tor sar-tak.” “jordan’s going tor mavau svi' wuh tournament fa-gad, ” danau daisy, “abru' na' westchester.” “oh—du’re jordan leipausu.” i fai-tor i' po ish-veh limuk vesh' familiar—its pleasing contemptuous sagluvaya had glazhau si' na' me s' wehk rotogravure bikuv t' wuh sporting ha'kiv na' asheville heh fal sikar heh ku shahov. I had puzhu-tor ein var t' ish-veh nuh', wuh bolik, unpleasant var, tonk'peh ra ish-veh vesh' i had yen-tor wu ago. “rom mu-yor, ” she leralmin-tor softly. “wake me na' ohkuh, skil-tor’t du.” “kuv du’ll prah abru.” “i dungi. Rom mu-yor, mr. Carraway. Gla-tor du anon.” “veling du dungi, ” wugau daisy. “svi' kla-min i nah-tor i’ll arrange wuh kal'i'farr. Sarlah abru' k'ashiv, nick, heh i’ll wihfelau t'—oh—fling du teretuhr. Du fai-tor—klachek du abru accidentally svi' linen tsorayek heh kwitaya du si' tor masutra svi' wuh masu-hali, heh ek' ik wihfelau t' vel—” “rom mu-yor, ” puvutau din-tor leipausu s' wuh kaiden. “i haven’t puzhu-tor wuh zhit.” “she’s wuh nice ko-kan, ” leralmin-tor tom po' wuh moment. “au oughtn’t tor kal-tor ish-veh sahr-tor pa' wuh shasol nash yut.” “vi oughtn’t tor?” inquired daisy coldly. “ish-veh skan.” “ish-veh skan nam-tor veh ezyet pa' wuh thousand tevun hinek. Isha, nick’s going tor glazhau po' ish-veh, aren’t du, nick? She’s going tor spend lots t' weekends si' la' nash belaar. I nah-tor wuh ha-kel vi-yumuk dungi nam-tor maut rom na' ish-veh.” daisy heh tom glazhau na' tik vath na' wuh moment svi' silence. “nam-tor she s' uzh york?” i ya'akash sahris. “s' louisville. Etwel wan-kur girlhood vesh' be' dvun-tor teretuhr tra'. Etwel vaksurik wan-kur—” “did du mazhiv-kur-tor nick wuh pi' khaf-spol tor khaf-spol variben fi' wuh veranda?” halishau tom suddenly. “did i?” she glazhau na' me. “i mokuhlek’t seem tor vokau, tonk'peh i nah-tor etek variben pa' wuh nordic ne-koshtri. Ha, i’m sure etek did. Ish-veh wihfelau t' crept abru fi' etek heh wuh'rak vel du fai-tor—” “don’t dva-tor kanok-vei du zhu-tor, nick, ” au na'shikhau me. I leralmin-tor lightly ik i had puzhu-tor nothing na' ek', heh wuh zamu minutes later i prah abru tor hal-tor ha-kel. Sarlah au tor wuh svep k' me heh lam-tor vla k' vla svi' wuh cheerful keh-vla t' ta'hal. U' i palikau t'nash-veh mishu daisy peremptorily puvutau: “bek-tor! “i forgot tor ya'akash du vel, heh ish-veh’s yauluhk. Etek puzhu-tor du vesh' engaged tor wuh ko-kan si' tev'rak.” “ik’s gas'rak, ” corroborated tom kindly. “etek puzhu-tor ik du vesh' engaged.” “ish-veh’s wuh libel. I’m nuh' ri donku-tor.” “tonk'peh etek puzhu-tor ish-veh, ” insisted daisy, surprising me k' sharu abru va'ashiv svi' wuh svai-spo' yut. “etek puzhu-tor ish-veh s' rehkuh sutra, ni ish-veh bolau nam-tor yeht.” veling i fai-tor ra au vesh' referring tor, tonk'peh i wasn’t kauk vaguely engaged. Wuh kla-min ik gossip had published wuh banns vesh' veh t' wuh utvau i had sarlah she'rak. Du mokuhlek’t pehkaya going k' wuh hinek t'hy'la fi' khrosahp t' rumours, heh fi' wuh vath el'ru i had rai intention t' hasu rumoured vi' kal'i'farr. Ish-veh eku'ko rather estuhl me heh tor au lehkuh remotely don-ka—nevertheless, i vesh' confused heh wuh pi' spa'ash u' i drove maf. Ish-veh seemed tor me ik wuh vel na' daisy tor tor vesh' tor rush si' t' wuh kelek, kan svi' kar—tonk'peh sauyaing tra' vesh' rai such intentions svi' ish-veh patam. U' na' tom, wuh kla-min ik au “had ein kosu svi' uzh york” vesh' really lehkuh surprising do ik au had vesh' depressed k' wuh dunap. Vel vesh' tor ish-veh nibble na' wuh rihk t' os ideas u' kuv ish-veh batai tukhik ritsuri-shai'es rai longer yem-mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh peremptory khaf-spol. Already ish-veh vesh' glu belaar fi' roadhouse kamu heh svi' khom t' wayside pi'hali-kel, wilat uzh yon-kur hal-masu-spol-tor hayal-tor si' svi' patra t' ta'hal, heh lu i pulau t'nash-veh estate na' tev'rak yu-mur i sahr-tor wuh poiq'lid ne' its foshuhl heh hayal-tor na' wuh du' fi' wuh abandoned yar roller svi' wuh ker. Wuh salan had blown ska', leaving wuh ral, ugelik mu-yor, k' rala beating svi' wuh lap heh wuh persistent nafek ralash u' wuh bosh vlei t' wuh terra blew wuh git'woa bosh t' ha'kiv. Wuh silhouette t' wuh dvun-tor aushfa wavered mes' wuh moonlight, heh, turning t'nash-veh patam tor glantau ish-veh, vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik i vesh' ri sa'awek—kau-leh ash'ya maf wuh khlop had sasarlah s' wuh duv t' t'nash-veh behsu’s mansion heh vesh' standing k' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh abru'lik fundauik wuh haul-tukh pepper t' wuh yel. Vel svi' ish-veh leisurely dvun heh wuh shar shul t' ish-veh ash'ya fi-tor wuh yartra suggested ik ish-veh vesh' mr. Gatsby himself, sasarlah tor satalau ra thresh vesh' ish-veh t' etwel local heavens. I klopau tor vutau tor ish-veh. Din-tor leipausu had mentioned ish-veh na' aru-yem, heh ik would tor na' wuh ragtaya. Tonk'peh i didn’t vutau tor ish-veh, na' au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sudden intimation ik au vesh' content tor nam-tor sa'awek—au sakadau si' ish-veh kar na' wuh gu'gelik masu svi' wuh curious yut, heh, irak u' i vesh' s' ish-veh, i kupi ma sworn au vesh' trembling. Involuntarily i glanced seaward—heh distinguished nothing kaula wuh single yar-kur ta'hal, minute heh irak maf, ik lau ma vesh' wuh shaht t' wuh kif. Lu i glazhau wuh'wak weht na' gatsby au had vanished, heh i vesh' sa'awek va'ashiv svi' wuh unquiet mu'khlup'es. Ii pa' halfway svi' tev'rak yu-mur heh uzh york wuh mishu fau-yut hastily hau wuh railroad heh sahr-tor be' ish-veh na' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile, ni u' tor shrink maf s' wuh ac'ruth desolate shal t' solektra. Nash nam-tor wuh ku-li t' vitush—wuh fantastic uroshal wilat vitush tor'ovau spo' kap-yar vi' tauf heh kunel heh grotesque bah-ker; wilat vitush nem-tor wuh shidau t' kelek heh vuzh-mev heh rising vuzh heh, t'forti, k' wuh transcendent urgam, t' vitush-zhai-kur sasu, vi dvun dimly heh already crumbling k'fai wuh powdery sov. Occasionally wuh zehl t' zhai-kur poiq'lid ukrau bi' wuh invisible yut, mazhiv-kur-tor si' wuh ghastly creak, heh sarlah tor shom, heh iyi wuh vitush-zhai-kur sasu bish abru k' leaden ash'ya-hilek heh stir abru wuh impenetrable wan, if gluvayek ish-veh obscure el'toraya s' ish-veh glan. Tonk'peh abru' wuh zhai-kur solektra heh wuh runev t' bleak grazhiv if maraya endlessly abru' ish-veh, du pakashogau, po' wuh moment, wuh bezhun t' hassu t. J. Eckleburg. Wuh bezhun t' hassu t. J. Eckleburg nam-tor pla-kur heh masuk'—ish-veh glan-nalatra-zhai-tukh nam-tor veh ker pid. Au glazhau s' rai limuk, tonk'peh, instead, s' wuh shif t' masuk' kin-kur spectacles if be' dvun abru' wuh nonexistent han. Evidently ein kwai wag t' wuh oculist eku au tra' tor fatten ish-veh practice svi' wuh borough t' ko-te'kru, heh yi sank ne' himself vi' ek'wakik glan-fam'es, il forgot au heh dvun-tor maf. Tonk'peh ish-veh bezhun, ha'khlup-ne-tor wuh pi' k' wehk paintless gad, ne' yel heh sov-masu, kesh-travek fi' abru' wuh solemn dumping solektra. Wuh ku-li t' vitush nam-tor bounded fi' veh vla k' wuh pi' flalik pilash, heh, lu wuh drawbridge nam-tor abru tor kal-tor tus-hali k'fai, wuh passengers fi' waiting ranau mokuhlek nantaya na' wuh dismal scene na' u' wu u' ulef wuh wadan. Tra' nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh halt tra' t' k'puu wuh minute, heh ish-veh vesh' fai'ei t' nash ik i wuh'rak ragel-tor tom buchanan’s mistress. Wuh kla-min ik au had veh vesh' insisted fi-tor wherever au vesh' fainu. Ish-veh acquaintances resented wuh kla-min ik au da-tor abru svi' popular cafés k' ish-veh heh, leaving ish-veh na' wuh pasu, sauntered pa', chatting k' whomsoever au fai-tor. Hi i vesh' curious tor gla-tor ish-veh, i had rai aitlun tor ragel-tor ish-veh—tonk'peh i did. I went abru tor uzh york k' tom fi' wuh ranau veh aru, heh lu etek pehkau k' wuh vitush-heaps au spen-tor tor ish-veh ash'ya heh, taking meskaraya t' t'nash-veh kar-nef, literally punekwitau me s' wuh poiq'lid. “etek’re getting ska', ” au insisted. “i aitlun du tor ragel-tor t'nash-veh ko-kan.” i nah-tor au’d tanked abru wuh rom deal na' luncheon, heh ish-veh determination ki' t'nash-veh apc'koik bordered fi' khrash. Wuh supercilious assumption vesh' ik fi' gad aru i had nothing weh-rom tor tor. I zahal-tor ish-veh abru' wuh neik whitewashed railroad foshek, heh etek lates-tor pla' wuh hundred ker bi' wuh fau-yut ne' hassu eckleburg’s persistent nantaya. Wuh goh kelek svi' glan vesh' wuh pi' vihpan t' kin-kur dok sitting fi' wuh rihk t' wuh thinoi solektra, wuh wihfelau t' lerakhovau nen yut ministering tor ish-veh, heh contiguous tor absolutely nothing. Veh t' wuh rehkuh mahr-kel ish-veh tuhlau vesh' na' rent heh wuh'ashiv vesh' wuh ek'-mu-yor restaurant, betau k' wuh yut t' vitush; wuh wuh vesh' wuh pi'hali-kel—teslau. George b. Wilson. Poiq'lid bought heh makau.—heh i zahal-tor tom svi'udish. Wuh interior vesh' unprosperous heh sai-famik; wuh goh poiq'lid visible vesh' wuh grazhiv-wein-tor vashau t' wuh masmezh if crouched svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup teruk. Ish-veh had paresh-tor tor me ik nash duv t' wuh pi'hali-kel bolau nam-tor wuh glan-fam, heh ik sumptuous heh romantic ha-shal vesh' ip-sut overhead, lu wuh proprietor himself saudau svi' wuh svep t' wuh office, psethau ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh krus t' thinoi. Au vesh' wuh blond, spiritless sasu, anaemic, heh faintly handsome. Lu gla-tor ish-veh etek wuh damp gleam t' rok sprang vi' ish-veh ha'pla-kur bezhun. “tonk'peh, wilson, hinek sasu, ” leralmin-tor tom, slapping ish-veh jovially fi' wuh tipan. “uf’s business?” “i mokuhlek’t complain, ” kilko-tor wilson unconvincingly. “lu nam-tor du going tor makau me ik poiq'lid?” “thurai wehk gad; i’ve prah t'nash-veh sasu working fi' ish-veh i'.” “ar'kada takov vohris, don’t au?” “rai, au doesn’t, ” leralmin-tor tom coldly. “heh kuv du olau ik yut pa' ish-veh, sos'eh i’d weh-rom makau ish-veh ein-wilat else po' ek'.” “i don’t tvai ik, ” danau wilson sahris. “i aishan tvai—” ish-veh spes spoh-tor ska' heh tom glanced impatiently pa' wuh pi'hali-kel. Yi i puzhu-tor footsteps fi' wuh kaiden, heh svi' wuh moment wuh thickish khlop t' wuh kosu klotau si' wuh ta'hal s' wuh office svep. She vesh' svi' wuh svitan thirties, heh faintly stout, tonk'peh she lesh ish-veh kahm sensuously u' ein kosu mokuhlek. Ish-veh limuk, abru' wuh gla-tor sai-vel t' gu'gelik pla-kur crêpe-de-chine, tuhlau rai pulva il gleam t' vaksur, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh iyi perceptible vitality pa' ish-veh u' kuv wuh tor'tsu t' ish-veh ak'shem vesh' continually smouldering. She abru'teruklar-ru'lut slowly heh, walking k'fai ish-veh sa-telsu u' kuv au vesh' wuh tam'a, hutau el'ru k' tom, looking ish-veh kluhvau svi' wuh bezhun. Yi she masupik ish-veh bru-lar, heh rik' turning pa' stariben tor ish-veh sa-telsu svi' wuh mos, dirik spes: “prah ein ku-san, po don’t du, ni somebody mokuhlek hayal-tor ne'.” “oh, sure, ” sep-wafikh wilson hurriedly, heh went na' wuh pi' office, mingling iyi k' wuh kluterek kur t' wuh temok. Wuh wan-kur ashen grazhiv veiled ish-veh gu'gelik saikhut heh ish-veh spoh isachya u' ish-veh veiled kanok-vei svi' wuh vicinity—kaula ish-veh ko-telsu, vi dvun-tor beyik tom. “i aitlun tor gla-tor du, ” leralmin-tor tom intently. “prah fi' wuh thurai ranau.” “ek' gas'rak.” “i’ll ragel-tor du k' wuh newsstand fi' wuh weh-neik volik.” she nodded heh sadvun-tor ish-veh aishan u' george wilson sasarlah k' dahkuh ku-san s' ish-veh office svep. Etek bek-tor na' ish-veh ne' wuh fau-yut heh s' glan. Ish-veh vesh' wuh zamu gad fa' wuh fourth t' july, heh wuh zhai-kur, scrawny italian kan vesh' setting lushun svi' wuh zehl bi' wuh railroad yut. “terrible shi, isn’t ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor tom, exchanging wuh kwal k' hassu eckleburg. “awful.” “ish-veh tor ish-veh rom tor prah maf.” “doesn’t ish-veh sa-telsu vel?” “wilson? Au nah-tor she hal-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh ko-kai svi' uzh york. Au’s ni dumb au doesn’t fai-tor au’s alive.” ni tom buchanan heh ish-veh ko-kan heh i went abru teretuhr tor uzh york—il ri ved teretuhr, na' mrs. Wilson hayal-tor discreetly svi' wuh'ashiv poiq'lid. Tom deferred ik mau tor wuh sensibilities t' eifa she'rak eggers vi lau nam-tor fi' wuh ranau. She had rubai ish-veh sai-vel tor wuh khav-kur figured muslin, if sakadau wufik abru' ish-veh rather eik gaf u' tom gol-tor ish-veh tor wuh skaf svi' uzh york. Na' wuh newsstand she bought wuh va'asau t' kahr tattle heh wuh dvun-tor-bikuv magazine, heh svi' wuh wurzel drugstore ein samu dyrk heh wuh pi' mashek t' perfume. Upstairs, svi' wuh solemn echoing yetur she kal-tor kehkuh taxicabs yetur maf fa' she dvel-tor wuh uzh veh, pulu-kur-kur-tor k' zhai-kur upholstery, heh svi' nash etek slid si' s' wuh shivak t' wuh wurzel vi' wuh glowing sunshine. Tonk'peh iyi she da-tor sharply s' wuh krani heh, leaning fa'rak, tapped fi' wuh khom makh. “i aitlun tor prah veh t' eifa dogs, ” she leralmin-tor earnestly. “i aitlun tor prah veh na' wuh ha-shal. Au’re nice ki'—wuh dog.” etek backed abru tor wuh zhai-kur hinek sasu vi spitau wuh absurd resemblance tor john d. Rockefeller. Svi' wuh ki'haf swung s' ish-veh talu cowered wuh dozen maut recent wil'tei t' wuh indeterminate kosh-ves. “ra ves nam-tor au?” ya'akash mrs. Wilson eagerly, u' sarlah ish-veh tor wuh taxi-krani. “ek' ves. Ra ves tor du aitlun, t'sai?” “i’d spo' tor prah veh t' eifa police dogs; i don’t suppose du prah ik ves?” wuh sasu peered doubtfully vi' wuh ki'haf, taul-tor svi' ish-veh el'ru heh drew veh abru, wriggling, k' wuh pla' t' wuh talu. “ik’s rai police dog, ” leralmin-tor tom. “rai, ish-veh’s ri exactly wuh police dog, ” leralmin-tor wuh sasu k' disappointment svi' ish-veh spes. “ish-veh’s weht t' wuh airedale.” au be' dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru abru' wuh khav-kur washrag t' wuh pla'. “glazhau na' ik tor-pal. Ein tor-pal. Ik’s wuh dog ik’ll worla ertau du k' catching samu.” “i nah-tor ish-veh’s cute, ” leralmin-tor mrs. Wilson enthusiastically. “uf mau nam-tor ish-veh?” “ik dog?” au glazhau na' ish-veh admiringly. “ik dog dungi kodona du lehkuh dollars.” wuh airedale—undoubtedly tra' vesh' wuh airedale concerned svi' ish-veh ein-wilat, hi its ash'ya vesh' startlingly wan-kur—rubai el'ru heh settled ne' vi' mrs. Wilson’s lap, wilat she fondled wuh weatherproof tor-pal k' rapture. “nam-tor ish-veh wuh sa-kan il wuh ko-kan?” she ya'akash delicately. “ik dog? Ik dog’s wuh sa-kan.” “ish-veh’s wuh bitch, ” leralmin-tor tom decisively. “la'’s ish-veh donku. Hal-tor heh mahr-tor lehkuh weht dogs k' ish-veh.” etek drove abru' tor fifth avenue, lamekh heh mos, siyah pastoral, fi' wuh belaar gad aru. I wouldn’t ma vesh' ak'wikmun tor gla-tor wuh lo'uk treit t' wan-kur sheep da-tor wuh teruk. “meskaraya fi', ” i leralmin-tor, “i ma tor trasha du la'.” “rai du don’t, ” interposed tom sahris. “myrtle’ll nam-tor dash-tor kuv du don’t sarlah abru tor wuh ha-shal. Skil-tor’t du, myrtle?” “sarlah fi', ” she urged. “i’ll telephone t'nash-veh ko-kai catherine. She’s leralmin-tor tor nam-tor maut vaksurik k' sutra vi ought tor fai-tor.” “muhl, i’d spo' tor, tonk'peh—” etek went fi', tresahk-tor pla' va'ashiv abru' wuh shi'sochya na' wuh tev'rak hundreds. Na' 158th yut wuh cab pehkau na' veh shihvek svi' wuh wu wan-kur cake t' ha-shal-kelek. Throwing wuh regal homecoming glance pa' wuh neighbourhood, mrs. Wilson hoknau abru ish-veh dog heh ish-veh vath purchases, heh went haughtily svi'. “i’m going ki' wuh mckees sarlah abru, ” she tor'pra u' etek she-tor svi' wuh sa'adek. “heh, veling, i prah tor vutau abru t'nash-veh ko-kai, nuh'.” wuh ha-shal vesh' fi' wuh fik lan-tol—wuh pi' living-tvi-shal, wuh pi' dining-tvi-shal, wuh pi' shi'yuk, heh wuh wu'sibav. Wuh living-tvi-shal vesh' crowded tor wuh svep k' wuh eku t' tapestried furniture entirely nuh' suk na' ish-veh, ni ik tor dvun pa' vesh' tor stumble continually abru' scenes t' t'sai swinging svi' wuh bah-ker t' versailles. Wuh goh bikuv vesh' wuh abru'-sukau ha'gel-bikuv, sauyaing wuh hen sitting fi' wuh blurred kov. Glazhau na' kwi', however, wuh hen resolved itself vi' wuh bonnet, heh wuh countenance t' wuh stout hinek t'sai beamed ne' vi' wuh tvi-shal. Several hinek va'asau t' kahr tattle ti fi' wuh pasu teretuhr k' wuh va'asau t' simon puvutau peter, heh ein t' wuh pi' scandal magazines t' broadway. Mrs. Wilson vesh' wuh'rak concerned k' wuh dog. Wuh reluctant sa'adek sa-kan went na' wuh natuhn bosh t' terp heh ein thas, tor if au hau fi' ish-veh sha' initiative wuh zhai-tukh t' suk, lerash dog kreyla—veh t' if ek'nehau apathetically svi' wuh ne-mathra t' thas ek' aru. Meanwhile tom katau si' wuh mashek t' whisky s' wuh klacha bureau svep. I ma vesh' mon-tor aishan dah'wak svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, heh wuh dahr wak vesh' ik aru; ni kanok-vei ik pavesh-tor has wuh neik-ha'khlup, hazy vishizhau abru' ish-veh, hi abi' po' ohkuh o’wak-vel wuh ha-shal vesh' bosh t' cheerful yel. Sitting fi' tom’s lap mrs. Wilson puvutau abru several sutra fi' wuh telephone; yi tra' vesh' rai cigarettes, heh i went si' tor mahr-tor ein na' wuh drugstore fi' wuh teruk. Lu vesht sarlah nash-veh pla' au had fi' sasaudau, ni i hayal-tor ne' discreetly svi' wuh living-tvi-shal heh telv-tor wuh chapter t' simon puvutau peter—either ish-veh vesh' terrible tukh il wuh whisky distorted vel, fai'ei ish-veh didn’t tor sovek kash-ral tor me. Aishan u' tom heh myrtle (po' wuh wuh'rak mon mrs. Wilson heh i puvutau tik vath k' etwel wuh'rak ahm) reappeared, apc'koik palikau tor lasha na' wuh ha-shal svep. Wuh ko-kai, catherine, vesh' wuh slender, worldly ko-kan t' pa' reh-leh, k' wuh huhtik, terpauk bob t' yon-kur isachya, heh wuh complexion powdered milky wan-kur. Ish-veh bezhun-zehl had vesh' plucked heh yi drawn fi' va'ashiv na' wuh weht rakish vulu, tonk'peh wuh urgam t' malat na' wuh restoration t' wuh hinek zehl'es mazhiv-kur-tor wuh blurred sov tor ish-veh limuk. Lu she dvun-tor pa' tra' vesh' wuh incessant clicking u' va' pottery kar-nik-zhel jingled abru heh ne' fi-tor ish-veh kar. Sarlah ish-veh svi' k' such wuh proprietary haste, heh glazhau pa' ni possessively na' wuh furniture ik i wondered kuv she ha-tor la'. Tonk'peh lu i ya'akash ish-veh she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor immoderately, ashiv-tor t'nash-veh deshker aloud, heh var-tor me she ha-tor k' wuh ko-kan t'hy'la na' wuh hotel. Mr. Mckee vesh' wuh spoh, kogavik sasu s' wuh pa'ash ne'. Au had aishan hohl-tor, na' tra' vesh' wuh wan-kur gla-tor t' lather fi' ish-veh cheekbone, heh au vesh' danik respectful svi' ish-veh na'shaya tor kanok-veh svi' wuh tvi-shal. Au informed me ik au vesh' svi' wuh “tanafluk zhagra, ” heh i hoknau later ik au vesh' wuh ha'gel-tanafsu heh had tor wuh neik-ha'khlup sukaya t' mrs. Wilson’s ko-mekh if hovered spo' wuh ectoplasm fi' wuh temok. Ish-veh ko-telsu vesh' shrill, languid, handsome, heh horrible. She var-tor me k' pride ik ish-veh sa-telsu had photographed ish-veh wuh hundred heh dah-leh-stehkuh wak opi' au had vesh' telik. Mrs. Wilson had rubai ish-veh costume ein wak fa', heh vesh' i' attired svi' wuh elaborate aru sai-vel t' dyrk-kur-tor chiffon, if mazhiv-kur-tor si' wuh continual rustle u' she swept pa' wuh tvi-shal. K' wuh vi-yumuk t' wuh sai-vel ish-veh nafu'es had isha undergone wuh rubah. Wuh intense vitality ik had vesh' ni remarkable svi' wuh pi'hali-kel vesh' rushan-tor vi' impressive hauteur. Ish-veh laughter, ish-veh gestures, ish-veh assertions became weht violently dau moment k' moment, heh u' she sa'ovau wuh tvi-shal grew smaller pa' ish-veh, abi' she seemed tor nam-tor revolving fi' wuh noisy, creaking da-sfek k'fai wuh smoky sov. “t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” she var-tor ish-veh ko-kai svi' wuh pid, mincing saul, “danik t' aifa fellas dungi kravau du kanok wak.
