Kanok-veh potau taran tor me: ‘lucille, ik sasu’s yut ne' du!’ tonk'peh kuv i hadn’t ragel-tor chester, au’d t' prah me sure.” “ha, tonk'peh shroi, ” leralmin-tor myrtle wilson, nodding ish-veh patam abru heh ne', “k'puu du didn’t marry ish-veh.” “i fai-tor i didn’t.” “muhl, i telik ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor myrtle, ambiguously. “heh ik’s wuh natyan svi' ish-veh nuf heh t'nash-veh.” “po did du, myrtle?” halishau catherine. “kling punekwitau du tor.” myrtle panah-tor. “i telik ish-veh fai'ei i nahp au vesh' wuh gentleman, ” she leralmin-tor t'forti. “i nahp au fai-tor vel pa' breeding, tonk'peh au wasn’t nunau tor lick t'nash-veh ash'el.” “du vesh' amp pa' ish-veh na' wuh du', ” leralmin-tor catherine. “amp pa' ish-veh!” maf-tor myrtle incredulously. “vi leralmin-tor i vesh' amp pa' ish-veh? I worla vesh' sovek weht amp pa' ish-veh do i vesh' pa' ik sasu tra'.” she sfekau suddenly na' me, heh kanok-veh glazhau na' me accusingly. I ar'kada tor gluvaya k' t'nash-veh sagluvaya ik i gishu rai affection. “wuh goh amp i vesh' vesh' lu i telik ish-veh. I fai-tor gas'rak maf i tor wuh lafosh. Au yahv-tor somebody’s buhfik saikhut tor prah telik svi', heh worla kauk var-tor me pa' ish-veh, heh wuh sasu sarlah po' ish-veh veh gad lu au vesh' si': ‘oh, nam-tor ik ish-veh saikhut?’ i leralmin-tor. ‘nash nam-tor wuh wuh'rak i ek'wak puzhu-tor pa' ish-veh.’ tonk'peh i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh heh yi i ti ne' heh maf-tor tor kuhsh-tor wuh zhel ek' aru.” “she really ought tor prah maf s' ish-veh, ” resumed catherine tor me. “au’ve vesh' living abru' ik pi'hali-kel na' leh-wun tevun. Heh tom’s wuh wuh'rak sweetie she ek'wak had.” wuh mashek t' whisky—wuh dahr veh—vesh' i' svi' ek'kayik haishaya k' ek' la', kaulaik catherine, vi “olau aishan u' rom fi' nothing na' ek'.” tom rang na' wuh janitor heh satau ish-veh na' ein u'thet sandwiches, if vesh' wuh ovsotik mu'yor-yem svi' themselves. I aitlu tor prah si' heh lates na'she'rak na' wuh shi'sochya k'fai wuh mos twilight, tonk'peh tik wak i ar'kada tor hal-tor i became entangled svi' ein kwai, strident nerau-kek-vuhnayek if seshau me pla', u' kuv k' man-elakh, vi' t'nash-veh ku-san. Wi pid abru' wuh kahr etwel zehl t' kin-kur krani bolau ma contributed ish-veh thresh t' komihn secrecy tor wuh casual watcher svi' wuh darkening yut, heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh nuh', looking abru heh wondering. I vesh' k'svi heh rik', simultaneously enchanted heh repelled k' wuh inexhaustible vuhna'es t' ha'kiv. Myrtle seshau ish-veh ku-san beyik t'nash-veh, heh suddenly ish-veh lamekh esh mukau abru' me wuh var t' ish-veh wuh'rak latva k' tom. “ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh dahkuh pi' ku-san limuk-tor tik vath ik nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh kim-shah ones losrak fi' wuh ranau. I vesh' going abru tor uzh york tor gla-tor t'nash-veh ko-kai heh spend wuh mu-yor. Au had fi' wuh sai-vel saikhut heh patent duf ash'el, heh i couldn’t potau t'nash-veh bezhun ska' ish-veh, tonk'peh kanok wak au glazhau na' me i had tor pretend tor nam-tor looking na' wuh advertisement abru' ish-veh patam. Lu sarlah etek vi' wuh wurzel au vesh' nam-tor' me, heh ish-veh wan-kur shirtfront hish-tor tehnat t'nash-veh kar, heh ni i var-tor ish-veh i’d ma tor vutau wuh policeman, tonk'peh au fai-tor i ti. I vesh' ni teporilau ik lu i prah vi' wuh taxi k' ish-veh i didn’t hardly fai-tor i wasn’t getting vi' wuh subway ranau. Ek' i potau thinking pa', abru' heh abru', vesh' ‘du mokuhlek’t ha-tor ek'wak; du mokuhlek’t ha-tor ek'wak.’ ” she da-tor tor mrs. Mckee heh wuh tvi-shal rang bosh t' ish-veh sutorik laughter. “t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” she maf-tor, “i’m going tor mazhiv-kur-tor du nash sai-vel u' ak u' i’m k'fai k' ish-veh. I’ve prah tor prah wuh'ashiv veh fa-gad. I’m going tor tor wuh feim t' ek' wuh vel i’ve prah tor prah. Wuh massage heh wuh pral, heh wuh hmoi'neks na' wuh dog, heh veh t' eifa cute pi' ashtrays wilat du esta wuh sikar, heh wuh wreath k' wuh nesh-kur silk kes-wun na' ko-mekh’s shi'vukhut ik’ll kim-shah ek' belaar. I prah tor kitau ne' wuh feim ni i skil-tor’t yen-tor ek' wuh vel i prah tor tor.” ish-veh vesh' naukuh o’wak-vel—siyah iyi afterward i glazhau na' t'nash-veh glantau heh afer-tor ish-veh vesh' lehkuh. Mr. Mckee vesh' asleep fi' wuh ku-san k' ish-veh ozh-dukal clenched svi' ish-veh lap, spo' wuh ha'gel-bikuv t' wuh sasu t' torai. Taking si' t'nash-veh handkerchief i psethau s' ish-veh nak wuh gla-tor t' psethau lather ik had worried me ek' wuh aru. Wuh pi' dog vesh' sitting fi' wuh pasu looking k' glan-fam bezhun k'fai wuh vuzh, heh s' wak tor wak groaning faintly. Sutra sasaudau, reappeared, tor dotoran tor hal-tor ein-wilat, heh yi pakik tik vath, pstha na' tik vath, afer-tor tik vath wuh zamu ash'ya maf. Ein wak na' midnight tom buchanan heh mrs. Wilson lam-tor limuk tor limuk discussing, svi' impassioned spes, whether mrs. Wilson had sovek gas'rak tor mention daisy’s ahm. “daisy! Daisy! Daisy!” saul-tor mrs. Wilson. “i’ll leralmin ish-veh whenever i aitlun tor! Daisy! Dai—” tor wuh pen deft dvun, tom buchanan shau ish-veh han k' ish-veh tu'ash el'ru. Yi tra' vesh' bloody towels fi-tor wuh bathroom lan-tol, heh kosu’s spes scolding, heh pid abru' wuh confusion wuh wu pushau wail t' kusut. Mr. Mckee awoke s' ish-veh doze heh palikau svi' wuh daze na' wuh svep. Lu au had hal-tor halfway au da-tor pa' heh nantau na' wuh scene—ish-veh ko-telsu heh catherine scolding heh consoling u' au stumbled la' heh tra' among wuh crowded furniture k' ua'mrki t' mamuk, heh wuh despairing khlop fi' wuh ku-san, khafaya fluently, heh trying tor sak-tor wuh va'asau t' kahr tattle abru' wuh tapestry scenes t' versailles. Yi mr. Mckee da-tor heh fator fi' si' wuh svep. Taking t'nash-veh taik s' wuh chandelier, i zahal-tor. “sarlah tor khi-gad-yem ein gad, ” au suggested, u' etek groaned ne' svi' wuh sa'adek. “wilat?” “sovek-wilat.” “potau ish-veh el'ru ska' wuh lever, ” snapped wuh sa'adek sa-kan. “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon, ” leralmin-tor mr. Mckee k' dignity, “i didn’t fai-tor i vesh' touching ish-veh.” “ek' gas'rak, ” i sep-wafikh, “i’ll nam-tor glad tor.” … i vesh' standing be' ish-veh sar-tak heh au vesh' sitting abru svi' wuh thalv, clad svi' ish-veh underwear, k' wuh lo'uk portfolio svi' ish-veh el'ru. “vaksur heh wuh beast … loneliness … hinek grocery jarel … brook’n mesut …” yi i vesh' lying ulef asleep svi' wuh samu weh-neik volik t' wuh pennsylvania wurzel, staring na' wuh asal tribune, heh waiting na' wuh kehkuh o’wak-vel ranau. Iii tra' vesh' ralash-tanaf s' t'nash-veh behsu’s kelek k'fai wuh belaar mu-yor. Svi' ish-veh pla-kur bah-ker sasu heh ko-kan sarlah heh went spo' moths among wuh whisperings heh wuh champagne heh wuh yel. Na' pid-mashen svi' wuh aru i glantau ish-veh be'hai'la diving s' wuh kispek t' ish-veh marshak, il taking wuh yel fi' wuh fal mazhiv t' ish-veh shahov du' ish-veh dahkuh motorboats slit wuh mashau t' wuh ralash, bestan aquaplanes abru' bezhun-ripa'shaya t' puhsh. Fi' weekends ish-veh padukau-royce became wuh omnibus, kuvish parties tor heh s' wuh kahr svi' naukuh svi' wuh asal heh wu vesht midnight, du' ish-veh wurzel wagon scampered spo' wuh brax kin-kur bug tor ragel-tor ek' ranau. Heh fi' mondays ohkuh dvinsu, including wuh hayaik bahsu, toiled ek' gad k' mops heh scrubbing-brushes heh mah-vel heh bah-ker-eitau, repairing wuh ravages t' wuh mu-yor fa'. Kanok gad kaukuh chasulh t' zhar-kur heh lemons lasha s' wuh fruiterer svi' uzh york—kanok gad aifa ka zhar-kur heh lemons losrak ish-veh pla' svep svi' wuh rekun t' pulpless ulef. Tra' vesh' wuh mish-vel svi' wuh af'tum if kupi saseshak wuh juice t' dah-teh zhar-kur svi' ulef wuh wadan kuv wuh pi' gonaf vesh' hish-tor dah-teh wak k' wuh butler’s kaur-ozh. K'puu wuh'wak wuh fortnight wuh corps t' caterers sarlah ne' k' several hundred ash'ya t' canvas heh hiyet kur-tor ha'ge tor tor wuh christmas lap t' gatsby’s masuk' bah-ker. Fi' buffet pasu, garnished k' glistening hors-d’oeuvre, spiced leipau hams crowded tehnat yarmok t' harlequin designs heh pastry pigs heh kushel bewitched tor wuh gu'gelik pi-maat-tukh. Svi' wuh nen tvur wuh mofek k' wuh yeht dvesh-tukh rail vesh' eku abru, heh stocked k' gins heh liquors heh k' cordials ni wu yen-tor ik danik t' ish-veh kotik be'hai'la vesh' nuh' nu'ri tor fai-tor veh s' wuh'ashiv. K' stehkuh o’wak-vel wuh orchestra has lasha, rai wonil kaukuh-krus tek'ik, tonk'peh wuh bosh pitful t' oboes heh trombones heh saxophones heh viols heh cornets heh piccolos, heh neik heh pid vluhn. Wuh kim-shah swimmers ma sarlah svi' s' wuh shahov i' heh nam-tor sai-vel-tor upstairs; wuh poiq'lid s' uzh york nam-tor parked kaukuh glu svi' wuh yetur, heh already wuh tvur heh salons heh verandas nam-tor gaudy k' nen-kurek, heh isachya bobbed svi' flekh uzh yut, heh shawls mesakh wuh sahr-tor-tor t' castile. Wuh mofek nam-tor svi' bosh swing, heh floating rounds t' cocktails permeate wuh bah-ker s'udish, abi' wuh sov nam-tor alive k' chatter heh laughter, heh casual innuendo heh ragtaya yen-tor fi' wuh gla-tor, heh buhlik latva svi' kosu vi worla fai-tor tik vath’s ahm. Wuh ha'ge tor'ovau brighter u' wuh terra lurches maf s' wuh yel, heh i' wuh orchestra nam-tor mavaun kin-kur cocktail ralash-tanaf, heh wuh opera t' spes pitches wuh tal-muv higher. Laughter nam-tor easier minute k' minute, ne-tor k' prodigality, tipped si' na' wuh cheerful zhit. Wuh travek rubah weht swiftly, puv-tor k' uzh lashan, fezhau heh shid svi' wuh ka esh; already tra' nam-tor wanderers, confident ko-kan vi pris-tor la' heh tra' among wuh stouter heh weht tihet, shetau na' wuh nasik, joyous moment wuh centre t' wuh travek, heh yi, teporilau k' triumph, glide fi' k'fai wuh masutra-rubah t' limuk heh spes heh kur ne' wuh constantly rubai ta'hal. Suddenly veh t' aifa gypsies, svi' trembling opal, seizes wuh cocktail s' wuh sov, dumps ish-veh ne' na' courage heh, dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru spo' frisco, tam-tor si' sa'awek fi' wuh canvas skaf. Wuh momentary hush; wuh orchestra leader vuhnau ish-veh farr-dath obligingly na' ish-veh, heh tra' nam-tor wuh thorau t' chatter u' wuh erroneous ro'fori hal-tor pa' ik she nam-tor gilda zhai-kur’s understudy s' wuh follies. Wuh party has palikau. I dva-tor ik fi' wuh wuh'rak mu-yor i went tor gatsby’s kelek i vesh' veh t' wuh zamu be'hai'la vi had actually vesh' invited. Sutra vesh' ri invited—au went tra'. Au prah vi' automobiles if spitau au si' tor wu vikuvtra, heh somehow au shahtau abru na' gatsby’s svep. Wuh'wak tra' au vesh' puragtau k' somebody vi fai-tor gatsby, heh po' ik au conducted themselves fupa s' wuh tor-go t' kloshai katravah k' wuh amusement shi'sochya. Sometimes sarlah au heh went rik' having ragel-tor gatsby na' ek', sarlah na' wuh party k' wuh simplicity t' khaf-spol ik vesh' its sha' ticket t' admission. I had vesh' actually invited. Wuh chauffeur svi' wuh uniform t' kushel’s-yu-mur pla-kur tuhsau t'nash-veh yartra lehkuh-mal ik gad asal k' wuh surprisingly hotorik pitoh s' ish-veh employer: wuh dor would nam-tor entirely gatsby’s, ish-veh leralmin-tor, kuv i would attend ish-veh “pi' party” ik mu-yor. Au had gla-tor me several wak, heh had intended tor vutau fi' me wu fa', tonk'peh wuh peculiar terish t' circumstances had prevented ish-veh—signed jay gatsby, svi' wuh majestic el'ru. Sai-vel-tor abru svi' wan-kur flannels i went abru' tor ish-veh yartra wuh pi' po' stehkuh, heh czar-tor pa' rather has-bosh na' ease among swirls heh pi'tchef t' sutra i didn’t fai-tor—hi la' heh tra' vesh' wuh limuk i had pubeglanau fi' wuh commuting ranau. I vesh' iyi kwul-tor k' wuh su'etek t' nu'ri englishmen dotted pa'; ek' muhl sai-vel-tor, ek' looking wuh pi' k'avon, heh ek' talking svi' neik, earnest spes tor huhtik heh prosperous americans. I vesh' sure ik au vesh' selling vel: tel il insurance il automobiles. Au vesh' k'puu agonizingly aware t' wuh hagik donku svi' wuh vicinity heh convinced ik ish-veh vesh' ish-veh na' wuh zamu zhit svi' wuh gas'rak tal-muv. U' ak u' i lasha i tor wuh attempt tor talal t'nash-veh kasu, tonk'peh wuh dahkuh il rehkuh sutra t' ik i ya'akash ish-veh whereabouts nantau na' me svi' such wuh putaurau yut, heh wafu ni vehemently sovek fai-tukh t' ish-veh dvun, ik i slunk ska' svi' wuh kharat t' wuh cocktail pasu—wuh goh shi svi' wuh bah-ker wilat wuh single sasu kupi svizh-tor rik' looking purposeless heh sa'awek. I vesh' fi' t'nash-veh yut tor prah roaring mon-tor s' sheer embarrassment lu jordan leipausu sasarlah t' wuh kelek heh lam-tor na' wuh patam t' wuh marble ash-tor, leaning wuh pi' pla'rak heh looking k' contemptuous eku'ko ne' vi' wuh bah-ker. Welcome il ri, i afer-tor ish-veh bolayatik tor attach myself tor ein-veh fa' i dang palikau tor shi'yavekh cordial remarks tor wuh passersby. “tonk'peh!” i roared, advancing na' ish-veh. T'nash-veh spes seemed unnaturally ral mes' wuh bah-ker. “i nahp du lau nam-tor la', ” she kesau absently u' vesht sarlah nash-veh abru. “i vokau du ha-tor thurai svep tor—” she meskarau t'nash-veh el'ru impersonally, u' wuh ugaya ik she’d nem-tor tun t' me svi' wuh minute, heh mazhiv-kur-tor kaluk tor dahkuh ko-kan svi' t'dahsu kin-kur sai-vel, vi pehkau na' wuh ash'ya t' wuh ash-tor. “tonk'peh!” au maf-tor teretuhr. “sorry du didn’t skil.” ik vesh' na' wuh golf tournament. She had pakik svi' wuh finals wuh wehk gad fa'. “du don’t fai-tor vi etek nam-tor, ” leralmin-tor veh t' wuh ko-kan svi' kin-kur, “tonk'peh etek ragel-tor du la' pa' wuh tevun-krus ago.” “du’ve kur-tor ish-veh isachya opi' yi, ” remarked jordan, heh i palikau, tonk'peh wuh ko-kan had dvun-tor casually fi' heh ish-veh remark vesh' addressed tor wuh fe-wakik aikum, torvau spo' wuh mu'yor-yem, rai vet, s' wuh caterer’s ki'haf. K' jordan’s slender pi-maat-kur kar resting svi' t'nash-veh, etek tev-tor wuh ash-tor heh sauntered pa' wuh bah-ker. Wuh tray t' cocktails markau na' etek k'fai wuh twilight, heh etek hayal-tor ne' na' wuh pasu k' wuh dahkuh ko-kan svi' kin-kur heh rehkuh sasu, tik veh puragtau tor etek u' mr. Mumble. “tor sarlah du tor aifa parties k'ashiv?” inquired jordan t' wuh ko-kan be' ish-veh. “wuh kim-shah veh vesh' wuh veh i ragel-tor du na', ” kilko-tor wuh ko-kan, svi' wuh alert confident spes. She da-tor tor ish-veh besu: “wasn’t ish-veh na' du, lucille?” ish-veh vesh' na' lucille, nuh'. “i spo' tor sarlah, ” lucille leralmin-tor. “i worla tun ra i tor, ni i kwon-hau-ov ma wuh rom wak. Lu i vesh' la' kim-shah i tore t'nash-veh gown fi' wuh ku-san, heh au ya'akash me t'nash-veh ahm heh shi'yavekh—svi' wuh wehk gad i prah wuh sakat s' croirier’s k' wuh uzh khru gown svi' ish-veh.” “did du potau ish-veh?” ya'akash jordan. “sure i did. I vesh' going sai-vel-tor ish-veh tonight, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' nuh' suk' svi' wuh bust heh had tor nam-tor rubitau. Ish-veh vesh' pa-tukh pla-kur k' pulu-kur o'lid. Dahkuh hundred heh sheh-leh-kaukuh dollars.” “tra'’s vel funny pa' wuh katravahsu ik’ll tor wuh vel spo' ik, ” leralmin-tor wuh vath ko-kan eagerly. “au doesn’t aitlun sovek trouble k' anybody.” “vi doesn’t?” i inquired. “gatsby. Somebody var-tor me—” wuh dahkuh ko-kan heh jordan gal-tor teretuhr confidentially. “somebody var-tor me au nahp au pustau wuh sasu wuh'wak.” wuh thrill be' dvun-tor abru' ek' t' etek. Wuh rehkuh mr. Mumbles keh'sei fa'rak heh shroi eagerly. “i don’t nah-tor ish-veh’s ni mau ik, ” gyirm'i lucille sceptically; “ish-veh’s weht ik au vesh' wuh german zamasu du' wuh t'naehm.” veh t' wuh sasu nodded svi' wugaya. “i puzhu-tor ik s' wuh sasu vi fai-tor ek' pa' ish-veh, grew abru k' ish-veh svi' germany, ” au assured etek positively. “oh, rai, ” leralmin-tor wuh wuh'rak ko-kan, “ish-veh couldn’t nam-tor ik, fai'ei au vesh' svi' wuh american ya'akash'er du' wuh t'naehm.” u' etwel credulity switched pla' tor ish-veh she gal-tor fa'rak k' buhl'es. “du glazhau na' ish-veh sometimes lu au nah-tor kling’s looking na' ish-veh. I’ll sihaya au pustau wuh sasu.” she wonilau ish-veh bezhun heh shivered. Lucille shivered. Etek ek' da-tor heh glazhau pa' na' gatsby. Ish-veh vesh' testimony tor wuh romantic speculation au vi'le-esh-tor ik tra' vesh' zhal-tor pa' ish-veh s' eifa vi had afer-tor pi' ik ish-veh vesh' bolayatik tor zhal pa' svi' nash panu. Wuh wuh'rak mu'yor-yem—tra' would nam-tor wuh'ashiv veh po' midnight—vesh' i' hasu dvin-tor, heh jordan invited me tor hau ish-veh sha' party, vi vesh' sak-tor pa' wuh pasu fi' wuh vath vla t' wuh bah-ker. Tra' vesh' rehkuh telik couples heh jordan’s escort, wuh persistent undergraduate putan-tor tor khrashik innuendo, heh obviously ne' wuh impression ik sooner il later jordan vesh' going tor yield ish-veh abru ish-veh person tor wuh greater il lesser degree. Instead t' rambling, nash party had korsau wuh dignified homogeneity, heh assumed tor itself wuh nam-tor-lof t' representing wuh staid thol'es t' wuh countryside—she'rak yu-mur condescending tor tev'rak yu-mur heh carefully fi' klashausu tehnat its spectroscopic gaiety. “kal-tor’s prah si', ” zhal-tor jordan, po' wuh somehow wasteful heh inappropriate ulef-wadan; “nash nam-tor mau nuh' polite na' me.” etek prah abru, heh she danau ik etek vesh' going tor talal wuh kasu: i had worla ragel-tor ish-veh, she leralmin-tor, heh ish-veh vesh' tor me uneasy. Wuh undergraduate nodded svi' wuh cynical, melancholy yut. Wuh mofek, wilat etek glanced wuh'rak, vesh' crowded, tonk'peh gatsby vesh' ri tra'. She couldn’t talal ish-veh s' wuh fik t' wuh ash-tor, heh au wasn’t fi' wuh veranda. Fi' wuh pavesh etek ar'kada wuh yauluhk-looking svep, heh lates-tor vi' wuh pid gothic shi'dunap, panelled k' skrim-tor eingelsu oak, heh probably ifis-tor ovsotik s' ein ruin overseas. Wuh stout, svitan-aged sasu, k' masuk' owl-eyed spectacles, vesh' sitting somewhat mon-tor fi' wuh rihk t' wuh lo'uk pasu, staring k' unsteady concentration na' wuh nef t' dunap. U' etek svi-tor au halek-tor excitedly pa' heh linisau jordan s' patam tor ash'ya. “ra tor du nah-tor?” au halishau impetuously. “pa' ra?” au pral-tor ish-veh el'ru na' wuh bookshelves. “pa' ik. U' wuh tukh t' kla-min du needn’t ertau tor ascertain. I ascertained. Au’re yeht.” “wuh dunap?” au nodded. “absolutely yeht—ma thalv heh kanok-vei. I nahp au’d nam-tor wuh nice durable cardboard. Tukh t' kla-min, au’re absolutely yeht. Thalv heh—la'! Lemme gluvaya du.” taking etwel scepticism na' vahl, au rushed tor wuh dunap-tsorayek heh fun-tor k' ral'es veh t' wuh stoddard lectures. “gla-tor!” au maf-tor triumphantly. “ish-veh’s wuh bona-fide krus t' hish-tor tukh. Ish-veh fooled me. Nash fella’s wuh regular belasco. Ish-veh’s wuh triumph. Ra thoroughness! Ra realism! Fai-tor lu tor pehkaya, nuh'—didn’t tresahk wuh thalv. Tonk'peh ra tor du aitlun? Ra tor du gish?” au snatched wuh dunap s' me heh va'prah ish-veh hastily fi' its nef, muttering ik kuv veh dok vesh' snem-tor wuh bosh shi'dunap vesh' liable tor neshaya. “vi katau du?” au halishau. “il did du aishan sarlah? I vesh' katau. Danik sutra vesh' katau.” jordan glazhau na' ish-veh alertly, cheerfully, rik' answering. “i vesh' katau k' wuh kosu ahmau roosevelt, ” au fator. “mrs. Claud roosevelt. Tor du fai-tor ish-veh? I ragel-tor ish-veh ein-wilat kim-shah mu-yor. I’ve vesh' mon-tor na' pa' wuh wehk gad i', heh i nahp ish-veh lau sober me abru tor hayal-tor svi' wuh shi'dunap.” “has ish-veh?” “wuh pi' zeshau, i nah-tor. I mokuhlek’t var-tor wi. I’ve goh vesh' la' wuh wadan. Did i var-tor du pa' wuh dunap? Au’re yeht. Au’re—” “du var-tor etek.” etek hutau el'ru k' ish-veh gravely heh went pla' outdoors. Tra' vesh' taman i' fi' wuh canvas svi' wuh bah-ker; hinek sasu pushing nu'ri ko-kan pla'rak svi' ek'wakik graceless da-kuv, superior couples holding tik vath tortuously, fashionably, heh keeping svi' wuh teruk—heh wuh lo'uk su'etek t' single ko-kan taman individually il relieving wuh orchestra na' wuh moment t' wuh burden t' wuh banjo il wuh pash-tor. K' midnight wuh hilarity had increased. Wuh u'thet tenor had uralau svi' italian, heh wuh notorious contralto had uralau svi' jazz, heh svi' wuh su'etek sutra vesh' doing “stunts” ek' abru' wuh bah-ker, du' kunli, vacuous thorau t' laughter she-tor na' wuh belaar igen. Wuh shif t' skaf t'dahsu, vi da-tor si' tor nam-tor wuh ko-kan svi' kin-kur, did wuh kan-bu bae'cok svi' costume, heh champagne vesh' dvin-tor svi' bezhun-zaneshu bigger do ozh-yerak. Wuh aikum had risen higher, heh floating svi' wuh ralash vesh' wuh reh-vla t' haul-tukh wef, trembling wuh pi' tor wuh stegel, tinny thezh t' wuh banjoes fi' wuh yartra. I vesh' fam dvun k' jordan leipausu. Etek vesh' sitting na' wuh pasu k' wuh sasu t' pa' t'nash-veh ya'shakhuv heh wuh rowdy pi' ko-kan, vi mazhiv-kur-tor yut fi-tor wuh slightest provocation tor uncontrollable laughter. I vesh' enjoying myself i'. I had taken dahkuh ozh-yerak t' champagne, heh wuh scene had rubai fa' t'nash-veh bezhun vi' vel significant, elemental, heh profound. Na' wuh lull svi' wuh entertainment wuh sasu glazhau na' me heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “ish-veh limuk nam-tor familiar, ” au leralmin-tor politely. “weren’t du svi' wuh wuh'rak dahsaya du' wuh t'naehm?” “po ha. I vesh' svi' wuh dah-leh-eighth infantry.” “i vesh' svi' wuh sixteenth abi' belaar leh-nau-leh-oh. I fai-tor i’d gla-tor du ein-wilat fa'.” etek variben na' wuh moment pa' ein masupik, zhai-kur pi' pi'kahr svi' france. Evidently au ha-tor svi' nash vicinity, na' au var-tor me ik au had aishan bought wuh hydroplane, heh vesh' going tor ar'kadan ish-veh si' svi' wuh asal. “aitlun tor hal-tor k' me, hinek torvukh? Aishan be' wuh gef bi' wuh ralash.” “ra wak?” “sovek wak ik saikhut du buhfik.” ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh um t' t'nash-veh lahv tor ya'akash ish-veh ahm lu jordan glazhau pa' heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “having wuh sa-ka-ashausu wak i'?” she inquired. “mau weh-rom.” i da-tor va'ashiv tor t'nash-veh uzh acquaintance. “nash nam-tor wuh ritsuri party na' me. I haven’t kauk gla-tor wuh kasu. I ha-tor abru' tra'—” i pral-tor t'nash-veh el'ru na' wuh invisible labah svi' wuh ir, “heh nash sasu gatsby satau abru' ish-veh chauffeur k' wuh k'waw'zhe.” na' wuh moment au glazhau na' me u' kuv au vravshau tor ken-tor. “i’m gatsby, ” au leralmin-tor suddenly. “ra!” i sporiben. “oh, i eit'jae ish-veh pardon.” “i nahp du fai-tor, hinek torvukh. I’m kwes i’m ri wuh maut rom kasu.” au abru'teruklar-ru'lut understandingly—mau weht do understandingly. Ish-veh vesh' veh t' eifa ritsuri abru'teruklar-ru'lut k' wuh quality t' ek'wakik reassurance svi' ish-veh, ik du lau sarlah mes' kehkuh il kaukuh wak svi' ha'kiv. Ish-veh limuk-tor—il seemed tor limuk—wuh bosh ek'wakik panu na' wuh instant, heh yi concentrated fi' du k' wuh irresistible prejudice svi' ish-veh favour. Ish-veh ken-tor du aishan ni irak u' du aitlu tor nam-tor ken-tor, pudva-tor svi' du u' du would spo' tor dva-tor svi' yourself, heh assured du ik ish-veh had precisely wuh impression t' du ik, na' ish-veh buhfik, du rok-tor tor zhelesh. Precisely na' ik sfek ish-veh vanished—heh i vesh' looking na' wuh sohkik nu'ri roughneck, wuh tevun il dahkuh abru' reh-leh, t'vi elaborate formality t' starun aishan din-tor hasu absurd. Ein wak fa' au puragtau himself i’d prah wuh karik impression ik au vesh' picking ish-veh zhit k' tun. Siyah na' wuh moment lu mr. Gatsby shasutan-tor himself wuh butler hurried na' ish-veh k' wuh ro'fori ik chicago vesh' calling ish-veh fi' wuh raf-elakh. Au tobeg-tor himself k' wuh pi' kes-wun ik vinan-tor tik t' etek svi' da-tor. “kuv du aitlun sovek-vel aishan ya'akash na' ish-veh, hinek torvukh, ” au urged me. “tobeg me. I dungi rejoin du later.” lu au vesh' hal-tor i da-tor iyi tor jordan—constrained tor assure ish-veh t' t'nash-veh ak'wikmun. I had gishu ik mr. Gatsby would nam-tor wuh florid heh corpulent person svi' ish-veh svitan tevun. “vi nam-tor au?” i halishau. “tor du fai-tor?” “au’s aishan wuh sasu ahmau gatsby.” “wilat nam-tor au s', i tvai? Heh ra tor au tor?” “i' du’re palikau fi' wuh subject, ” she kilko-tor k' wuh wan abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “muhl, au var-tor me wuh'wak au vesh' wuh oxford sasu.” wuh neik-ha'khlup za-mesu palikau tor nem-tor shid za' ish-veh, tonk'peh na' ish-veh thurai remark ish-veh spoh-tor maf. “however, i don’t dva-tor ish-veh.” “po ri?” “i don’t fai-tor, ” she insisted, “i aishan don’t nah-tor au went tra'.” vel svi' ish-veh molu reminded me t' wuh vath ko-kan’s “i nah-tor au pustau wuh sasu, ” heh had wuh daya t' stimulating t'nash-veh curiosity. I would ma nar-tor rik' deshker wuh ro'fori ik gatsby sprang s' wuh flash t' louisiana il s' wuh weh-neik she'rak vla t' uzh york. Ik vesh' comprehensible. Tonk'peh nu'ri sasu didn’t—k'puu svi' t'nash-veh provincial inexperience i pudva-tor au didn’t—maraya coolly s' nowhere heh mahr-tor wuh palace fi' wu vikuvtra ralash. “anyhow, au mazhiv-kur-tor suk parties, ” leralmin-tor jordan, rubai wuh subject k' wuh urban distaste na' wuh nok. “heh i spo' suk parties. Au’re ni intimate. Na' pi' parties tra' isn’t sovek awek'es.” tra' vesh' wuh ork t' wuh neralash vluhn, heh wuh spes t' wuh orchestra leader rang si' suddenly abru' wuh echolalia t' wuh bah-ker. “t'sai heh gentlemen, ” au maf-tor. “na' wuh ya'akash t' mr. Gatsby etek nam-tor going tor mavau na' du mr. Vladmir tostoff’s latest ar'kadan, if skamau ni mau attention na' carnegie tvur kim-shah lau. Kuv du telv-tor wuh dun du fai-tor tra' vesh' wuh suk' kashan.” au abru'teruklar-ru'lut k' jovial condescension, heh hau: “ein kashan!” whereupon kanok-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “wuh krus nam-tor fainu, ” au concluded lustily, “u' ‘vladmir tostoff’s jazz vesht-var t' wuh panu!’ ” wuh malat t' mr. Tostoff’s composition savlau me, fai'ei aishan u' ish-veh began t'nash-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi' gatsby, standing sa'awek fi' wuh marble ash-tor heh looking s' veh travek tor wuh'ashiv k' approving bezhun. Ish-veh tanned wadi vesh' drawn attractively wufik fi' ish-veh limuk heh ish-veh pen isachya glazhau u' hi ish-veh vesh' trimmed kanok gad. Kupi gla-tor nash-veh nothing sinister pa' ish-veh. I wondered kuv wuh kla-min ik au vesh' ri drinking gol-tor tor eku ish-veh ska' s' ish-veh be'hai'la, na' ish-veh seemed tor me ik au grew weht yeht u' wuh fraternal hilarity increased. Lu wuh “jazz vesht-var t' wuh panu” vesh' abru', ko-kan vesh' putting ish-veh patam fi' sasu’s tipan svi' wuh puppyish, convivial yut, ko-kan vesh' swooning pla'rak playfully vi' sasu’s kar, kauk vi' travek, fai-tor ik ein-veh would pehkaya ish-veh tevan-tor—tonk'peh kling swooned pla'rak fi' gatsby, heh rai french bob estuhl gatsby’s tipan, heh rai uralaun kehek vesh' shidau k' gatsby’s patam na' veh naf. “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon.” gatsby’s butler vesh' suddenly standing be' etek. “din-tor leipausu?” au inquired. “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon, tonk'peh mr. Gatsby would spo' tor stariben tor du sa'awek.” “k' me?” she sporiben svi' ak'wikmun. “ha, madame.” she prah abru slowly, raising ish-veh bezhun-zehl na' me svi' astonishment, heh zahal-tor wuh butler na' wuh kelek. I pubeglanau ik she sai-vel-tor ish-veh khru-sai-vel, ek' ish-veh sai-vel, spo' torvukh sai-vel—tra' vesh' wuh jauntiness pa' ish-veh dvun u' kuv she had wuh'rak oren-tor tor lates fi-tor golf rivak fi' sok'i, crisp asal. I vesh' sa'awek heh ish-veh vesh' siyah dahkuh. Na' ein wak confused heh intriguing sounds had issued s' wuh wu, wehk-windowed tvi-shal if overhung wuh nef. Eluding jordan’s undergraduate, vi vesh' i' engaged svi' wuh obstetrical conversation k' dahkuh sular uralaun ko-kan, heh vi implored me tor hau ish-veh, i went svi'udish. Wuh suk tvi-shal vesh' bosh t' sutra. Veh t' wuh ko-kan svi' kin-kur vesh' mavaun wuh piano, heh be' ish-veh lam-tor wuh ha-vol, yon-kur-haired nu'ri t'sai s' wuh khinik sular uralaun, engaged svi' song. She had mon-tor wuh nosahp t' champagne, heh du' wuh rivak t' ish-veh song she had klopau, ineptly, ik kanok-vei vesh' maut, maut maf—she vesh' ri goh uralaun, she vesh' weeping nuh'. Whenever tra' vesh' wuh svizh svi' wuh song she boshau ish-veh k' gasping, pushau sobs, heh yi nem-tor abru wuh lyric va'ashiv svi' wuh quavering soprano. Wuh bezhun-masu coursed ne' ish-veh nak—ri freely, however, na' lu sarlah au vi' contact k' ish-veh heavily beaded bezhun-isach au assumed wuh inky kur, heh pursued wuh shom t' ish-veh yut svi' vohris nesh-kur rivulets. Wuh humorous suggestion vesh' tor ik she uralau wuh pitoh fi' ish-veh limuk, whereupon she threw abru ish-veh el'ru, sank vi' wuh ku-san, heh went ska' vi' wuh glu vinous yuk. “she had wuh puk k' wuh sasu vi leralmin-tor au’s ish-veh sa-telsu, ” danau wuh ko-kan na' t'nash-veh kar-nef. I glazhau pa'. Danik t' wuh remaining kosu vesh' i' having puk-tor k' sasu leralmin-tor tor nam-tor ish-veh sa-telsu. Kauk jordan’s party, wuh kehek s' she'rak yu-mur, vesh' rent asunder k' dissension. Veh t' wuh sasu vesh' talking k' curious flan'es tor wuh nu'ri fundauik-ithop, heh ish-veh ko-telsu, po' attempting tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' wuh situation svi' wuh dignified heh indifferent yut, shau ne' entirely heh resorted tor flank nashiv-tor—na' tvi-wak she saudau suddenly na' ish-veh vla spo' wuh reshnek lerash-khush, heh shisau: “du ugau!” vi' ish-veh kaluk. Wuh reluctance tor hal-tor ha-kel vesh' ri confined tor wayward sasu. Wuh tvur vesh' na' la' occupied k' dahkuh deplorably sober sasu heh ish-veh highly indignant ko-telsu. Wuh ko-telsu vesh' sympathizing k' tik vath svi' slightly ashenau spes. “whenever gla-tor ish-veh i’m having wuh rom wak au aitlu tor hal-tor ha-kel.” “worla puzhu-tor sovek-vel ni selfish svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv.” “etek’re kwon-hau-ov wuh wuh'rak ones tor trasha.” “ni nam-tor etek.” “muhl, etek’re siyah wuh kim-shah tonight, ” leralmin-tor veh t' wuh sasu sheepishly. “wuh orchestra losrak ulef wuh wadan ago.” svi' spite t' wuh ko-telsu’ agreement ik such malevolence vesh' mesakh credibility, wuh dispute shahtau svi' wuh pen struggle, heh fi' ko-telsu vesh' abertau, kicking, vi' wuh mu-yor. U' i bek-tor na' t'nash-veh taik svi' wuh tvur wuh svep t' wuh shi'dunap tu'ash heh jordan leipausu heh gatsby sasarlah teretuhr. Au vesh' taran ein kim-shah zhit tor ish-veh, tonk'peh wuh eagerness svi' ish-veh manner tightened abruptly vi' formality u' several sutra betau ish-veh tor leralmin goodbye. Jordan’s party vesh' calling impatiently tor ish-veh s' wuh porch, tonk'peh she svizh-tor na' wuh moment tor hutau el'ru. “i’ve aishan puzhu-tor wuh danik taurauk vel, ” she zhal-tor. “uf wu vesh' etek svi' tra'?” “po, pa' wuh wadan.” “ish-veh vesh' … veling taurauk, ” she ashiv-tor abstractedly. “tonk'peh i swore i wouldn’t var-tor ish-veh heh la' i am tantalizing du.” she luvau gracefully svi' t'nash-veh limuk. “sanoi sarlah heh gla-tor me … phone dunap … ne' wuh ahm t' mrs. Sigourney howard … t'nash-veh ezyet …” she vesh' hurrying ska' u' she variben—ish-veh khav-kur el'ru pral-tor wuh jaunty salute u' she klimtau vi' ish-veh party na' wuh svep. I aitlu tor danau ik i’d shi'kar na' ish-veh lehkuh-mal svi' wuh khru heh tor apologize na' ri having fainu ish-veh svi' wuh bah-ker. “don’t mention ish-veh, ” au enjoined me eagerly. “don’t mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh'ashiv nahp, hinek torvukh.” wuh familiar sagluvaya meskarau rai weht familiarity do wuh el'ru if reassuringly brushed t'nash-veh tipan. “heh don’t yen-tor etek’re going abru svi' wuh hydroplane fa-gad asal, na' naukuh o’wak-vel.” yi wuh butler, za' ish-veh tipan: “philadelphia aitlu du fi' wuh phone, osu.” “ek' gas'rak, svi' wuh minute. Var-tor au i’ll nam-tor gas'rak tra' … rom mu-yor.” “rom mu-yor.” “rom mu-yor.” au abru'teruklar-ru'lut—heh suddenly tra' seemed tor nam-tor wuh vaksurik significance svi' having vesh' among wuh kim-shah tor hal-tor, u' kuv au had aitlu ish-veh ek' wuh wak. “rom mu-yor, hinek torvukh … rom mu-yor.” tonk'peh u' i lates-tor ne' wuh ash-tor vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik wuh khru vesh' ri ved abru'. Kau-leh ash'ya s' wuh svep wuh dozen headlights illuminated wuh bizarre heh tumultuous scene. Svi' wuh razh be' wuh fau-yut, gas'rak vla abru, tonk'peh violently shorn t' veh halek, shom-tor wuh uzh coupé if had losrak gatsby’s yetur ri dahkuh minutes fa'. Wuh nasik jut t' wuh temok accounted na' wuh detachment t' wuh halek, if vesh' i' getting considerable attention s' ulef wuh dozen curious chauffeurs. However, u' au had losrak ish-veh poiq'lid blocking wuh fau-yut, wuh harsh, discordant stiralash s' eifa svi' wuh za' had vesh' zhu-yehat na' ein wak, heh hau tor wuh already khrashik confusion t' wuh scene. Wuh sasu svi' wuh wu duster had dismounted s' wuh vashau heh i' lam-tor svi' wuh svitan t' wuh fau-yut, looking s' wuh poiq'lid tor wuh tyre heh s' wuh tyre tor wuh observers svi' wuh vaksurik, puzzled yut. “gla-tor!” au danau. “ish-veh went svi' wuh razh.” wuh kla-min vesh' infinitely astonishing tor ish-veh, heh i recognized wuh'rak wuh ritsuri quality t' wonder, heh yi wuh sasu—ish-veh vesh' wuh tab-ma patron t' gatsby’s shi'dunap. “uf’d ish-veh pavesh-tor?” au shrugged ish-veh tipan. “i fai-tor nothing whatever pa' tor-velsu, ” au leralmin-tor decisively. “tonk'peh uf did ish-veh pavesh-tor? Did du sahr-tor vi' wuh temok?” “don’t ya'akash me, ” leralmin-tor owl bezhun, washing ish-veh el'ru t' wuh bosh tukh. “i fai-tor maut pi' pa' driving—nam-tor' nothing. Ish-veh pavesh-tor, heh ik’s ek' i fai-tor.” “muhl, kuv du’re wuh ri donku-tor yetursu du oughtn’t tor ar'kadan driving na' mu-yor.” “tonk'peh i wasn’t kauk trying, ” au danau indignantly, “i wasn’t kauk trying.” wuh putesha hush tevan-tor fi-tor wuh bystanders. “tor du aitlun tor kugau suicide?” “du’re kunli ish-veh vesh' aishan wuh halek! Wuh rasahkos yetursu heh ri kauk trying!” “du don’t ken-tor, ” danau wuh criminal. “i wasn’t driving. Tra'’s wuh'ashiv sasu svi' wuh poiq'lid.” wuh kolaya ik zahal-tor nash afsakaya afer-tor spes svi' wuh potun-tor “ah-h-h!” u' wuh svep t' wuh coupé swung slowly tu'ash. Wuh patreitan—ish-veh vesh' i' wuh patreitan—ash-tor pla' involuntarily, heh lu wuh svep had tu'ash eik tra' vesh' wuh ghostly svizh. Yi, maut gradually, krus k' krus, wuh spoh, dangling wuhsu ash-tor s' wuh vashau, pawing tentatively na' wuh solektra k' wuh suk uncertain taman ash'el. Blinded k' wuh glare t' wuh headlights heh confused k' wuh incessant groaning t' wuh stonn, wuh apparition lam-tor swaying na' wuh moment fa' au pakashogau wuh sasu svi' wuh duster. “wha’s tukh?” au inquired calmly. “did etek sahr-tor outa pa-tukh?” “glazhau!” ulef wuh dozen ozh sfekau na' wuh sanesh-tor halek—au nantau na' ish-veh na' wuh moment, heh yi glazhau abru'le u' hi au suspected ik ish-veh had eku-tor s' wuh igen. “sarlah ish-veh ska', ” ein-veh danau. Au nodded. “palikauk i stiralash’ beglanau etek’d pehkau.” wuh svizh. Yi, taking wuh wu esh heh straightening ish-veh tipan, au remarked svi' wuh satalau spes: “wonder’ff var-tor me wilat tra'’s wuh pa-tukh’zehl wurzel?” k'puu wuh dozen sasu, ein t' au wuh pi' weh-rom ska' do au vesh', danau tor ish-veh ik halek heh poiq'lid vesh' rai longer hau k' sovek tukhik tel-tor. “pla' si', ” au suggested po' wuh moment. “shitau ish-veh svi' reverse.” “tonk'peh wuh halek’s ska'!” au hesitated. “rai klau svi' trying, ” au leralmin-tor. Wuh caterwauling stonn had pulau wuh crescendo heh i da-tor maf heh tresahk mes' wuh yartra na' ha-kel. I glanced pla' wuh'wak. Wuh wafer t' wuh aikum vesh' shining abru' gatsby’s kelek, tor wuh mu-yor tok-ti u' fa', heh surviving wuh laughter heh wuh ralash t' ish-veh fam dvun glowing bah-ker. Wuh sudden emptiness seemed tor yumaya i' s' wuh krani heh wuh lo'uk svep, endowing k' ovsotik isolation wuh khlop t' wuh kasu, vi lam-tor fi' wuh porch, ish-veh el'ru abru svi' wuh hotorik gesture t' rom-halan. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ telvan abru' ra i ma written ni irak, gla-tor nash-veh i ma putan-tor wuh impression ik wuh pavek t' rehkuh mu-yor several wehk gad k'wuhli vesh' ek' ik absorbed me. Fi' wuh contrary, au vesh' goh casual pavek svi' wuh crowded belaar, heh, abi' mau later, au absorbed me infinitely lehkuh tor t'nash-veh personal tek'ik. Danik t' wuh wak i ar'kada. Svi' wuh lehkuh-mal asal wuh yel threw t'nash-veh duv na'tev'rak u' i hurried ne' wuh wan-kur chasms t' weh-neik uzh york tor wuh probity sahrafel. I fai-tor wuh vath clerks heh nu'ri tel-tor-salesmen k' ish-veh wuh'rak ahm, heh lunched k' au svi' gu'gelik, crowded restaurants fi' pi' pig kahm heh mashed potatoes heh mon. I kauk had wuh pen tek'ik k' wuh ko-kan vi ha-tor svi' jersey kahr heh ar'kada svi' wuh accounting department, tonk'peh ish-veh sa-kai began throwing tvai glazhau svi' t'nash-veh kharat, ni lu she went fi' ish-veh vacation svi' july i kal-tor ish-veh salur quietly maf. I nem-tor aru-yem usually na' wuh yale muhd—na' ein utvau ish-veh vesh' wuh gloomiest pavek t' t'nash-veh gad—heh yi i went upstairs tor wuh shi'dunap heh orenau investments heh shar'es na' wuh conscientious wadan. Tra' vesh' paik wuh zamu rioters pa', tonk'peh au worla sarlah vi' wuh shi'dunap, ni ish-veh vesh' wuh rom shi tor ar'kadan. Po' ik, kuv wuh mu-yor vesh' mellow, i strolled ne' madison avenue vesht wuh hinek murray kunel hotel, heh abru' 33rd yut tor wuh pennsylvania wurzel. I began tor spo' uzh york, wuh racy, adventurous olau t' ish-veh na' mu-yor, heh wuh satisfaction ik wuh ek'kayik hanuvaya t' sasu heh kosu heh mish-vel mazhiv-kur-tor tor wuh restless bezhun. I tishau tor lates abru fifth avenue heh pick si' romantic kosu s' wuh patreitan heh glenonau ik svi' wuh zamu minutes i vesh' going tor svi-tor vi' ish-veh ha-tor, heh kling would ek'wak fai-tor il disapprove. Sometimes, svi' t'nash-veh kashek, i zahal-tor au tor ish-veh ha-shal fi' wuh teruk t' ipik yut, heh au da-tor heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut pla' na' me fa' au spoh-tor k'fai wuh svep vi' lamekh mu'khlup'es. Na' wuh enchanted metropolitan twilight i olau wuh haunting loneliness sometimes, heh olau ish-veh svi' vath—ri donku-tor nu'ri clerks vi loitered svi' khom t' krani waiting abi' ish-veh vesh' wak na' wuh solitary restaurant aru-yem—nu'ri clerks svi' wuh dusk, wasting wuh danik poignant moments t' mu-yor heh ha'kiv. Va'ashiv na' ohkuh o’wak-vel, lu wuh gu'gelik lanes t' wuh forties vesh' zehl-tor kaukuh glu k' throbbing taxicabs, bound na' wuh theatre kahkrus, i olau wuh sinking svi' t'nash-veh khaf-spol. Shidau gal-tor teretuhr svi' wuh taxis u' au bek-tor, heh spes sang, heh tra' vesh' laughter s' unheard kha'wal, heh lighted cigarettes tor unintelligible da-kuv svi'udish. Imagining ik i, nuh', vesh' hurrying na' gaiety heh thresh-tor ish-veh intimate tepor'es, i istau au muhl. Na' wuh du' i pakik glan t' jordan leipausu, heh yi svi' midsummer i afer-tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Palikauk i vesh' snuhkrol-tor tor hal-tor shitau k' ish-veh, fai'ei she vesh' wuh golf skilamu, heh kanok-veh fai-tor ish-veh ahm. Yi ish-veh vesh' vel weht. I wasn’t actually svi' ashaya, tonk'peh i olau wuh wihfelau t' sival curiosity. Wuh bored haughty limuk ik she da-tor tor wuh panu ip-sut vel—danik affectations ip-sut vel eventually, kauk hi au don’t svi' wuh palikaya—heh veh gad i afer-tor ra ish-veh vesh'. Lu etek vesh' fi' wuh kelek-party teretuhr abru svi' warwick, she losrak wuh yahv-tor poiq'lid si' svi' wuh sov-masu k' wuh fik ne', heh yi ti pa' ish-veh—heh suddenly i vokau wuh var pa' ish-veh ik had savlau me ik mu-yor na' daisy’s. Na' ish-veh wuh'rak suk' golf tournament tra' vesh' wuh zehl ik nearly pulau wuh newspapers—wuh suggestion ik she had dvun-tor ish-veh rin'k'n s' wuh rasahkos ti svi' wuh semifinal pauk. Wuh vel betau wuh proportions t' wuh scandal—yi tev-tor maf. Wuh caddy retracted ish-veh star-krus, heh wuh goh vath toglantausu nafai-tor ik au lau ma vesh' mistaken. Wuh incident heh wuh ahm had hafau teretuhr svi' t'nash-veh kashek. Jordan leipausu instinctively nan'woi clever, shrewd sasu, heh i' vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik nash vesh' fai'ei she olau safer fi' wuh sov-hali wilat sovek sataya s' wuh kiht would nam-tor nahp impossible. She vesh' incurably ritrau. She wasn’t kup tor palesh-tor hasu na' wuh disadvantage heh, putan-tor nash unwillingness, i suppose she had palikau dealing svi' subterfuges lu she vesh' maut nu'ri svi' zek tor potau ik samuyau, insolent abru'teruklar-ru'lut da-tor tor wuh panu heh wi satisfy wuh halishau t' ish-veh lerash, jaunty ak'shem. Ish-veh tor rai natyan tor me. Dishonesty svi' wuh kosu nam-tor wuh vel du worla tenai deeply—i vesh' casually sorry, heh yi i forgot. Ish-veh vesh' fi' ik ka kelek-party ik etek had wuh curious conversation pa' driving wuh poiq'lid. Ish-veh palikau fai'ei she be' dvun-tor ni beyik ein workmen ik etwel fender flicked wuh gonaf fi' veh sasu’s tor-pal. “du’re wuh rotten yetursu, ” i protested. “either du ought tor nam-tor weht tun-bosh, il du oughtn’t tor yetur na' ek'.” “i am tun-bosh.” “rai, du’re ri.” “muhl, vath sutra nam-tor, ” she leralmin-tor lightly. “ra’s ik prah tor tor k' ish-veh?” “au’ll potau s' t'nash-veh yut, ” she insisted. “ish-veh nem-tor dahkuh tor tor wuh kisheya.” “suppose du ragel-tor somebody aishan u' careless u' yourself.” “i rok i worla dungi, ” she kilko-tor. “i fnu-ven careless sutra. Ik’s po i spo' du.” ish-veh zhai-kur, yel-ish-veh-tor bezhun nantau zehik ahead, tonk'peh she had deliberately izau etwel relations, heh na' wuh moment i nahp i ashau ish-veh. Tonk'peh i am vohris-thinking heh bosh t' interior tor-go ik bae'cok u' vohrayek fi' t'nash-veh aitlu, heh i fai-tor ik wuh'rak i had tor prah myself definitely s' ik tangle pla' ha-kel. I’d vesh' kitaun nuhm wuh'wak wuh wehk gad heh signing au: “ashaya, nick, ” heh ek' i kupi nah-tor t' vesh' uf, lu ik ac'ruth ko-kan mavau tennis, wuh faint moustache t' wadashaya saudau fi' ish-veh upper bru. Nevertheless tra' vesh' wuh vague understanding ik had tor nam-tor tactfully pushau ska' fa' i vesh' elik. Kanok-veh suspects himself t' k'puu veh t' wuh cardinal virtues, heh nash nam-tor t'nash-veh: i am veh t' wuh zamu trau sutra ik i ma ek'wak fainu. Iv fi' gad asal du' church kus-vakh rang svi' wuh pi'kahr alongshore, wuh panu heh its mistress fun-tor tor gatsby’s kelek heh twinkled hilariously fi' ish-veh yartra. “au’s wuh bootlegger, ” leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri t'sai, dvun-tor ein-wilat svi' ish-veh cocktails heh ish-veh svai. “veh wak au pustau wuh sasu vi had afer-tor si' ik au vesh' sa-bath tor von hindenburg heh dahr krei tor wuh e'shua. Pulau me wuh she-tor, honey, heh mukau me wuh kim-shah eku vi' ik tra' khush makh.” wuh'wak i kitau ne' fi' wuh herbosh ret t' wuh timetable wuh ahm t' eifa vi sarlah tor gatsby’s kelek ik belaar. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh hinek timetable i', disintegrating na' its hesha, heh headed “nash schedule svi' daya july 5th, 1922.” tonk'peh i mokuhlek fam dvun telv-tor wuh zhai-kur ahm, heh au dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh weh-rom impression do t'nash-veh generalities t' eifa vi nar-tor gatsby’s hospitality heh vlitau ish-veh wuh subtle tribute t' fai-tor nothing whatever pa' ish-veh. S' she'rak yu-mur, yi, sarlah wuh chester beckers heh wuh leeches, heh wuh sasu ahmau bunsen, ik i fai-tor na' yale, heh hassu webster civet, vi vesh' mastevau kim-shah belaar abru svi' maine. Heh wuh hornbeams heh wuh willie voltaires, heh wuh bosh maat ahmau blackbuck, vi kwon-hau-ov hoknau svi' wuh teruk heh vathlau abru ish-veh han spo' vralt na' whosoever sarlah be'. Heh wuh ismays heh wuh chrysties (il rather hubert auerbach heh mr. Chrystie’s ko-telsu), heh edgar beaver, t'vi isachya, au leralmin, da-tor cotton-wan-kur veh karil aru na' rai rom utvau na' ek'. Clarence endive vesh' s' she'rak yu-mur, u' i vokau. Sarlah ish-veh goh wuh'wak, svi' wan-kur knickerbockers, heh had wuh puk k' wuh bum ahmau etty svi' wuh bah-ker. S' weh-irak si' fi' wuh vikuvtra sarlah wuh cheadles heh wuh o. R. P. Schraeders, heh wuh stonewall jackson abrams t' georgia, heh wuh fishguards heh wuh ripley snells. Snell vesh' tra' rehkuh gad fa' au went tor wuh penitentiary, ni mon-tor si' fi' wuh krus-kov yetur ik mrs. Ulysses swett’s automobile sahr-tor abru' ish-veh gas'rak el'ru. Wuh dancies sarlah, nuh', heh s. B. Whitebait, vi vesh' muhl abru' sheh-leh, heh maurice wuh. Flink, heh wuh hammerheads, heh beluga wuh tobacco importer, heh beluga’s ko-kan. S' tev'rak yu-mur sarlah wuh fek heh wuh mulreadys heh cecil roebuck heh cecil schoen heh gulick wuh fupa s' senator heh newton orchid, vi tash-tor films par marom'es, heh eckhaust heh clyde cohen heh don s. Schwartz (wuh sa-fu) heh arthur mccarty, ek' tersau k' wuh movies svi' veh yut il wuh'ashiv. Heh wuh catlips heh wuh bembergs heh g. Earl muldoon, sa-kai tor ik muldoon vi afterward strangled ish-veh ko-telsu. Da fontano wuh promoter sarlah tra', heh ed legros heh james b. (“nehaya-gut”) ferret heh wuh de jongs heh ernest lilly—sarlah au tor gamble, heh lu ferret czar-tor vi' wuh bah-ker ish-veh tvai au vesh' pu-tor si' heh katravah traction would ma tor kapralau profitably thurai gad. Wuh sasu ahmau klipspringer vesh' tra' ni k'ashiv ik au became fainu u' “wuh boarder”—i vet kuv au had sovek vath ha-kel. T' theatrical sutra tra' vesh' gus waize heh horace o’donavan heh lester myer heh george duckweed heh francis bull. Isha s' uzh york vesh' wuh chromes heh wuh backhyssons heh wuh dennickers heh russel betty heh wuh corrigans heh wuh kellehers heh wuh dewars heh wuh scullys heh s. W. Belcher heh wuh smirkes heh wuh nu'ri quinns, divorced i', heh henry l. Palmetto, vi pustau himself k' jumping svi' khom t' wuh subway ranau svi' wak keh-vla. Benny mcclenahan lasha kwon-hau-ov k' kehkuh ko-kan. Au vesh' worla ved wuh ka ones svi' tukhik person, tonk'peh au vesh' ni ka veh k' wuh'ashiv ik ish-veh inevitably seemed au had vesh' tra' fa'. I ma yen-tor ish-veh ahm—jaqueline, i nah-tor, il else consuela, il gloria il judy il belaar, heh ish-veh kim-shah ahm vesh' either wuh melodious ahm t' svai heh tevun-krus il wuh sterner ones t' wuh lo'uk american capitalists t'vi krei, kuv hish-tor, au would confess themselves tor nam-tor. Svi' haya tor ek' aifa i mokuhlek vokau ik faustina o’brien sarlah tra' k'puu wuh'wak heh wuh baedeker ko-kan heh nu'ri brewer, vi had ish-veh han pohshaya ska' svi' wuh t'naehm, heh mr. Albrucksburger heh din-tor haag, ish-veh fiancée, heh ardita fitz-peters heh mr. P. Jewett, wuh'wak patam t' wuh american legion, heh din-tor claudia gaf, k' wuh sasu reputed tor nam-tor ish-veh chauffeur, heh wuh prince t' vel, ik etek puvutau duke, heh t'vi ahm, kuv i ek'wak fai-tor ish-veh, i ma yen-tor. Ek' aifa sutra sarlah tor gatsby’s kelek svi' wuh belaar. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ na' naukuh o’wak-vel, veh asal tab-ma svi' july, gatsby’s gorgeous poiq'lid lurched abru wuh rocky yetur tor t'nash-veh svep heh mazhiv-kur-tor si' wuh thorau t' melody s' its rehkuh-noted stonn. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wuh'rak wak au had puvutau fi' me, hi i had hal-tor tor dahkuh t' ish-veh parties, mounted svi' ish-veh hydroplane, heh, na' ish-veh akali k'waw'zhe, tor vakavik nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh shahov. “rom asal, hinek torvukh. Du’re having khi-gad-yem k' me nash-gad heh i nahp etek’d fau abru teretuhr.” au vesh' balancing himself fi' wuh glutash-dohn t' ish-veh poiq'lid k' ik resourcefulness t' dvun ik nam-tor ni peculiarly american—ik sarlah, i suppose, k' wuh k'torr lifting ar'kadan svi' youth heh, kauk weht, k' wuh shid-fam takov t' etwel nervous, sporadic zhagra. Nash quality vesh' continually breaking k'fai ish-veh punctilious manner svi' wuh shid t' restlessness. Au vesh' worla ved fam dvun; tra' vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh tapping ash'ya ein-wilat il wuh impatient sharu heh ikapik t' wuh el'ru. Gla-tor ish-veh me looking k' admiration na' ish-veh poiq'lid. “ish-veh’s takov, isn’t ish-veh, hinek torvukh?” au spen-tor ska' tor mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh weh-rom zan-tor. “haven’t du ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh fa'?” i’d gla-tor ish-veh. Kanok-veh had gla-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh don-ka dyrk kur, ugelik k' orn-tukh, puvik la' heh tra' svi' its monstrous wu-vath k' triumphant hatboxes heh mu'yor-yem-natuhn heh toolboxes, heh terraced k' wuh labyrinth t' salan-krani ik mirrored wuh dozen yel. Sitting ne' za' wehk zhai-tukh t' makh svi' wuh wihfelau t' yar-kur duf conservatory, etek palikau tor kahr. I had variben k' ish-veh sos'eh ulef wuh dozen wak svi' wuh vesht tevun-krus heh afer-tor, tor t'nash-veh disappointment, ik au had pi' tor leralmin. Ni t'nash-veh wuh'rak impression, ik au vesh' wuh person t' ein undefined consequence, had gradually spoh-tor heh au had shetau veling wuh proprietor t' wuh elaborate roadhouse thurai svep. Heh yi sarlah ik disconcerting fau. Etek hadn’t pulau tev'rak yu-mur pi'kahr fa' gatsby began leaving ish-veh sohkik zhit-bal unfinished heh slapping himself indecisively fi' wuh mal-nef t' ish-veh caramel-kur-tor saikhut. “glazhau la', hinek torvukh, ” au shau si' surprisingly, “ra’s ish-veh opinion t' me, anyhow?” wuh pi' overwhelmed, i began wuh generalized savlaya if ik deshker nazh-tor. “muhl, i’m going tor var-tor du vel pa' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, ” au svi-shau. “i don’t aitlun du tor prah wuh riyeht idea t' me s' ek' aifa var du zhu-tor.” ni au vesh' aware t' wuh bizarre accusations ik flavoured conversation svi' ish-veh tvur. “i’ll var-tor du oekon’s yeht'es.” ish-veh gas'rak el'ru suddenly ordered ekonik retribution tor lamok k'. “i am wuh sa-fu t' ein wealthy sutra svi' wuh svitan tev'rak—ek' tevik i'. I vesh' katau abru svi' america tonk'peh educated na' oxford, fai'ei ek' t'nash-veh orfik-kel ma vesh' educated tra' na' wehk tevun. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh skan ba'tak.” au glazhau na' me sideways—heh i fai-tor po jordan leipausu had pudva-tor au vesh' lying. Au hurried wuh zhit-bal “educated na' oxford, ” il vitem-tor ish-veh, il khluhkau fi' ish-veh, u' hi ish-veh had bothered ish-veh fa'. Heh k' nash vet, ish-veh bosh star-krus tevan-tor tor krus, heh i wondered kuv tra' wasn’t vel wuh pi' sinister pa' ish-veh, po' ek'. “ra krus t' wuh svitan tev'rak?” i inquired casually. “san francisco.” “gla-tor nash-veh.” “t'nash-veh skan ek' tev-tor heh vesht sarlah nash-veh vi' wuh rom deal t' donku.” ish-veh spes vesh' solemn, u' kuv wuh vokaya t' ik sudden ek'tevan t' wuh maat fam dvun haunted ish-veh. Na' wuh moment i suspected ik au vesh' pulling t'nash-veh mal, tonk'peh wuh glance na' ish-veh convinced me vathru. “po' ik i ha-tor spo' wuh nu'ri rajah svi' ek' wuh capitals t' europe—paris, venice, rome—collecting ek'zer, chiefly yon-ek'zer, hunting suk' zhagra, krasan wuh pi', vel na' myself goh, heh trying tor yen-tor vel maut maf ik had pavesh-tor tor me wu ago.” k' wuh urgam i khartau tor restrain t'nash-veh incredulous laughter. Wuh maut zhit-bal vesh' worn ni threadbare ik au evoked rai glakuv kaula ik t' wuh turbaned “character” leaking sawdust na' kanok wadi-sharu u' au pursued wuh tiger k'fai wuh bois de boulogne. “yi sarlah wuh t'naehm, hinek torvukh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh lo'uk vas, heh i ar'kada maut lerash tor tev-tor, tonk'peh i seemed tor lesh wuh enchanted ha'kiv. I nar-tor wuh kadvin u' wuh'rak ot-lan lu ish-veh began. Svi' wuh argonne laptra i nem-tor wuh hafau t' t'nash-veh mish-vel-pohshayek battalion ni irak fa'rak ik tra' vesh' wuh ulef mile haf fi' either vla t' etek wilat wuh infantry couldn’t storilaya. Etek stayed tra' dahkuh gad heh dahkuh mu-yor, wuh hundred heh reh-leh sasu k' leh-sheh lewis pohshayek, heh lu wuh infantry sarlah abru na' kim-shah au afer-tor wuh terseht t' rehkuh german dahsaya among wuh tuh t' tevik. I vesh' promoted tor nam-tor wuh tra-lan, heh kanok puk'ai'la government mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh decoration—kauk montenegro, pi' montenegro ne' fi' wuh adriatic masutra!” pi' montenegro! Au abertau abru wuh zhit heh nodded na' au—k' ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut comprehended montenegro’s troubled vesht-var heh sympathized k' wuh kyi'i struggles t' wuh montenegrin sutra. Ish-veh appreciated fully wuh naf-elakh t' national circumstances if had elicited nash tribute s' montenegro’s lamekh pi' khaf-spol. T'nash-veh incredulity vesh' submerged svi' sem i'; ish-veh vesh' spo' skimming hastily k'fai wuh dozen magazines. Au pulau svi' ish-veh abru'lik, heh wuh krus t' mokev, slung fi' wuh ribbon, tevan-tor vi' t'nash-veh ku. “ik’s wuh veh s' montenegro.” tor t'nash-veh astonishment, wuh vel had wuh authentic glazhau. “orderi di danilo, ” sahr-tor wuh raf-kuvik legend, “montenegro, nicolas rex.” “da-tor ish-veh.” “tra-lan jay gatsby, ” i telv-tor, “na' valour wehtsuri.” “la'’s wuh'ashiv vel i kwon-hau-ov lesh. Wuh souvenir t' oxford gad. Ish-veh vesh' taken svi' trinity quad—wuh sasu fi' t'nash-veh losrak nam-tor i' wuh earl t' doncaster.” ish-veh vesh' wuh ha'gel-bikuv t' ulef wuh dozen nu'ri sasu svi' blazers loafing svi' wuh archway k'fai'ei vesh' visible wuh kasu t' spires. Tra' vesh' gatsby, looking wuh pi', ri mau, younger—k' wuh cricket starok svi' ish-veh el'ru. Yi ish-veh vesh' ek' yeht. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh wadi t' tigers flaming svi' ish-veh palace fi' wuh grand masu-yut; vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh sharu wuh tuf t' yon-ek'zer tor ease, k' ish-veh hirat-kur-lighted gluder, wuh gnawings t' ish-veh pushau khaf-spol. “i’m going tor tor wuh suk' ya'akash t' du nash-gad, ” au leralmin-tor, pocketing ish-veh souvenirs k' satisfaction, “ni i nahp du ought tor fai-tor vel pa' me. I didn’t aitlun du tor nah-tor i vesh' aishan ein kling. Gla-tor du, i usually talal myself among ri-fainusu fai'ei i maraya la' heh tra' trying tor yen-tor wuh maf vel ik pavesh-tor tor me.” au hesitated. “du’ll zhu-tor pa' ish-veh nash aru.” “na' khi-gad-yem?” “rai, nash aru. I pavesh-tor tor talal si' ik du’re taking din-tor leipausu tor theris-masu.” “tor du tvai du’re svi' ashaya k' din-tor leipausu?” “rai, hinek torvukh, i’m ri. Tonk'peh din-tor leipausu has kindly consented tor stariben tor du pa' nash tukh.” i hadn’t wuh faintest idea ra “nash tukh” vesh', tonk'peh i vesh' weht annoyed do interested. I hadn’t ya'akash jordan tor theris-masu svi' zek tor discuss mr. Jay gatsby. I vesh' sure wuh ya'akash would nam-tor vel utterly fantastic, heh na' wuh moment i vesh' sorry i’d ek'wak eku ash'ya fi-tor ish-veh overpopulated yartra. Au wouldn’t leralmin wuh'ashiv zhit. Ish-veh correctness grew fi' ish-veh u' etek betau wuh kahr. Etek be' dvun-tor kif roosevelt, wilat tra' vesh' wuh glimpse t' yon-kur-belted oceangoing ships, heh thresh-tor bi' wuh cobbled slum zehl-tor k' wuh gu'gelik, undeserted saloons t' wuh spoh-tor-gilt leh-nau-hundreds. Yi wuh ku-li t' vitush tu'ash si' fi' fi' vla t' etek, heh i had wuh glimpse t' mrs. Wilson straining na' wuh pi'hali-kel spol k' panting vitality u' etek went k'. K' fenders sak-tor spo' rala etek scattered ta'hal k'fai ulef astoria—goh ulef, na' u' etek kuvoran-tor among wuh pillars t' wuh ashenau i puzhu-tor wuh familiar “mashek-mashek-spat!” t' wuh motorcycle, heh wuh frantic policeman fau-tor alongside. “ek' gas'rak, hinek torvukh, ” puvutau gatsby. Etek slowed ne'. Taking wuh wan-kur nop s' ish-veh wallet, au pral-tor ish-veh fa' wuh sasu’s bezhun. “gas'rak du nam-tor, ” sep-wafikh wuh policeman, tipping ish-veh taik. “fai-tor du thurai wak, mr. Gatsby. Tobeg me!” “ra vesh' ik?” i inquired. “wuh bikuv t' oxford?” “i vesh' kup tor tor wuh commissioner wuh favour wuh'wak, heh au satau me wuh christmas nop kanok tevun.” abru' wuh lo'uk mesut, k' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel k'fai wuh girders tor wuh ek'kayik hanuvaya fi-tor wuh dvun-tor poiq'lid, k' wuh kahr rising abru mes' wuh pilash svi' wan-kur heaps heh slor-tukh vihk ek' torvau k' wuh istaya s' nonolfactory donku. Wuh kahr gla-tor s' wuh queensboro mesut nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh kahr gla-tor na' wuh wuh'rak wak, svi' its wuh'rak kwai ugaya t' ek' wuh mystery heh wuh vaksur svi' wuh panu. Wuh tevik sasu be' dvun-tor etek svi' wuh hearse heaped k' svai-tor, zahal-tor k' dahkuh carriages k' drawn blinds, heh k' weht cheerful carriages na' t'hylara. Wuh t'hylara glazhau si' na' etek k' wuh tragic bezhun heh pen upper bru-lar t' southeastern europe, heh i vesh' glad ik wuh glan t' gatsby’s splendid poiq'lid vesh' vinan-tor svi' ish-veh sombre holiday. U' etek tuhsau blackwell’s vikuvtra wuh limousine be' dvun-tor etek, driven k' wuh wan-kur chauffeur, svi' if hayal-tor rehkuh modish negroes, dahkuh bucks heh wuh ko-kan. I abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor aloud u' wuh vek t' ish-veh bezhun-kal padukau na' etek svi' haughty rivalry. “sovek-vel mokuhlek pavesh-tor i' ik etek’ve slid abru' nash mesut, ” i nahp; “sovek-vel na' ek' …” kauk gatsby kupi pavesh-tor, rik' sovek particular wonder. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ roaring aru. Svi' wuh muhl-fanned keh-leh-dahr yut cellar i ragel-tor gatsby na' khi-gad-yem. Blinking maf wuh ugel'es t' wuh yut s'udish, t'nash-veh bezhun picked ish-veh si' obscurely svi' wuh anteroom, talking tor wuh'ashiv sasu. “mr. Carraway, nash nam-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la mr. Wolfshiem.” wuh pi', pa'ash-nosed jew ashenau ish-veh suk patam heh fudau me k' dahkuh tok-ti tor'ovak t' isachya if luxuriated svi' either nostril. Po' wuh moment i discovered ish-veh tiny bezhun svi' wuh ulef-mu'khlup'es. “—ni i nem-tor veh glazhau na' ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor mr. Wolfshiem, shaking t'nash-veh el'ru earnestly, “heh ra tor du nah-tor i did?” “ra?” i inquired politely. Tonk'peh evidently au vesh' ri addressing me, na' au eku-tor t'nash-veh el'ru heh wein-tor gatsby k' ish-veh expressive han. “i handed wuh donku tor katspaugh heh i leralmin-tor: ‘ek' gas'rak, katspaugh, don’t vlitau ish-veh wuh qsu'lit till au ikap-tor ish-veh ru'lut.’ au ikap-tor ish-veh yi heh tra'.” gatsby nem-tor wuh kar t' tik t' etek heh dvun-tor fa'rak vi' wuh restaurant, whereupon mr. Wolfshiem vitem-tor wuh uzh zhit-bal au vesh' starting heh lapsed vi' wuh somnambulatory abstraction. “highballs?” ya'akash wuh patam waiter. “nash nam-tor wuh nice restaurant la', ” leralmin-tor mr. Wolfshiem, looking na' wuh presbyterian nymphs fi' wuh abru-tol. “tonk'peh i spo' mes' wuh yut weh-rom!” “ha, highballs, ” sep-wafikh gatsby, heh yi tor mr.
