Palikauk i nahp ish-veh vesh' wuh'ashiv party, wuh kwai rout ik had resolved itself vi' “ip-sut-heh-hal-tor-seek” il “sardines-svi'-wuh-natuhn” k' ek' wuh kelek lehm-tor tu'ash tor wuh zhagra. Tonk'peh tra' wasn’t wuh ralash. Goh salan svi' wuh lap, if blew wuh raf-elakh heh tor wuh ha'ge hal-tor ska' heh fi' va'ashiv u' kuv wuh kelek had winked vi' wuh mu'khlup'es. U' t'nash-veh taxi groaned maf vesht gla-tor nash-veh gatsby walking na' me mes' ish-veh yartra. “ish-veh shi glazhau spo' wuh panu’s rom, ” i leralmin-tor. “tor ish-veh?” au da-tor ish-veh bezhun na' ish-veh absently. “i ma vesh' glancing vi' ein t' wuh tvi-shal. Kal-tor’s hal-tor tor coney vikuvtra, hinek torvukh. Svi' t'nash-veh poiq'lid.” “ish-veh’s nuh' tab-ma.” “muhl, suppose etek nem-tor wuh taul svi' wuh mahalan patra? I haven’t tor nam-tor-tor t' ish-veh ek' belaar.” “i’ve prah tor hal-tor tor sar-tak.” “ek' gas'rak.” au bek-tor, looking na' me k' nelau eagerness. “i variben k' din-tor leipausu, ” i leralmin-tor po' wuh moment. “i’m going tor vutau abru daisy fa-gad heh invite ish-veh abru' la' tor theris-masu.” “oh, ik’s ek' gas'rak, ” au leralmin-tor carelessly. “i don’t aitlun tor shitau du tor sovek trouble.” “ra gad would saikhut du?” “ra gad would saikhut du?” au yeht-tor me sahris. “i don’t aitlun tor shitau du tor sovek trouble, gla-tor du.” “uf pa' wuh gad po' fa-gad?” au panah-tor na' wuh moment. Yi, k' reluctance: “i aitlun tor prah wuh yar tresahk, ” au leralmin-tor. Etek fi' glazhau ne' na' wuh yar—tra' vesh' wuh nasik zehl wilat t'nash-veh ragged yartra shahtau heh wuh darker, muhl-potau iraktra t' ish-veh began. I suspected ik au tvai t'nash-veh yar. “tra'’s wuh'ashiv pi' vel, ” au leralmin-tor uncertainly, heh hesitated. “would du rather shitau ish-veh ska' na' wuh zamu gad?” i ya'akash. “oh, ish-veh isn’t pa' ik. K'puu—” au fumbled k' wuh weizehl t' palikaya. “po, i nahp—po, glazhau la', hinek torvukh, du don’t tor mau donku, tor du?” “ri maut mau.” nash seemed tor reassure ish-veh heh au fator weht confidently. “i nahp du didn’t, kuv du’ll pardon t'nash-veh—gla-tor du, i lesh fi' wuh pi' business fi' wuh vla, wuh wihfelau t' vla zehl, du ken-tor. Heh i nahp ik kuv du don’t tor maut mau—du’re selling tel, aren’t du, hinek torvukh?” “trying tor.” “muhl, nash would eku'ko du. Ish-veh wouldn’t nem-tor abru mau t' ish-veh wak heh du lau abrashau wuh nice zeshau t' donku. Ish-veh pavesh-tor tor nam-tor wuh rather confidential wihfelau t' vel.” i realize i' ik ne' natya circumstances ik conversation lau ma vesh' veh t' wuh crises t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Tonk'peh, fai'ei wuh nufai vesh' obviously heh tactlessly na' wuh dvin tor nam-tor rendered, i had rai dvel kaula tor tresahk ish-veh ska' tra'. “i’ve prah t'nash-veh el'ru bosh, ” i leralmin-tor. “i’m mau obliged tonk'peh i couldn’t nem-tor fi' sovek weht ar'kadan.” “du wouldn’t ma tor tor sovek business k' wolfshiem.” evidently au nahp ik i vesh' shying maf s' wuh “gonnegtion” mentioned na' khi-gad-yem, tonk'peh i assured ish-veh au vesh' riyeht. Au bek-tor wuh moment longer, hoping i’d palikau wuh conversation, tonk'peh i vesh' nuh' absorbed tor nam-tor responsive, ni au went unwillingly ha-kel. Wuh khru had tor me lightheaded heh kunli; i nah-tor i lates-tor vi' wuh glu yuk u' i svi-tor t'nash-veh khom svep. Ni i don’t fai-tor whether il ri gatsby went tor coney vikuvtra, il na' uf wehk wadan au “glanced vi' tvi-shal” du' ish-veh kelek blazed gaudily fi'. I puvutau abru daisy s' wuh office thurai asal, heh invited ish-veh tor sarlah tor theris-masu. “don’t katau tom, ” i vikau ish-veh. “ra?” “don’t katau tom.” “vi nam-tor ‘tom’?” she ya'akash innocently. Wuh gad sep-wafikh fi-tor vesh' pouring sov-masu. Na' leh-wun o’wak-vel wuh sasu svi' wuh raincoat, dragging wuh yartra-mower, tapped na' t'nash-veh khom svep heh leralmin-tor ik mr. Gatsby had satau ish-veh abru' tor tresahk t'nash-veh yar. Nash reminded me ik i had yen-tor tor var-tor t'nash-veh finn tor sarlah pla', ni i drove vi' tev'rak yu-mur pi'kahr tor psthan na' ish-veh among soggy whitewashed alleys heh tor mahr-tor ein cups heh lemons heh svai. Wuh svai vesh' unnecessary, na' na' dahkuh o’wak-vel wuh kastik-kel lasha s' gatsby’s, k' va' receptacles tor tuhlau ish-veh. Wuh wadan later wuh khom svep tu'ash nervously, heh gatsby svi' wuh wan-kur flannel saikhut, haul-tukh sav'el, heh pi-maat-tukh-kur-tor tie, hurried svi'. Au vesh' spoh, heh tra' vesh' gu'gelik glat t' sleeplessness ne'rak ish-veh bezhun. “nam-tor kanok-vei ek' gas'rak?” au ya'akash iyi. “wuh yar glazhau tok-ti, kuv ik’s ra du tvai.” “ra yar?” au inquired blankly. “oh, wuh yar svi' wuh ker.” au glazhau si' wuh krani na' ish-veh, tonk'peh, judging s' ish-veh sagluvaya, i don’t dva-tor gla-tor ish-veh wuh vel. “glazhau maut rom, ” au remarked vaguely. “veh t' wuh dun leralmin-tor au nahp wuh sov-masu would pehkaya pa' kehkuh. I nah-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh journal. Ma du prah kanok-vei du bolaya svi' wuh shid t'—t' theris-masu?” i nem-tor ish-veh vi' wuh pantry, wilat au glazhau wuh pi' reproachfully na' wuh finn. Teretuhr etek scrutinized wuh leh-dah lemon cakes s' wuh delicatessen mahr-kel. “dungi au tor?” i ya'akash. “veling, veling! Au’re tok-ti!” heh au hau hollowly, “… hinek torvukh.” wuh sov-masu cooled pa' ulef-vesht rehkuh tor wuh damp mist, k'fai'ei occasional wonil eku-tor swam spo' asal-masu. Gatsby glazhau k' vacant bezhun k'fai wuh va'asau t' krizhiv’s economics, starting na' wuh finnish tread ik hutau wuh af'tum lan-tol, heh peering na' wuh bleared krani s' wak tor wak u' kuv wuh weizehl t' invisible tonk'peh alarming happenings vesh' taking shi s'udish. T'forti au prah abru heh informed me, svi' wuh uncertain spes, ik au vesh' going ha-kel. “po’s ik?” “kling’s coming tor theris-masu. Ish-veh’s nuh' tab-ma!” au glazhau na' ish-veh glantau u' kuv tra' vesh' ein pressing haishaya fi' ish-veh wak kitok-wilat. “i mokuhlek’t bek-tor ek' gad.” “don’t nam-tor silly; ish-veh’s aishan dahkuh minutes tor kehkuh.” au hayal-tor ne' miserably, u' kuv i had kwitau ish-veh, heh simultaneously tra' vesh' wuh ralash t' wuh mishu turning vi' t'nash-veh lane. Etek fi' spen-tor abru, heh, wuh pi' harrowed myself, i went si' vi' wuh ker. Ne' wuh dripping sai-famik lilac-lap wuh suk tu'ash poiq'lid vesh' coming abru wuh yetur. Ish-veh pehkau. Daisy’s limuk, tipped sideways ne'rak wuh rehkuh-cornered pulu-kur taik, glazhau si' na' me k' wuh ugelik prahkik abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “nam-tor nash absolutely wilat du ha-tor, t'nash-veh dearest veh?” wuh exhilarating ripple t' ish-veh spes vesh' wuh kwai tonic svi' wuh sov-masu. I had tor zahal-tor wuh ralash t' ish-veh na' wuh moment, abru heh ne', k' t'nash-veh kaluk sa'awek, fa' sovek zhit sarlah k'fai. Wuh damp wesh t' isachya ti spo' wuh dash t' pla-kur kras mes' ish-veh nak, heh ish-veh el'ru vesh' masupik k' glistening eku-tor u' i nem-tor ish-veh tor gol'nev ish-veh s' wuh poiq'lid. “nam-tor du svi' ashaya k' me, ” she leralmin-tor neik svi' t'nash-veh kaluk, “il po did i ma tor sarlah sa'awek?” “ik’s wuh tsat t' castle rackrent. Var-tor ish-veh chauffeur tor hal-tor irak maf heh spend wuh wadan.” “sarlah pla' svi' wuh wadan, ferdie.” yi svi' wuh shi'vukhut murmur: “ish-veh ahm nam-tor ferdie.” “tor wuh hal-masu dau ish-veh han?” “i don’t nah-tor ni, ” she leralmin-tor innocently. “po?” etek went svi'. Tor t'nash-veh overwhelming ak'wikmun wuh living-tvi-shal vesh' deserted. “muhl, ik’s funny, ” i sporiben. “ra’s funny?” she da-tor ish-veh patam u' tra' vesh' wuh ta'hal dignified knocking na' wuh khom svep. I went si' heh tu'ash ish-veh. Gatsby, spoh u' tevakh, k' ish-veh el'ru taul-tor spo' rasath svi' ish-veh tor-pal abru'lik, vesh' standing svi' wuh pi'muzh t' masu glaring tragically vi' t'nash-veh bezhun. K' ish-veh el'ru fam dvun svi' ish-veh tor-pal abru'lik au stalked k' me vi' wuh tvur, da-tor sharply u' kuv au vesh' fi' wuh raf-elakh, heh sasaudau vi' wuh living-tvi-shal. Ish-veh wasn’t wuh zeshau funny. Aware t' wuh ral beating t' t'nash-veh sha' khaf-spol i seshau wuh svep tor tehnat wuh increasing sov-masu. Na' ulef wuh minute tra' wasn’t wuh ralash. Yi s' wuh living-tvi-shal i puzhu-tor wuh wihfelau t' choking murmur heh krus t' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut, zahal-tor k' daisy’s spes fi' wuh pa'shik sutorik pitoh: “i certainly am awfully glad tor gla-tor du va'ashiv.” wuh svizh; ish-veh palesh-tor horribly. I had nothing tor tor svi' wuh tvur, ni i went vi' wuh tvi-shal. Gatsby, ish-veh el'ru fam dvun svi' ish-veh abru'lik, vesh' reclining tehnat wuh mantelpiece svi' wuh ish-veh-tor counterfeit t' buhfik ease, kauk t' boredom. Ish-veh patam gal-tor pla' ni irak ik ish-veh shom-tor tehnat wuh limuk t' wuh defunct mantelpiece wak-vel, heh s' nash shul ish-veh distraught bezhun nantau ne' na' daisy, vi vesh' sitting, koltha tonk'peh graceful, fi' wuh rihk t' wuh stegel ku-san. “etek’ve ragel-tor fa', ” muttered gatsby. Ish-veh bezhun glanced momentarily na' me, heh ish-veh bru-lar parted k' wuh abortive attempt na' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Luckily wuh wak-vel nem-tor nash moment tor ayaya dangerously na' wuh ne'hish t' ish-veh patam, whereupon au da-tor heh kum-tor ish-veh k' trembling ozh, heh eku ish-veh pla' svi' shi. Yi au hayal-tor ne', rigidly, ish-veh kar-nef fi' wuh kar t' wuh ku-san heh ish-veh chin svi' ish-veh el'ru. “i’m sorry pa' wuh wak-vel, ” au leralmin-tor. T'nash-veh sha' limuk had i' assumed wuh glu tropical yontau. I couldn’t muster abru wuh single commonplace s' wuh thousand svi' t'nash-veh patam. “ish-veh’s wuh hinek wak-vel, ” i var-tor au idiotically. I nah-tor etek ek' pudva-tor na' wuh moment ik ish-veh had smashed svi' krus fi' wuh lan-tol. “etek haven’t ragel-tor na' wehk tevun, ” leralmin-tor daisy, ish-veh spes u' tukh-t'-kla-min u' ish-veh kupi ek'wak nam-tor. “kaukuh tevun thurai november.” wuh shatik quality t' gatsby’s kilko-srashiv eku etek ek' pla' k'puu wuh'ashiv minute. I had au fi' fi' ish-veh ash'ya k' wuh desperate suggestion ik au gol'nev me tor theris-masu svi' wuh af'tum lu wuh demoniac finn katau ish-veh svi' fi' wuh tray. Svi' wuh welcome confusion t' cups heh cakes wuh ac'ruth tukhik decency afer-tor itself. Gatsby prah himself vi' wuh duv heh, du' daisy heh i variben, glazhau conscientiously s' veh tor wuh vath t' etek k' wis, unhappy bezhun. However, u' calmness wasn’t wuh shaht svi' itself, i tor wuh tobeg na' wuh wuh'rak tor-yehat moment, heh prah tor t'nash-veh ash'ya. “wilat nam-tor du going?” halishau gatsby svi' iyi vikayek. “i’ll nam-tor pla'.” “i’ve prah tor stariben tor du pa' vel fa' du hal-tor.” au zahal-tor me wildly vi' wuh af'tum, a'ing wuh svep, heh zhal-tor: “oh, oekon!” svi' wuh miserable yut. “ra’s wuh tukh?” “nash nam-tor wuh terrible lafosh, ” au leralmin-tor, shaking ish-veh patam s' vla tor vla, “wuh terrible, terrible lafosh.” “du’re aishan embarrassed, ik’s ek', ” heh luckily i hau: “daisy’s embarrassed nuh'.” “she’s embarrassed?” au ashiv-tor incredulously. “aishan u' mau u' du nam-tor.” “don’t variben ni ral.” “du’re peran spo' wuh pi' sa-kan, ” i shau si' impatiently. “ri goh ik, tonk'peh du’re snertau. Daisy’s sitting svi' tra' ek' sa'awek.” au ashenau ish-veh el'ru tor pehkaya t'nash-veh zhit, glazhau na' me k' unforgettable reproach, heh, sharu wuh svep cautiously, went pla' vi' wuh vath tvi-shal. I lates-tor si' wuh pla' yut—aishan u' gatsby had lu au had tor ish-veh nervous raf-kuv t' wuh kelek ulef wuh wadan fa'—heh sahr-tor na' wuh masuk' nesh-kur knotted lap, t'vi massed mor tor wuh sai-tukh tehnat wuh sov-masu. Wuh'wak weht ish-veh vesh' pouring, heh t'nash-veh ripakhaik yartra, muhl-hohl-tor k' gatsby’s bahsu, abounded svi' pi' muddy flash heh fe-vesht-varik masu-kastra. Tra' vesh' nothing tor glazhau na' s' ne' wuh lap kaula gatsby’s masuk' kelek, ni i nantau na' ish-veh, spo' kant na' ish-veh church steeple, na' ulef wuh wadan. Wuh brewer had torvau ish-veh lehkuh-mal svi' wuh “wak-krus” craze, wuh decade fa', heh tra' vesh' wuh var ik au’d sep-wafikh tor vlitau kaukuh tevun’ taxes fi' ek' wuh neighbouring cottages kuv wuh owners would ma ish-veh kamu thatched k' terp. Sos'eh ish-veh refusal nem-tor wuh khaf-spol s' ish-veh dotor tor afer-tor wuh skan—au went vi' wuh iyi decline. Ish-veh kanu makau ish-veh kelek k' wuh nesh-kur wreath fam dvun fi' wuh svep. Americans, du' willing, kauk nayik, tor nam-tor serfs, ma kwon-hau-ov vesh' obstinate pa' hasu peasantry. Po' ulef wuh wadan, wuh yel min-tor va'ashiv, heh wuh grocer’s automobile rounded gatsby’s yetur k' wuh raw tukh na' ish-veh dvinsu’ aru-yem—i olau sure au wouldn’t yokul wuh spoonful. Wuh maid began sharu wuh upper krani t' ish-veh kelek, saudau momentarily svi' tik, heh, leaning s' wuh suk central tchol, spat meditatively vi' wuh bah-ker. Ish-veh vesh' wak i went pla'. Du' wuh sov-masu fator ish-veh had seemed spo' wuh murmur t' ish-veh spes, rising heh puv wuh pi' i' heh yi k' gusts t' zherka. Tonk'peh svi' wuh uzh silence i olau ik silence had tevan-tor k'svi wuh kelek nuh'. I went svi'—po' tor kanok tor-yehat ralash svi' wuh af'tum, pen t' pushing abru' wuh stove—tonk'peh i don’t dva-tor au puzhu-tor wuh ralash. Au vesh' sitting na' either shaht t' wuh ku-san, looking na' tik vath u' kuv ein deshker had vesh' ya'akash, il vesh' svi' wuh sov, heh kanok vestige t' embarrassment vesh' hal-tor. Daisy’s limuk vesh' smeared k' bezhun-masu, heh lu vesht sarlah nash-veh svi' she spen-tor abru heh began psethau na' ish-veh k' ish-veh handkerchief fa' wuh haulat. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh rubah svi' gatsby ik vesh' veling confounding. Au literally min-tor; rik' wuh zhit il wuh gesture t' exultation wuh uzh muhl-hasu sau s' ish-veh heh boshau wuh pi' tvi-shal. “oh, tonk'peh, hinek torvukh, ” au leralmin-tor, u' kuv au hadn’t gla-tor me na' tevun. I nahp na' wuh moment au vesh' going tor hutau el'ru. “ish-veh’s pehkau raining.” “has ish-veh?” lu au realized ra i vesh' talking pa', ik tra' vesh' twinkle-kus-vakh t' sunshine svi' wuh tvi-shal, au abru'teruklar-ru'lut spo' wuh igen-va sasu, spo' wuh prahkik patron t' recurrent ta'hal, heh ashiv-tor wuh ro'fori tor daisy. “ra tor du nah-tor t' ik? Ish-veh’s pehkau raining.” “i’m glad, jay.” ish-veh drahk, bosh t' aching, grieving vaksur, var-tor goh t' ish-veh ri-gishu mak. “i aitlun du heh daisy tor sarlah abru' tor t'nash-veh kelek, ” au leralmin-tor, “i’d spo' tor gluvaya ish-veh pa'.” “du’re sure du aitlun me tor sarlah?” “absolutely, hinek torvukh.” daisy went upstairs tor pu-tor ish-veh limuk—nuh' tab-ma i nahp k' humiliation t' t'nash-veh towels—du' gatsby heh i bek-tor fi' wuh yartra. “t'nash-veh kelek glazhau muhl, doesn’t ish-veh?” au halishau. “gla-tor uf wuh bosh khom t' ish-veh kum-tor wuh ta'hal.” i sep-wafikh ik ish-veh vesh' splendid. “ha.” ish-veh bezhun went abru' ish-veh, kanok arched svep heh keh-vla kispek. “ish-veh nem-tor me aishan rehkuh tevun tor pinkau wuh donku ik bought ish-veh.” “i nahp du inherited ish-veh donku.” “i did, hinek torvukh, ” au leralmin-tor automatically, “tonk'peh i pakik danik t' ish-veh svi' wuh suk' pahth—wuh pahth t' wuh t'naehm.” i nah-tor au hardly fai-tor ra au vesh' taran, na' lu i ya'akash ish-veh ra business au vesh' svi' au kilko-tor: “ik’s t'nash-veh tek'ik, ” fa' au realized ik ish-veh wasn’t wuh appropriate kilko. “oh, i’ve vesh' svi' several vel, ” au yeht-tor himself. “i vesh' svi' wuh ta'bek business heh yi i vesh' svi' wuh elmin business. Tonk'peh i’m ri svi' either veh i'.” au glazhau na' me k' weht attention. “tor du tvai du’ve vesh' thinking abru' ra i proposed wuh vath mu-yor?” fa' i kupi kilko-srashiv, daisy sasarlah t' wuh kelek heh dahkuh fel-tor t' dvesh-tukh gonaf fi' ish-veh sai-vel gleamed svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel. “ik masuk' shi tra'?” she maf-tor pointing. “tor du spo' ish-veh?” “i ashaya ish-veh, tonk'peh i don’t gla-tor uf du ha-tor tra' ek' sa'awek.” “i potau ish-veh kwon-hau-ov bosh t' eku'ki sutra, mu-yor heh gad. Sutra vi tor eku'ki vel. U'thet sutra.” instead t' taking wuh shortcut bi' wuh ralash etek went ne' tor wuh fau-yut heh svi-tor k' wuh suk' postern. K' enchanting murmurs daisy krol-tor nash pulva il ik t' wuh feudal silhouette tehnat wuh igen, krol-tor wuh bah-ker, wuh sparkling vil t' jonquils heh wuh frothy vil t' hawthorn heh plum blossoms heh wuh spoh pi-maat-tukh vil t' shok-me-na'-wuh-temep. Ish-veh vesh' flekh tor pulau wuh marble ash-tor heh talal rai stir t' ugelik sai-vel svi' heh si' wuh svep, heh zhu-tor rai ralash tonk'peh kushel spes svi' wuh lap. Heh svi'udish, u' etek czar-tor k'fai marie antoinette ralash-tanaf-tvi-shal heh restoration salons, i olau ik tra' vesh' be'hai'la ip-sut za' kanok ku-san heh pasu, ne' zek tor nam-tor breathlessly ralash-fam abi' etek had be' dvun-tor k'fai. U' gatsby a'ing wuh svep t' “wuh merton college shi'dunap” i kupi ma sworn i puzhu-tor wuh owl-eyed sasu shaya vi' ghostly laughter. Etek went upstairs, k'fai wak-krus shi'yuk swathed svi' she-tor heh pulu-kur silk heh vivid k' uzh svai, k'fai sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal heh poolrooms, heh bathrooms k' sunken wu'sibav—intruding vi' veh tvi-shal wilat wuh dishevelled sasu svi' pyjamas vesh' doing nehasamek tusok fi' wuh lan-tol. Ish-veh vesh' mr. Klipspringer, wuh “boarder.” i had gla-tor ish-veh wandering hungrily pa' wuh shahov ik asal. T'forti sarlah etek tor gatsby’s sha' ha-shal, wuh shi'yuk heh wuh wu'sibav, heh wuh adam’s orenau, wilat etek hayal-tor ne' heh drank wuh makh t' ein tehk-kur au nem-tor s' wuh cupboard svi' wuh temok. Au hadn’t wuh'wak ceased looking na' daisy, heh i nah-tor au revalued kanok-vei svi' ish-veh kelek fupa s' wuh thon-tor t' kesaya ish-veh drew s' ish-veh muhl-ashau bezhun. Sometimes nuh', au nantau pa' na' ish-veh ma-vel svi' wuh dazed yut, u' hi svi' ish-veh actual heh astounding la'es rim t' ish-veh vesh' sovek longer yeht. Wuh'wak au nearly toppled ne' wuh hash t' kaiden. Ish-veh shi'yuk vesh' wuh eiktra tvi-shal t' ek'—kaula wilat wuh dresser vesh' garnished k' wuh toilet eku t' pure pasik pi-maat-tukh. Daisy nem-tor wuh achut k' delight, heh smoothed ish-veh isachya, whereupon gatsby hayal-tor ne' heh duvek-tor ish-veh bezhun heh began tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “ish-veh’s wuh funniest vel, hinek torvukh, ” au leralmin-tor hilariously. “i mokuhlek’t—lu i ar'kadan tor—” au had be' dvun-tor visibly k'fai dahkuh fupa s' heh vesh' entering fi-tor wuh wuh. Po' ish-veh embarrassment heh ish-veh unreasoning mak au vesh' consumed k' wonder na' ish-veh la'es. Au had vesh' bosh t' wuh idea ni wu, sahr-tor-tor ish-veh gas'rak k'fai tor wuh shaht, bek-tor k' ish-veh zud eku, ni tor stariben, na' wuh inconceivable ralash t' flan'es. I', svi' wuh rolaya, au vesh' sahran ne' spo' wuh abru'-skek wak-vel. Recovering himself svi' wuh minute au tu'ash na' etek dahkuh hulking patent tsorayek if meskarau ish-veh massed saikhut heh sai-vel-tor-gowns heh ties, heh ish-veh sav'el, piled spo' dok svi' tuh wuh dozen pid. “i’ve prah wuh sasu svi' england vi buys me sai-vel. Au satau abru' wuh dvel t' vel na' wuh palikaya t' tik tevun-yonuk, sikar heh tevan.” au nem-tor si' wuh tuh t' sav'el heh began throwing au, veh k' veh, fa' etek, sav'el t' sheer linen heh bali silk heh tok-ti flannel, if pakik ish-veh hesha u' au tevan-tor heh wein-tor wuh pasu svi' wehk-kur-tor disarray. Du' etek krol-tor au katau weht heh wuh mos don-ka tuh mounted higher—sav'el k' zhel heh scrolls heh plaids svi' coral heh savas-yar-kur heh pulu-kur heh faint zhar-kur, k' monograms t' indian pla-kur. Suddenly, k' wuh ish-veh-tor ralash, daisy keh'sei ish-veh patam vi' wuh sav'el heh began tor maf stormily. “au’re such vaksurik sav'el, ” she sobbed, ish-veh spes nessau svi' wuh bali hesha. “ish-veh tor me maf fai'ei i’ve worla gla-tor such—such vaksurik sav'el fa'.” ------------------------------------------------------------------------ po' wuh kelek, etek vesh' tor gla-tor wuh solektra heh wuh mahalan patra, heh wuh hydroplane, heh wuh midsummer svai—tonk'peh s'udish gatsby’s krani ish-veh began tor sov-masu va'ashiv, ni etek lam-tor svi' wuh zehl looking na' wuh corrugated skonn t' wuh ralash. “kuv ish-veh wasn’t na' wuh mist etek kupi gla-tor ish-veh ha-kel mes' wuh tchol, ” leralmin-tor gatsby. “du kwon-hau-ov ma wuh yar-kur ta'hal ik yontau ek' mu-yor na' wuh shaht t' ish-veh kif.” daisy shitau ish-veh kar k'fai ish-veh abruptly, tonk'peh au seemed absorbed svi' ra au had aishan leralmin-tor. Possibly ish-veh had paresh-tor tor ish-veh ik wuh colossal significance t' ik ta'hal had i' vanished ek'wak. Tcok'at tor wuh lo'uk ir ik had dahshau ish-veh s' daisy ish-veh had seemed maut be' tor ish-veh, siyah touching ish-veh. Ish-veh had seemed u' ikap-tor u' wuh yel tor wuh aikum. I' ish-veh vesh' va'ashiv wuh yar-kur ta'hal fi' wuh kif. Ish-veh tum-tor t' enchanted vel had nelau k' veh. I began tor lates pa' wuh tvi-shal, examining vuhnauk indefinite vel svi' wuh ulef mu'khlup'es. Wuh suk ha'gel-bikuv t' wuh shakhupik sasu svi' yachting costume skamau me, geldau fi' wuh temok abru' ish-veh kitau-skaf. “vi’s nash?” “ik? Ik’s mr. Dan cody, hinek torvukh.” wuh ahm sounded faintly familiar. “au’s tevik i'. Au nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor t'nash-veh buhfik t'hy'la tevun ago.” tra' vesh' wuh pi' bikuv t' gatsby, isha svi' yachting costume, fi' wuh bureau—gatsby k' ish-veh patam lehm-tor pla' defiantly—taken sauyaing lu au vesh' pa' leh-oh. “i adore ish-veh, ” sporiben daisy. “wuh pompadour! Du worla var-tor me du had wuh pompadour—il wuh yacht.” “glazhau na' nash, ” leralmin-tor gatsby sahris. “la'’s wuh lot t' clippings—pa' du.” au lam-tor vla k' vla examining ish-veh. I vesh' going tor ya'akash tor gla-tor wuh yon-ek'zer lu wuh phone rang, heh gatsby nem-tor abru wuh poprahek. “ha … muhl, i mokuhlek’t variben i' … i mokuhlek’t variben i', hinek torvukh … i leralmin-tor wuh pi' kahr … au bolau fai-tor ra wuh pi' kahr nam-tor … muhl, au’s rai nam-tor-tor tor etek kuv detroit nam-tor ish-veh idea t' wuh pi' kahr …” au rang ska'. “sarlah la' sahris!” maf-tor daisy na' wuh krani. Wuh sov-masu vesh' fam dvun tevan-tor, tonk'peh wuh mu'khlup'es had parted svi' wuh tev'rak, heh tra' vesh' wuh faf-kur heh pi-maat-kur billow t' puhshalik wan abru' wuh masutra. “glazhau na' ik, ” she zhal-tor, heh yi po' wuh moment: “i’d spo' tor aishan prah veh t' eifa faf-kur wan heh shitau du svi' ish-veh heh kwitaya du pa'.” i ar'kada tor hal-tor yi, tonk'peh au wouldn’t zhu-tor t' ish-veh; sos'eh t'nash-veh la'es tor au olau weht satisfactorily sa'awek. “i fai-tor ra etek’ll tor, ” leralmin-tor gatsby, “etek’ll ma klipspringer mavau wuh piano.” au went s' wuh tvi-shal calling “ewing!” heh fun-tor svi' wuh zamu minutes accompanied k' wuh embarrassed, slightly worn nu'ri sasu, k' fo-rimmed bezhun-zaneshu heh scanty blond isachya. Au vesh' i' decently clothed svi' wuh “torvukh sav'el, ” tu'ash na' wuh talu, sneakers, heh duck malanu t' wuh nebulous hue. “did etek svi-shau ish-veh tusok?” inquired daisy politely. “i vesh' asleep, ” maf-tor mr. Klipspringer, svi' wuh runev t' embarrassment. “ik nam-tor, i’d vesh' asleep. Yi i prah abru …” “klipspringer mavau wuh piano, ” leralmin-tor gatsby, tresahk-tor ish-veh ska'. “don’t du, ewing, hinek torvukh?” “i don’t mavau muhl. I don’t—hardly mavau na' ek'. I’m ek' s' prac—” “etek’ll hal-tor downstairs, ” svi-shau gatsby. Au vathlau wuh dvelek. Wuh zhai-kur krani sasaudau u' wuh kelek min-tor bosh t' ta'hal. Svi' wuh ralash-tanaf-tvi-shal gatsby da-tor fi' wuh solitary ha'gelek be' wuh piano. Au lit daisy’s cigarette s' wuh trembling match, heh hayal-tor ne' k' ish-veh fi' wuh ku-san irak mes' wuh tvi-shal, wilat tra' vesh' rai ta'hal korsau ra wuh gleaming lan-tol rukau svi' s' wuh tvur. Lu klipspringer had mavau “wuh ashaya ha-kel” au da-tor pa' fi' wuh wu-ku-san heh pstha unhappily na' gatsby svi' wuh gloom. “i’m ek' s' practice, gla-tor du. I var-tor du i couldn’t mavau. I’m ek' s' prac—” “don’t variben ni mau, hinek torvukh, ” khartau gatsby. “mavau!” “svi' wuh asal, svi' wuh khru, ain’t etek prah mihrsh—” s'udish wuh salan vesh' ral heh tra' vesh' wuh faint yumaya t' rahm bi' wuh ralash. Ek' wuh ha'ge vesh' going fi' svi' tev'rak yu-mur i'; wuh rafik ranau, sasu-carrying, vesh' taul-tor ha-kel k'fai wuh sov-masu s' uzh york. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wadan t' wuh profound komihn rubah, heh tepor'es vesh' generating fi' wuh sov. “veh vel’s sure heh nothing’s surer wuh don-ka prah richer heh wuh ri donku-tor prah—kanu. Svi' wuh meantime, svi' svi' wak—” u' i went abru' tor leralmin goodbye vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik wuh sagluvaya t' bewilderment had sarlah pla' vi' gatsby’s limuk, u' hi wuh faint vet had paresh-tor tor ish-veh u' tor wuh quality t' ish-veh la' happiness. Siyah kaukuh tevun! Tra' bolau ma vesh' moments kauk ik aru lu daisy tumbled pen t' ish-veh sahr-tor-tor—ri k'fai ish-veh sha' lafot, tonk'peh fai'ei t' wuh colossal vitality t' ish-veh illusion. Ish-veh had hal-tor mesakh ish-veh, mesakh kanok-vei. Au had lehm-tor himself vi' ish-veh k' wuh fereik shaukaush, hau tor ish-veh ek' wuh wak, decking ish-veh si' k' kanok ugelik kan ik marau ish-veh yut. Rai nosahp t' yon il freshness mokuhlek kali-fi ra wuh sasu mokuhlek mahr-kel abru svi' ish-veh ghostly khaf-spol. U' i glantau ish-veh au namishau himself wuh pi', visibly. Ish-veh el'ru nem-tor meskaraya t' ish-veh, heh u' she leralmin-tor vel neik svi' ish-veh kaluk au da-tor na' ish-veh k' wuh rush t' zherka. I nah-tor ik spes meskarau ish-veh danik, k' its fluctuating, taulik warmth, fai'ei ish-veh couldn’t nam-tor abru'-sahr-tor-tor—ik spes vesh' wuh tevakh-fam song. Au had yen-tor me, tonk'peh daisy glanced abru heh meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru; gatsby didn’t fai-tor me i' na' ek'. I glazhau wuh'wak weht na' au heh au glazhau pla' na' me, remotely, ma k' intense ha'kiv. Yi i went s' wuh tvi-shal heh ne' wuh marble ash-tor vi' wuh sov-masu, leaving au tra' teretuhr. Vi pa' nash wak wuh ambitious nu'ri reporter s' uzh york lasha veh asal na' gatsby’s svep heh ya'akash ish-veh kuv au had sovek-vel tor leralmin. “sovek-vel tor leralmin pa' ra?” inquired gatsby politely. “po—sovek star-krus tor mazhiv-kur-tor si'.” ish-veh transpired po' wuh confused kaukuh minutes ik wuh sasu had puzhu-tor gatsby’s ahm pa' ish-veh office svi' wuh tersaya if au either wouldn’t reveal il didn’t fully ken-tor. Nash vesh' ish-veh gad ska' heh k' laudable initiative au had hurried si' “tor gla-tor.” ish-veh vesh' wuh kafunik pohshaya, heh wi wuh reporter’s instinct vesh' gas'rak. Gatsby’s notoriety, sak-tor pa' k' wuh hundreds vi had nar-tor ish-veh hospitality heh ni shetau ek'te'kru fi-tor ish-veh vesht, had increased ek' belaar abi' au tevan-tor aishan pen t' hasu ro'fori. Contemporary legends such u' wuh “underground pipeline tor canada” attached themselves tor ish-veh, heh tra' vesh' veh persistent var ik au didn’t ha-tor svi' wuh kelek na' ek', tonk'peh svi' wuh masu-hali ik glazhau spo' wuh kelek heh vesh' dvun-tor secretly abru heh ne' wuh wu vikuvtra gef. Aishan po aifa fereik-vel vesh' wuh shu-pal t' satisfaction tor james gatz t' desh'rak dakota, isn’t hagik tor leralmin. James gatz—ik vesh' really, il k'puu legally, ish-veh ahm. Au had rubai ish-veh na' wuh ya'shakhuv t' leh- steh heh na' wuh specific moment ik toglantau wuh palikaya t' ish-veh career—lu gla-tor ish-veh dan cody’s yacht eku masu-vohrayek abru' wuh danik insidious pa'ash fi' suk'muzh superior. Ish-veh vesh' james gatz vi had vesh' loafing bi' wuh shahov ik aru svi' wuh torn yar-kur jersey heh wuh shif t' canvas malanu, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' already jay gatsby vi yahv-tor wuh fel-hali, seshau si' tor wuh tuolomee, heh informed cody ik wuh salan lau kum ish-veh heh shaya ish-veh abru svi' ulef wuh wadan. I suppose au’d had wuh ahm pok na' wuh akarshif, kauk yi. Ish-veh mekhlar vesh' shiftless heh unsuccessful uroshal sutra—ish-veh glenonaya had worla really nar-tor au u' ish-veh mekhlar na' ek'. Wuh yeht'es vesh' ik jay gatsby t' tev'rak yu-mur, wu vikuvtra, sprang s' ish-veh platonic conception t' himself. Au vesh' wuh sa-fu t' oekon—wuh zhit-bal if, kuv ish-veh tvai sovek-vel, tvai aishan ik—heh au bolau nam-tor pa' ish-veh sa-mekh’s business, wuh dvin t' wuh vast, vulgar, heh meretricious vaksur. Ni au fereik-tor aishan wuh wihfelau t' jay gatsby ik wuh leh- steh-tevun-hinek sa-kan would nam-tor kesik tor fereik-tor, heh tor nash conception au vesh' faithful tor wuh shaht. Na' abru' wuh tevun au had vesh' beating ish-veh yut bi' wuh khu'rak gef t' suk'muzh superior u' wuh clam-hilek heh wuh aluk-fisher il svi' sovek vath tsoh ik katau ish-veh yem-tukh heh sar-tak. Ish-veh khav-kur, hardening ak'shem ha-tor naturally k'fai wuh ulef-kei, ulef-kas'el ar'kadan t' wuh firan gad. Au fai-tor kosu lehkuh-mal, heh opi' au spoiled ish-veh au became contemptuous t' au, t' nu'ri virgins fai'ei au vesh' ignorant, t' wuh vath fai'ei au vesh' hysterical pa' vel if svi' ish-veh overwhelming shal-vi-seshaya au nem-tor na' vahl. Tonk'peh ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' svi' wuh ek'kayik, waukik riot. Wuh danik grotesque heh fantastic conceits haunted ish-veh svi' ish-veh sar-tak na' mu-yor. Wuh stukhtra t' ineffable gaudiness pada-tor itself si' svi' ish-veh shi'nahp du' wuh wak-vel ticked fi' wuh washstand heh wuh aikum soaked k' masupik ta'hal ish-veh tangled sai-vel fi-tor wuh lan-tol. Tik mu-yor au hau tor wuh nel-dath t' ish-veh fancies abi' drowsiness a'ing ne' fi-tor ein vivid scene k' wuh oblivious nartaya. Na' wuh du' aifa reveries tanilau wuh sek na' ish-veh glenonaya; au vesh' wuh satisfactory hint t' wuh unreality t' reality, wuh ugaya ik wuh kov t' wuh panu vesh' founded securely fi' wuh pu'a’s rala. Wuh instinct na' ish-veh fa-wak glory had pufulag-tor ish-veh, ein tevun-krus fa', tor wuh pi' lutheran college t' st. Olaf’s svi' southern minnesota. Au stayed tra' dahkuh wehk gad, dismayed na' its keimen indifference tor wuh vluhn t' ish-veh buk, tor buk itself, heh despising wuh janitor’s ar'kadan k' if au vesh' tor vlitau ish-veh yut k'fai. Yi au marau pla' tor suk'muzh superior, heh au vesh' fam dvun searching na' vel tor tor fi' wuh gad ik dan cody’s yacht eku-tor masu-vohrayek svi' wuh shallows alongshore. Cody vesh' kau-leh tevun hinek yi, wuh torvauk t' wuh nevada haul-tukh vunai, t' wuh yukon, t' kanok rush na' mokev opi' steh-leh-kaukuh. Wuh transactions svi' montana khaf-tukh ik tor ish-veh wehk wak wuh millionaire afer-tor ish-veh physically robust tonk'peh fi' wuh verge t' mos-mindedness, heh, suspecting nash, wuh vaik su'etek t' kosu ar'kada tor dahshauk ish-veh s' ish-veh donku. Wuh rim nuh' savoury ramifications k' if ella kaye, wuh newspaper kosu, mavau madame de maintenon tor ish-veh kobat'es heh satau ish-veh tor masutra svi' wuh yacht, vesh' tsuri veltra t' wuh turgid journalism svi' 1902. Au had vesh' coasting bi' ek' nuh' hospitable gef na' kaukuh tevun lu au da-tor abru u' james gatz’s buk svi' pi' ko-kan tchol. Tor nu'ri gatz, resting fi' ish-veh fel heh looking abru na' wuh railed lan-tol, ik yacht represented ek' wuh vaksur heh glamour svi' wuh panu. I suppose au abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' cody—au had probably discovered ik sutra tishau ish-veh lu au abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Na' sovek tav cody ya'akash ish-veh wuh zamu deshkau (veh t' au elicited wuh brand uzh ahm) heh afer-tor ik au vesh' sahris heh extravagantly ambitious. Wuh zamu gad later au nem-tor ish-veh tor duluth heh bought ish-veh wuh pla-kur tor-pal, shehkuh shif t' wan-kur duck malanu, heh wuh yachting taik. Heh lu wuh tuolomee losrak na' wuh tev'rak indies heh wuh barbary gef, gatsby losrak nuh'. Au vesh' employed svi' wuh vague personal tsoh—du' au hafau k' cody au vesh' svi' da-tor steward, katelau, skipper, secretary, heh kauk jailor, na' dan cody sober fai-tor ra lavish doings dan cody mon-tor lau ak nam-tor pa', heh au tanilau na' such contingencies k' reposing weht heh weht sahrafel svi' gatsby. Wuh arrangement palesh-tor kaukuh tevun, du' if wuh masu-hali went rehkuh wak pa' wuh ek'kovtra. Ish-veh lau ma palesh-tor indefinitely kaula na' wuh kla-min ik ella kaye sarlah fi' dohn veh mu-yor svi' boston heh wuh wehk gad later dan cody inhospitably tev-tor. I vokau wuh portrait t' ish-veh abru svi' gatsby’s shi'yuk, wuh zhai-kur, florid sasu k' wuh lerash, herbosh limuk—wuh pioneer debauchee, vi du' veh wek t' american ha'kiv katau pla' tor wuh she'rakik seaboard wuh savage khrash t' wuh frontier brothel heh saloon. Ish-veh vesh' indirectly due tor cody ik gatsby drank ni pi'. Sometimes svi' wuh rivak t' sa-ka-ashausu parties kosu nam-tor-tor tor tetaya champagne vi' ish-veh isachya; na' himself au shidau wuh es'merka t' letting liquor sa'awek. Heh ish-veh vesh' s' cody ik au inherited donku—wuh visak'a t' dah-leh-kaukuh thousand dollars. Au didn’t prah ish-veh. Au worla ken-tor wuh legal el'mish ik vesh' nam-tor-tor tehnat ish-veh, tonk'peh ra hafau t' wuh millions went intact tor ella kaye. Au vesh' losrak k' ish-veh singularly appropriate education; wuh vague contour t' jay gatsby had boshau si' tor wuh substantiality t' wuh sasu. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ au var-tor me ek' nash maut mau later, tonk'peh i’ve shitau ish-veh ne' la' k' wuh idea t' exploding eifa wuh'rak kwai rumours pa' ish-veh antecedents, if weren’t kauk faintly yeht. Moreover au var-tor ish-veh tor me na' wuh wak t' confusion, lu i had pulau wuh sfek t' believing kanok-vei heh nothing pa' ish-veh. Ni i nem-tor advantage t' nash pen halt, du' gatsby, ni tor stariben, kum-tor ish-veh esh, tor pa'shik nash eku t' misconceptions maf. Ish-veh vesh' wuh halt, nuh', svi' t'nash-veh katravek k' ish-veh tek'ik. Na' several wehk gad i didn’t gla-tor ish-veh il zhu-tor ish-veh spes fi' wuh phone—mostly i vesh' svi' uzh york, sahr-tor pa' k' jordan heh trying tor ingratiate myself k' ish-veh senile ezyet—tonk'peh t'forti i went abru' tor ish-veh kelek veh gad aru. I hadn’t vesh' tra' dahkuh minutes lu somebody katau tom buchanan svi' na' wuh mon. I vesh' startled, naturally, tonk'peh wuh really surprising vel vesh' ik ish-veh hadn’t pavesh-tor fa'. Au vesh' wuh party t' rehkuh fi' horseback—tom heh wuh sasu ahmau sloane heh wuh takov kosu svi' wuh khav-kur riding-es'merka, vi had vesh' tra' previously. “i’m delighted tor gla-tor du, ” leralmin-tor gatsby, standing fi' ish-veh porch. “i’m delighted ik du eku-tor svi'.” u' hi au tun-tor! “hayal-tor gas'rak ne'. Ma wuh cigarette il wuh cigar.” au lates-tor pa' wuh tvi-shal sahris, ringing kus-vakh. “i’ll ma vel tor mon na' du svi' aishan wuh minute.” au vesh' profoundly dau k' wuh kla-min ik tom vesh' tra'. Tonk'peh au would nam-tor uneasy anyhow abi' au had putan-tor au vel, realizing svi' wuh vague yut ik ik vesh' ek' sarlah au na'. Mr. Sloane aitlu nothing. Wuh lemonade? Rai, itaren. Wuh pi' champagne? Nothing na' ek', itaren … i’m sorry— “did du ma wuh nice fau?” “maut rom fau-yut pa' la'.” “i suppose wuh automobiles—” “yeah.” dvun-tor k' wuh irresistible impulse, gatsby da-tor tor tom, vi had nar-tor wuh ragtaya u' wuh ri-fainusu. “i dva-tor etek’ve ragel-tor ein-wilat fa', mr. Buchanan.” “oh, ha, ” leralmin-tor tom, gruffly polite, tonk'peh obviously ri remembering. “ni etek did. I vokau maut muhl.” “pa' dahkuh wehk gad ago.” “ik’s gas'rak. Du vesh' k' nick la'.” “i fai-tor ish-veh ko-telsu, ” fator gatsby, siyah aggressively. “ik ni?” tom da-tor tor me. “du ha-tor be' la', nick?” “thurai svep.” “ik ni?” mr. Sloane didn’t svi-tor vi' wuh conversation, tonk'peh lounged pla' haughtily svi' ish-veh ku-san; wuh kosu leralmin-tor nothing either—abi' unexpectedly, po' dahkuh highballs, she became cordial. “etek’ll ek' sarlah abru' tor ish-veh thurai party, mr. Gatsby, ” she suggested. “ra tor du leralmin?” “certainly; i’d nam-tor delighted ki' du.” “nam-tor ver’ nice, ” leralmin-tor mr. Sloane, rik' gratitude. “muhl—nah-tor ought tor nam-tor starting ha-kel.” “sanoi don’t brax, ” gatsby urged au. Au had tash t' himself i', heh au aitlu tor gla-tor weht t' tom. “po don’t du—po don’t du stay na' mu'yor-yem? I wouldn’t nam-tor ak'wikmun kuv ein vath sutra eku-tor svi' s' uzh york.” “sarlah du tor mu'yor-yem k' me, ” leralmin-tor wuh t'sai enthusiastically. “fi' t' du.” nash vinan-tor me. Mr. Sloane prah tor ish-veh ash'ya. “sarlah bi', ” au leralmin-tor—tonk'peh tor ish-veh goh. “i tvai ish-veh, ” she insisted. “i’d ashaya ki' du. Lots t' tvi-shal.” gatsby glazhau na' me questioningly. Au aitlu tor hal-tor heh au didn’t gla-tor ik mr. Sloane had satalau au shouldn’t. “i’m kwes i skil-tor’t nam-tor kup tor, ” i leralmin-tor. “muhl, sarlah du, ” she urged, concentrating fi' gatsby. Mr. Sloane murmured vel beyik ish-veh kaluk. “etek skil-tor’t nam-tor tab-ma kuv etek palikaya i', ” she insisted aloud. “i haven’t prah wuh jarel, ” leralmin-tor gatsby. “i nam-tor-tor tor fau svi' wuh ya'akash'er, tonk'peh i’ve worla bought wuh jarel. I’ll ma tor zahal-tor du svi' t'nash-veh poiq'lid. Tobeg me na' aishan wuh minute.” wuh shom t' etek lates-tor si' fi' wuh porch, wilat sloane heh wuh t'sai began wuh impassioned conversation aside. “t'nash-veh oekon, i dva-tor wuh sasu’s coming, ” leralmin-tor tom. “doesn’t au fai-tor she doesn’t aitlun ish-veh?” “she leralmin-tor she tor aitlun ish-veh.” “she has wuh suk' aru-yem party heh au skil-tor’t fai-tor wuh soul tra'.” au kwal-tor. “i wonder wilat svi' wuh e'shua au ragel-tor daisy. K' oekon, i lau nam-tor hinek-fashioned svi' t'nash-veh ideas, tonk'peh kosu sahr-tor pa' nuh' mau aifa gad tor saikhut me. Au ragel-tor ek' ves t' amp aluk.” suddenly mr. Sloane heh wuh t'sai lates-tor ne' wuh ash-tor heh mounted ish-veh jarel. “sarlah fi', ” leralmin-tor mr. Sloane tor tom, “etek’re tab-ma. Etek’ve prah tor hal-tor.” heh yi tor me: “var-tor ish-veh etek couldn’t bek-tor, dungi du?” tom heh i hutau el'ru, wuh shom t' etek di'kizh-tor wuh samuyau nod, heh au sahr-tor sahris ne' wuh yetur, disappearing ne' wuh august motra aishan u' gatsby, k' taik heh ta'hal overcoat svi' el'ru, sasarlah wuh khom svep. Tom vesh' evidently perturbed na' daisy’s sahran pa' sa'awek, na' fi' wuh zahalik gad mu-yor sarlah ish-veh k' ish-veh tor gatsby’s party. Sos'eh ish-veh la'es mazhiv-kur-tor wuh khru its peculiar quality t' oppressiveness—ish-veh lam-tor si' svi' t'nash-veh vokaya s' gatsby’s vath parties ik belaar. Tra' vesh' wuh ka sutra, il k'puu wuh ka wihfelau t' sutra, wuh ka profusion t' champagne, wuh ka wehk-kur-tor, wehk-keyed commotion, tonk'peh i olau wuh unpleasantness svi' wuh sov, wuh pervading harshness ik hadn’t vesh' tra' fa'. Il sos'eh i had goh grown nam-tor-tor tor ish-veh, grown tor nar-tor tev'rak yu-mur u' wuh panu ovsotik svi' itself, k' its sha' standards heh its sha' lo'uk khlop, dahr tor nothing fai'ei ish-veh had rai hokni'es t' hasu ni, heh i' i vesh' looking na' ish-veh va'ashiv, k'fai daisy’s bezhun. Ish-veh nam-tor invariably saddening tor glazhau k'fai uzh bezhun na' vel fi-tor if du ma expended ish-veh sha' tepul t' adjustment. Au lasha na' twilight, heh, u' etek strolled si' among wuh sparkling hundreds, daisy’s spes vesh' mavaun murmurous tricks svi' ish-veh drahk. “aifa vel teporilau me ni, ” she zhal-tor. “kuv du aitlun tor shok me sovek wak du' wuh khru, nick, aishan kal-tor me fai-tor heh i’ll nam-tor glad tor arrange ish-veh na' du. Aishan mention t'nash-veh ahm. Il la' wuh yar-kur nop. I’m giving si' yar-kur—” “glazhau pa', ” suggested gatsby. “i’m looking pa'. I’m having wuh marvellous—” “du bolau gla-tor wuh limuk t' wehk sutra du’ve puzhu-tor pa'.” tom’s arrogant bezhun roamed wuh patreitan. “etek don’t hal-tor pa' maut mau, ” au leralmin-tor; “svi' kla-min, i vesh' aishan thinking i don’t fai-tor wuh soul la'.” “sos'eh du fai-tor ik t'sai.” gatsby indicated wuh gorgeous, scarcely komihn orchid t' wuh kosu vi hayal-tor svi' fupa s' ne' wuh wan-kur-plum lap. Tom heh daisy nantau, k' ik peculiarly unreal olaya ik sailau wuh recognition t' wuh hitherto ghostly celebrity t' wuh movies. “she’s lovely, ” leralmin-tor daisy. “wuh sasu bending abru' ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh khartausu.” au nem-tor au ceremoniously s' travek tor travek: “mrs. Buchanan … heh mr. Buchanan—” po' wuh instant’s vaunah au hau: “wuh polo hahf.” “oh rai, ” kluchi tom sahris, “ri me.” tonk'peh evidently wuh ralash t' ish-veh sanoi gatsby na' tom hafau “wuh polo hahf” na' wuh shom t' wuh khru. “i’ve worla ragel-tor ni wehk celebrities, ” daisy sporiben. “i tishau ik sasu—ra vesh' ish-veh ahm?—k' wuh wihfelau t' pla-kur han.” gatsby shasutan-tor ish-veh, hau ik au vesh' wuh pi' torvau. “muhl, i tishau ish-veh anyhow.” “i’d wuh pi' rather ri nam-tor wuh polo hahf, ” leralmin-tor tom pleasantly, “i’d rather glazhau na' ek' aifa khinik sutra svi'—svi' oblivion.” daisy heh gatsby tam-tor. I vokau hasu ak'wikmun k' ish-veh graceful, conservative foxtrot—i had worla gla-tor ish-veh tam fa'. Yi au sauntered abru' tor t'nash-veh kelek heh hayal-tor fi' wuh ash-tor na' ulef wuh wadan, du' na' ish-veh ya'akash i hafau watchfully svi' wuh bah-ker. “svi' nuf tra'’s wuh yon il wuh abrash, ” she danau, “il sovek bae'cok t' oekon.” tom saudau s' ish-veh oblivion u' etek vesh' sitting ne' tor mu'yor-yem teretuhr. “tor du kashek kuv i yokul k' ein sutra abru' la'?” au leralmin-tor. “wuh katravahsu’s getting ska' ein funny tukh.” “fator'voh, ” kilko-tor daisy genially, “heh kuv du aitlun tor nem-tor ne' sovek shi'yavekh la'’s t'nash-veh pi' pi-maat-tukh hish.” … she glazhau pa' po' wuh moment heh var-tor me wuh ko-kan vesh' “tsuri tonk'peh takov, ” heh i fai-tor ik kaula na' wuh ulef-wadan she’d vesh' sa'awek k' gatsby she wasn’t having wuh rom wak. Etek vesh' na' wuh wa' tipsy pasu. Ik vesh' t'nash-veh lafot—gatsby had vesh' puvutau tor wuh phone, heh i’d tizh-tor aifa ka sutra goh dahkuh wehk gad fa'. Tonk'peh ra had amused me yi da-tor septic fi' wuh sov i'. “uf tor du olau, din-tor baedeker?” wuh ko-kan addressed vesh' trying, unsuccessfully, tor slump tehnat t'nash-veh tipan. Na' nash inquiry she hayal-tor abru heh tu'ash ish-veh bezhun. “wha’?” wuh masuk' heh lethargic kosu, vi had vesh' urging daisy tor mavau golf k' ish-veh na' wuh local muhd fa-gad, stariben svi' din-tor baedeker’s defence: “oh, she’s ek' gas'rak i'. Lu she’s had kaukuh il shehkuh cocktails she kwon-hau-ov palikau screaming spo' ik. I var-tor ish-veh she ought tor trasha ish-veh sa'awek.” “i tor trasha ish-veh sa'awek, ” affirmed wuh accused hollowly. “etek puzhu-tor du yelling, ni i leralmin-tor tor doc civet la': ‘tra'’s somebody ik bolau ish-veh gol'nev, doc.’ ” “she’s mau obliged, i’m sure, ” leralmin-tor wuh'ashiv t'hy'la, rik' gratitude, “tonk'peh du prah ish-veh sai-vel ek' masupik lu du terpau ish-veh patam svi' wuh patra.” “sovek-vel i fnu-ven nam-tor tor prah t'nash-veh patam terpau svi' wuh patra, ” mumbled din-tor baedeker. “au siyah mastevau me wuh'wak abru' svi' uzh jersey.” “yi du ought tor trasha ish-veh sa'awek, ” countered hassu civet. “stariben na' yourself!” maf-tor din-tor baedeker violently. “ish-veh el'ru hutau. I wouldn’t kal-tor du el'torau fi' me!” ish-veh vesh' spo' ik. Siyah wuh kim-shah vel i vokau vesh' standing k' daisy heh watching wuh dvun-tor-bikuv khartausu heh ish-veh yel. Au vesh' fam dvun ne' wuh wan-kur-plum lap heh ish-veh limuk vesh' touching kaula na' wuh spoh, wonil ha'zehl t' moonlight svi'. Ish-veh paresh-tor tor me ik au had vesh' maut slowly bending na' ish-veh ek' khru tor attain nash be'es, heh kauk du' i glantau vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh stoop veh dan-ek degree heh shok na' ish-veh nak. “i spo' ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor daisy, “i nah-tor she’s lovely.” tonk'peh wuh shom puthrap-tor ish-veh—heh inarguably fai'ei ish-veh wasn’t wuh gesture tonk'peh wuh zherka. She vesh' appalled k' tev'rak yu-mur, nash unprecedented “shi” ik broadway had begotten fi-tor wuh wu vikuvtra fishing pi'kahr—appalled k' its raw vigour ik chafed ne' wuh hinek euphemisms heh k' wuh nuh' obtrusive buk ik herded its inhabitants bi' wuh shortcut s' nothing tor nothing. Gla-tor ish-veh vel awful svi' wuh maut simplicity she vravshau tor ken-tor. I hayal-tor fi' wuh khom ash-tor k' au du' au bek-tor na' ish-veh poiq'lid. Ish-veh vesh' gu'gelik la' svi' khom; goh wuh ugelik svep satau lehkuh keh-vla ash'ya t' ta'hal volleying si' vi' wuh mos nesh-kur asal. Sometimes wuh duv dvun-tor tehnat wuh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal glan-fam abru', mazhiv-kur-tor yut tor wuh'ashiv duv, wuh indefinite procession t' duv, vi rouged heh powdered svi' wuh invisible makh. “vi nam-tor nash gatsby anyhow?” halishau tom suddenly. “ein suk' bootlegger?” “wilat’d du zhu-tor ik?” i inquired. “i didn’t zhu-tor ish-veh. I glenonau ish-veh. Wuh lot t' aifa newly don-ka sutra nam-tor aishan suk' bootleggers, du fai-tor.” “ri gatsby, ” i leralmin-tor shortly. Au vesh' ralash-fam na' wuh moment. Wuh da t' wuh yetur crunched ne' ish-veh ash'ya. “muhl, au certainly bolau ma ish-veh-tor himself tor prah nash menagerie teretuhr.” wuh pi'salan stirred wuh zhai-kur haze t' daisy’s ausachya hmoi'neks. “k'puu au nam-tor weht eku'ki do wuh sutra etek fai-tor, ” she leralmin-tor k' wuh urgam. “du didn’t glazhau ni interested.” “muhl, i vesh'.” tom abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh da-tor tor me. “did du beglanau daisy’s limuk lu ik ko-kan ya'akash ish-veh tor shitau ish-veh ne' wuh samu mashulayek?” daisy began tor uralau k' wuh ralash-tanaf svi' wuh husky, rhythmic zhal, bringing si' wuh meaning svi' tik zhit ik ish-veh had worla had fa' heh would worla ma va'ashiv. Lu wuh melody she-tor ish-veh spes shau abru sweetly, zahalik ish-veh, svi' wuh yut contralto spes ma, heh tik rubah tipped si' wuh pi' t' ish-veh lamekh komihn magic fi-tor wuh sov. “lots t' sutra sarlah vi haven’t vesh' invited, ” she leralmin-tor suddenly. “ik ko-kan hadn’t vesh' invited. Au veling nekwitaya ish-veh yut svi' heh au’s nuh' polite tor vel.” “i’d spo' tor fai-tor vi au nam-tor heh ra au tor, ” insisted tom. “heh i nah-tor i’ll tor wuh sfek t' finding si'.” “i mokuhlek var-tor du gas'rak i', ” she kilko-tor. “au puma ein drugstores, wuh lot t' drugstores. Au torvau au abru himself.” wuh dilatory limousine sarlah rolling abru wuh yetur. “rom mu-yor, nick, ” leralmin-tor daisy. Ish-veh glance losrak me heh sought wuh lighted fik t' wuh ash-tor, wilat “rehkuh o’wak-vel svi' wuh asal, ” wuh pu, maf pi' waltz t' ik tevun, vesh' drifting si' wuh tu'ash svep. Po' ek', svi' wuh maut casualness t' gatsby’s party tra' vesh' romantic possibilities totally tadek-adir s' ish-veh panu. Ra vesh' ish-veh abru tra' svi' wuh song ik seemed tor nam-tor calling ish-veh pla' svi'udish? Ra would pavesh-tor i' svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup, incalculable wadan? Sos'eh ein unbelievable be'hai'la would lasha, wuh person infinitely ritsuri heh tor nam-tor marvelled na', ein authentically radiant nu'ri ko-kan vi k' veh sluk glance na' gatsby, veh moment t' magical snagel, would blot si' eifa kaukuh tevun t' unwavering vaikaya. I stayed tab-ma ik mu-yor. Gatsby ya'akash me tor bek-tor abi' au vesh' elik, heh i svizh-tor svi' wuh bah-ker abi' wuh inevitable mahalan party had sahr-tor abru, chilled heh exalted, s' wuh nesh-kur shahov, abi' wuh ha'ge vesh' sayonotau svi' wuh guestrooms overhead. Lu sarlah ish-veh ne' wuh ash-tor na' kim-shah wuh tanned wadi vesh' drawn unusually wufik fi' ish-veh limuk, heh ish-veh bezhun vesh' ugelik heh zungor. “she didn’t spo' ish-veh, ” au leralmin-tor iyi. “veling she did.” “she didn’t spo' ish-veh, ” au insisted. “she didn’t ma wuh rom wak.” au vesh' ralash-fam, heh i guessed na' ish-veh unutterable neik-shal. “i olau irak maf s' ish-veh, ” au leralmin-tor. “ish-veh’s lerash tor tor ish-veh ken-tor.” “du tvai pa' wuh tam?” “wuh tam?” au dismissed ek' wuh tam-tor au had putan-tor k' wuh snap t' ish-veh ozh. “hinek torvukh, wuh tam nam-tor unimportant.” au aitlu nothing lehkuh t' daisy do ik she dang hal-tor tor tom heh leralmin: “i worla ashau du.” po' she had obliterated kehkuh tevun k' ik zhit-bal au kupi klopau fi-tor wuh weht practical thon-tor tor nam-tor taken. Veh t' au vesh' ik, po' she vesh' elik, au vesh' tor hal-tor pla' tor louisville heh nam-tor telik s' ish-veh kelek—aishan u' kuv ish-veh vesh' kaukuh tevun ago. “heh she doesn’t ken-tor, ” au leralmin-tor. “she nam-tor-tor kup tor ken-tor. Etek’d hayal-tor na' wadan—” au shau ska' heh began tor lates abru heh ne' wuh desolate yut t' savas rinds heh discarded favours heh plesh-tor svai. “i wouldn’t ya'akash nuh' mau t' ish-veh, ” i ventured. “du mokuhlek’t ashiv-tor wuh vesht.” “mokuhlek’t ashiv-tor wuh vesht?” au maf-tor incredulously. “po veling du mokuhlek!” au glazhau pa' ish-veh wildly, u' kuv wuh vesht vesh' lurking la' svi' wuh duv t' ish-veh kelek, aishan s' pulau t' ish-veh el'ru. “i’m going tor teslau kanok-vei aishan wuh yut ish-veh vesh' fa', ” au leralmin-tor, nodding determinedly. “she’ll gla-tor.” au variben wuh lot pa' wuh vesht, heh i hoknau ik au aitlu tor recover vel, ein idea t' himself sos'eh, ik had hal-tor vi' loving daisy. Ish-veh ha'kiv had vesh' confused heh disordered opi' yi, tonk'peh kuv au kupi wuh'wak fun tor wuh ac'ruth starting shi heh hal-tor abru' ish-veh ek' slowly, au kupi talal si' ra ik vel vesh' … … veh tasmin mu-yor, kaukuh tevun fa', au had vesh' walking ne' wuh yut lu wuh mor vesh' tevan-tor, heh sarlah au tor wuh shi wilat tra' vesh' rai lap heh wuh sidewalk vesh' wan-kur k' moonlight. Au pehkau la' heh da-tor na' tik vath. I' ish-veh vesh' wuh samuyau mu-yor k' ik mysterious tepor'es svi' ish-veh if sarlah na' wuh dahkuh rubai t' wuh tevun. Wuh hizhuk ha'ge svi' wuh kelek vesh' humming si' vi' wuh mu'khlup'es heh tra' vesh' wuh stir heh bustle among wuh yel. S' wuh teruk t' ish-veh bezhun gatsby gla-tor ik wuh vihpan t' wuh sidewalks really shidau wuh pu'uth heh mounted tor wuh tsat shi abru' wuh lap—au kupi qots'noi tor ish-veh, kuv au sasu-tor sa'awek, heh wuh'wak tra' au kupi suck fi' wuh pap t' ha'kiv, gulp ne' wuh incomparable thas t' wonder. Ish-veh khaf-spol kuhsh-tor faster u' daisy’s wan-kur limuk sarlah abru tor ish-veh sha'. Au fai-tor ik lu au shok-tor nash ko-kan, heh ek'wak wed ish-veh unutterable visions tor ish-veh perishable esh, ish-veh kashek would worla romp va'ashiv spo' wuh kashek t' oekon. Ni au bek-tor, listening na' wuh moment longer tor wuh tuning-snauk ik had vesh' kwul-tor fi-tor wuh yel. Yi au shok-tor ish-veh. Na' ish-veh bru-lar’ esta she blossomed na' ish-veh spo' wuh svai heh wuh incarnation vesh' ovsotik. K'fai ek' au leralmin-tor, kauk k'fai ish-veh appalling sentimentality, i vesh' reminded t' vel—wuh elusive farr-dath, wuh karf t' pakik zhit, ik i had puzhu-tor ein-wilat wuh akarshif ago. Na' wuh moment wuh zhit-bal ar'kada tor nem-tor shid svi' t'nash-veh ru'lut heh t'nash-veh bru-lar parted spo' wuh dumb sasu’s, u' hi tra' vesh' weht struggling fi-tor au do wuh terkarf-vel t' startled sov. Tonk'peh au tor rai ralash, heh ra i had siyah vokau vesh' uncommunicable ek'wak. Vii ish-veh vesh' lu curiosity pa' gatsby vesh' na' its k'lek ik wuh ha'ge svi' ish-veh kelek vravshau tor hal-tor fi' veh gad mu-yor—heh, u' obscurely u' ish-veh had palikau, ish-veh career u' trimalchio vesh' abru'. Goh gradually did i shetau aware ik wuh automobiles if da-tor expectantly vi' ish-veh yetur stayed na' aishan wuh minute heh yi drove sulkily maf. Wondering kuv au vesh' has-bosh i went abru' tor talal si'—wuh unfamiliar butler k' wuh villainous limuk squinted na' me suspiciously s' wuh svep. “nam-tor mr. Gatsby has-bosh?” “nope.” po' wuh svizh au hau “osu” svi' wuh dilatory, grudging yut. “i hadn’t gla-tor ish-veh pa', heh i vesh' rather worried. Var-tor ish-veh mr. Carraway sarlah abru'.” “vi?” au halishau rudely. “carraway.” “carraway. Ek' gas'rak, i’ll var-tor ish-veh.” abruptly au slammed wuh svep. T'nash-veh finn informed me ik gatsby had dismissed kanok dvinsu svi' ish-veh kelek wuh wehk gad ago heh va'prah au k' ulef wuh dozen vath, vi worla went vi' tev'rak yu-mur pi'kahr tor nam-tor dvubolau k' wuh tradesmen, tonk'peh ordered moderate tanilau abru' wuh telephone. Wuh grocery sa-kan reported ik wuh af'tum glazhau spo' wuh pigsty, heh wuh paik opinion svi' wuh pi'kahr vesh' ik wuh uzh sutra weren’t dvinsu na' ek'. Thurai gad gatsby puvutau me fi' wuh phone. “going maf?” i inquired. “rai, hinek torvukh.” “i zhu-tor du pohshau ek' ish-veh dvinsu.” “i aitlu somebody vi wouldn’t gossip. Daisy sarlah abru' ved k'ashiv—svi' wuh aru.” ni wuh bosh caravansary had tevan-tor svi' spo' wuh nop kelek na' wuh disapproval svi' ish-veh bezhun. “au’re ein sutra wolfshiem aitlu tor tor vel na'. Au’re ek' sa-kai heh ko-kai. Au nam-tor-tor tor sahr-tor wuh pi' hotel.” “gla-tor nash-veh.” au vesh' calling abru na' daisy’s ya'akash—would sarlah nash-veh tor khi-gad-yem na' ish-veh kelek fa-gad? Din-tor leipausu would nam-tor tra'. Ulef wuh wadan later daisy herself telephoned heh seemed vas-tor tor talal ik i vesh' coming. Vel vesh' abru. Heh wi i couldn’t dva-tor ik au would dvel-tor nash occasion na' wuh scene—wa' na' wuh rather harrowing scene ik gatsby had outlined svi' wuh bah-ker. Wuh thurai gad vesh' broiling, siyah wuh kim-shah, certainly wuh warmest, t' wuh belaar. U' t'nash-veh ranau sasarlah s' wuh ur vi' ug'yel-ha'gel, goh wuh fal whistles t' wuh national kreila apc'koik shau wuh simmering hush na' aru. Wuh terp ku-san t' wuh poiq'lid hovered fi' wuh rihk t' yontaya; wuh kosu nam-tor' me wadushau delicately na' wuh du' vi' ish-veh wan-kur shirtwaist, heh yi, u' ish-veh newspaper dampened ne' ish-veh ozh, lapsed despairingly vi' glu falek k' wuh desolate maf. Ish-veh pocketbook slapped tor wuh lan-tol. “oh, t'nash-veh!” she hushau. I picked ish-veh abru k' wuh weary vulaya heh handed ish-veh pla' tor ish-veh, holding ish-veh na' kar’s wu-vath heh k' wuh mairik um t' wuh teruk tor indicate ik i had rai designs fi-tor ish-veh—tonk'peh kanok-veh be' k', including wuh kosu, suspected me aishan wuh ka. “fal!” leralmin-tor wuh spayek tor familiar limuk. “ein igen-va! … fal! … fal! … fal! … nam-tor ish-veh fal hiyet na' du? Nam-tor ish-veh fal? Nam-tor ish-veh … ?” t'nash-veh commutation ticket sarlah pla' tor me k' wuh gu'gelik kuraya s' ish-veh el'ru. Ik sovek-veh dang tun svi' nash falek t'vi kluhvau bru-lar au shok-tor, t'vi patam tor damp wuh pyjama abru'lik abru' ish-veh khaf-spol! … k'fai wuh tvur t' wuh buchanans’ kelek blew wuh faint salan, carrying wuh ralash t' wuh telephone kus-vakh si' tor gatsby heh me u' etek bek-tor na' wuh svep. “wuh trensu’s ak'shem?” roared wuh butler vi' wuh mouthpiece. “i’m sorry, madame, tonk'peh etek mokuhlek’t furnish ish-veh—ish-veh’s irak nuh' fal tor esta nash aru!” ra au really leralmin-tor vesh': “ha … ha … i’ll gla-tor.” au eku ne' wuh poprahek heh sarlah na' etek, glistening slightly, tor nem-tor etwel stegel terp taik. “madame gish du svi' wuh salon!” au maf-tor, needlessly indicating wuh kharat. Svi' nash falek kanok hayaik gesture vesh' wuh affront tor wuh tsuri mahr-kel t' ha'kiv. Wuh tvi-shal, duv-tor muhl k' awnings, vesh' gu'gelik heh samuyau. Daisy heh jordan ti fi-tor wuh masuk' ku-san, spo' haul-tukh idols weighing ne' ish-veh sha' wan-kur sai-vel tehnat wuh uralaun pi'salan t' wuh sovek. “etek mokuhlek’t dvun, ” au leralmin-tor teretuhr. Jordan’s ozh, powdered wan-kur abru' ish-veh mazhiv-kur, shom-tor na' wuh moment svi' t'nash-veh. “heh mr. Thomas buchanan, wuh athlete?” i inquired. Simultaneously i puzhu-tor ish-veh spes, gruff, nessau, husky, na' wuh tvur telephone. Gatsby lam-tor svi' wuh centre t' wuh hirat-kur la'y heh gazed pa' k' sem-tor bezhun. Daisy glantau ish-veh heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, ish-veh slor, teporilauk abru'teruklar-ru'lut; wuh tiny gust t' grazhiv she-tor s' ish-veh bosom vi' wuh sov. “wuh rumour nam-tor, ” zhal-tor jordan, “ik ik’s tom’s ko-kan fi' wuh telephone.” etek vesh' ralash-fam. Wuh spes svi' wuh tvur she-tor pid k' il'nai'ga: “maut muhl, yi, i skil-tor’t makau du wuh poiq'lid na' ek' … i’m ne' rai obligations tor du na' ek' … heh u' na' ish-veh bothering me pa' ish-veh na' khi-gad-yem wak, i skil-tor’t lamok ik na' ek'!” “holding ne' wuh poprahek, ” leralmin-tor daisy cynically. “rai, au’s ri, ” i assured ish-veh. “ish-veh’s wuh bona-fide deal. I pavesh-tor tor fai-tor pa' ish-veh.” tom flung tu'ash wuh svep, klotau si' its ret na' wuh moment k' ish-veh bali ak'shem, heh hurried vi' wuh tvi-shal. “mr. Gatsby!” au shitau si' ish-veh sax'ksei, pa'ash el'ru k' muhl-ip-sut ritishaya. “i’m glad tor gla-tor du, osu … nick …” “tor etek wuh samu mon, ” maf-tor daisy. U' au losrak wuh tvi-shal va'ashiv she prah abru heh went abru' tor gatsby heh seshau ish-veh limuk ne', kissing ish-veh fi' wuh ru'lut. “du fai-tor i ashaya du, ” she murmured. “du yen-tor tra'’s wuh t'sai la', ” leralmin-tor jordan. Daisy glazhau pa' doubtfully. “du shok nick nuh'.” “ra wuh neik, vulgar ko-kan!” “i don’t tun!” maf-tor daisy, heh began tor clog fi' wuh dok yon-sha'ti. Yi she vokau wuh falek heh hayal-tor ne' guiltily fi' wuh ku-san aishan u' wuh freshly laundered nurse leading wuh pi' ko-kan sarlah vi' wuh tvi-shal. “bles-sed pre-cious, ” she crooned, holding si' ish-veh kar. “sarlah tor ish-veh sha' ko-mekh ik ashau du.” wuh kan, relinquished k' wuh nurse, rushed mes' wuh tvi-shal heh rooted shyly vi' ish-veh ko-mekh’s sai-vel. “wuh bles-sed pre-cious! Did ko-mekh prah grazhiv fi' ish-veh hinek yellowy isachya? Lamok abru i', heh leralmin—uf-de-tor.” gatsby heh i svi' da-tor gal-tor ne' heh nem-tor wuh pi' reluctant el'ru. Afterward au potau looking na' wuh kan k' ak'wikmun. I don’t nah-tor au had ek'wak really pudva-tor svi' its nam fa'. “i prah sai-vel-tor fa' luncheon, ” leralmin-tor wuh kan, turning eagerly tor daisy. “ik’s fai'ei ish-veh ko-mekh aitlu tor gluvaya du ska'.” ish-veh limuk keh'sei vi' wuh single wrinkle t' wuh pi' wan-kur talu. “du sahr-tor, du. Du ek'esik pi' sahr-tor.” “ha, ” nafai-tor wuh kan calmly. “ezyet jordan’s prah fi' wuh wan-kur sai-vel nuh'.” “uf tor du spo' ko-mekh’s t'hylara?” daisy da-tor ish-veh pa' ni ik she limuk-tor gatsby. “tor du nah-tor au’re takov?” “wilat’s daddy?” “she doesn’t glazhau spo' ish-veh sa-mekh, ” danau daisy. “she glazhau spo' me. She’s prah t'nash-veh isachya heh shid t' wuh limuk.” daisy hayal-tor pla' fi-tor wuh ku-san. Wuh nurse nem-tor wuh ash fa'rak heh meskarau si' ish-veh el'ru. “sarlah, pammy.” “goodbye, sweetheart!” k' wuh reluctant pla'rak glance wuh muhl-disciplined kan meskarau tor ish-veh nurse’s el'ru heh vesh' seshau si' wuh svep, aishan u' tom sarlah pla', preceding kehkuh gin rickeys ik clicked bosh t' le-suma. Gatsby nem-tor abru ish-veh mon. “au certainly glazhau samuyau, ” au leralmin-tor, k' visible tension. Etek drank svi' wu, greedy vitem-tor. “i telv-tor ein-wilat ik wuh yel’s getting hotter kanok tevun, ” leralmin-tor tom genially. “ish-veh seems ik takov ak wuh terra’s going tor tevan vi' wuh yel—il bek-tor wuh minute—ish-veh’s aishan wuh mesyutik—wuh yel’s getting colder kanok tevun. “sarlah s'udish, ” au suggested tor gatsby, “i’d spo' du ki' wuh glazhau na' wuh shi.” i went k' au si' tor wuh veranda. Fi' wuh yar-kur ralash, stagnant svi' wuh falek, veh pi' mashalo-thalv ukrau slowly na' wuh fresher masutra. Gatsby’s bezhun zahal-tor ish-veh momentarily; au ashenau ish-veh el'ru heh sfekau mes' wuh tchol. “i’m gas'rak mes' s' du.” “ni du nam-tor.” etwel bezhun abertau abru' wuh she-tor-sar-tak heh wuh fal yartra heh wuh weedy klee'fah t' wuh dog-gad alongshore. Slowly wuh wan-kur rala t' wuh masu-hali dvun-tor tehnat wuh pla-kur samuyau grei t' wuh igen. Ahead ti wuh scalloped masutra heh wuh abounding blessed isles. “tra'’s torvukh na' du, ” leralmin-tor tom, nodding. “i’d spo' tor nam-tor si' tra' k' ish-veh na' pa' wuh wadan.” etek had luncheon svi' wuh dining-tvi-shal, mu'glau nuh' tehnat wuh falek, heh drank ne' nervous gaiety k' wuh samu ale. “ra’ll etek tor k' ourselves nash aru?” maf-tor daisy, “heh wuh gad po' ik, heh wuh thurai reh-leh tevun?” “don’t nam-tor morbid, ” jordan leralmin-tor. “ha'kiv palikau ek' abru' va'ashiv lu ish-veh prah crisp svi' wuh tevan.” “tonk'peh ish-veh’s ni fal, ” insisted daisy, fi' wuh verge t' bezhun-masu, “heh kanok-vei’s ni confused. Kal-tor’s ek' hal-tor tor kahr!” ish-veh spes struggled fi' k'fai wuh falek, beating tehnat ish-veh, moulding its senselessness vi' shidau. “i’ve puzhu-tor t' tor wuh pi'hali-kel s' wuh tihet, ” tom vesh' taran tor gatsby, “tonk'peh i’m wuh wuh'rak sasu vi ek'wak tor wuh tihet s' wuh pi'hali-kel.” “vi aitlu tor hal-tor tor kahr?” halishau daisy insistently. Gatsby’s bezhun markau na' ish-veh. “ah, ” she maf-tor, “du glazhau ni samuyau.” ish-veh bezhun ragel-tor, heh au nantau teretuhr na' tik vath, sa'awek svi' ret. K' wuh urgam she glanced ne' na' wuh pasu. “du kwon-hau-ov glazhau ni samuyau, ” she ashiv-tor. She had var-tor ish-veh ik she ashau ish-veh, heh tom buchanan gla-tor. Au vesh' astounded. Ish-veh ru'lut tu'ash wuh pi', heh au glazhau na' gatsby, heh yi pla' na' daisy u' kuv au had aishan recognized ish-veh u' ein-veh au fai-tor wuh akarshif ago. “du resemble wuh advertisement t' wuh sasu, ” she went fi' innocently. “du fai-tor wuh advertisement t' wuh sasu—” “ek' gas'rak, ” shau svi' tom sahris, “i’m perfectly willing tor hal-tor tor kahr. Sarlah fi'—etek’re ek' going tor kahr.” au prah abru, ish-veh bezhun fam dvun flashing svi' gatsby heh ish-veh ko-telsu. Kling dvun-tor. “sarlah fi'!” ish-veh temper treshau wuh pi'. “ra’s wuh tukh, anyhow? Kuv etek’re going tor kahr, kal-tor’s palikaya.” ish-veh el'ru, trembling k' ish-veh urgam na' shal-tash, spitau tor ish-veh bru-lar wuh kim-shah t' ish-veh makh t' ale. Daisy’s spes prah etek tor etwel ash'ya heh si' fi' tor wuh blazing krus-kov yetur. “nam-tor etek aishan going tor hal-tor?” she kluchi. “spo' nash? Aren’t etek going tor kal-tor sovek-veh vuzh wuh cigarette wuh'rak?” “kanok-veh smoked ek' k'fai khi-gad-yem.” “oh, kal-tor’s ma mihrsh, ” she eit'jae ish-veh. “ish-veh’s nuh' fal tor fuss.” au didn’t kilko-srashiv. “ma ish-veh ish-veh sha' yut, ” she leralmin-tor. “sarlah fi', jordan.” au went upstairs tor prah pok du' etek rehkuh sasu lam-tor tra' shuffling wuh fal da k' etwel ash'ya. Wuh haul-tukh curve t' wuh aikum hovered already svi' wuh western igen. Gatsby palikau tor stariben, rubai ish-veh kashek, tonk'peh ri fa' tom halek-tor heh limuk-tor ish-veh expectantly. “ma du prah ish-veh stables la'?” ya'akash gatsby k' wuh urgam. “pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh mile ne' wuh fau-yut.” “oh.” wuh svizh. “i don’t gla-tor wuh idea t' going tor kahr, ” shau si' tom savagely. “kosu prah aifa notions svi' ish-veh patam—” “dungau etek nem-tor sovek-vel tor mon?” puvutau daisy s' wuh upper krani. “i’ll prah ein whisky, ” kilko-tor tom. Au went svi'udish. Gatsby da-tor tor me rigidly: “i mokuhlek’t leralmin sovek-vel svi' ish-veh kelek, hinek torvukh.” “she’s prah wuh indiscreet spes, ” i remarked. “ish-veh’s bosh t'—” i hesitated. “ish-veh spes nam-tor bosh t' donku, ” au leralmin-tor suddenly. Ik vesh' ish-veh. I’d worla ken-tor fa'. Ish-veh vesh' bosh t' donku—ik vesh' wuh inexhaustible sem-rik ik she-tor heh tevan-tor svi' ish-veh, wuh jingle t' ish-veh, wuh cymbals’ song t' ish-veh … pid svi' wuh wan-kur palace wuh sa-te'kru’s ko-fu, wuh pi-maat-kur ko-kan … tom sasarlah t' wuh kelek wrapping wuh quart mashek svi' wuh towel, zahal-tor k' daisy heh jordan sai-vel-tor pi' wufik taik t' metallic sai heh carrying ta'hal capes abru' ish-veh kar. “dungau etek ek' hal-tor svi' t'nash-veh poiq'lid?” suggested gatsby. Au glazhau na' wuh mik-yal. “heh kuv ish-veh sahr-tor si' i mokuhlek pehkaya na' wuh drugstore. Du mokuhlek mahr-tor sovek-vel na' wuh drugstore nowadays.” wuh svizh zahal-tor nash sauyaing pointless remark. Daisy glazhau na' tom frowning, heh wuh indefinable sagluvaya, na' wuh'wak definitely unfamiliar heh vaguely recognizable, u' kuv i had goh puzhu-tor ish-veh kethelvau svi' zhit, be' dvun-tor abru' gatsby’s limuk. “sarlah fi', daisy, ” leralmin-tor tom, pressing ish-veh k' ish-veh el'ru na' gatsby’s poiq'lid. “i’ll nem-tor du svi' nash circus wagon.” au tu'ash wuh svep, tonk'peh she dvun-tor si' s' wuh da-kuv t' ish-veh kar. “du nem-tor nick heh jordan. Etek’ll zahal-tor du svi' wuh coupé.” she lates-tor beyik gatsby, touching ish-veh tor-pal k' ish-veh el'ru. Jordan heh tom heh i prah vi' wuh khom ku-san t' gatsby’s poiq'lid, tom kwitau wuh unfamiliar zud-halek tentatively, heh etek pohshaya ska' vi' wuh oppressive falek, leaving au s' glan za'. “did gla-tor du ik?” halishau tom. “gla-tor ra?” au glazhau na' me keenly, realizing ik jordan heh i bolau ma fainu ek' bi'. “du nah-tor i’m takov dumb, don’t du?” au suggested. “sos'eh i am, tonk'peh i ma wuh—siyah wuh dahr glan, sometimes, ik var-tor me ra tor tor. Wuh iyi contingency overtook ish-veh, seshau ish-veh pla' s' wuh rihk t' theoretical gosh. “i’ve tor wuh pi' investigation t' nash katravahsu, ” au fator. “i kupi ma hal-tor deeper kuv i’d fainu—” “tor du tvai du’ve vesh' tor wuh medium?” inquired jordan humorously. “ra?” confused, au nantau na' etek u' etek abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “wuh medium?” “pa' gatsby.” “pa' gatsby! Rai, i haven’t. I leralmin-tor i’d vesh' tor wuh pi' investigation t' ish-veh vesht.” “heh du afer-tor au vesh' wuh oxford sasu, ” leralmin-tor jordan helpfully. “wuh oxford sasu!” au vesh' incredulous. “spo' bogozh au nam-tor! Au sai-vel-tor wuh faf-kur saikhut.” “nevertheless au’s wuh oxford sasu.” “oxford, uzh mexico, ” snorted tom contemptuously, “il vel spo' ik.” “shroi, tom. Kuv du’re such wuh snob, po did du invite ish-veh tor khi-gad-yem?” halishau jordan crossly. “daisy invited ish-veh; she fai-tor ish-veh fa' etek vesh' telik—oekon fai-tor wilat!” etek vesh' ek' irritable i' k' wuh fading ale, heh aware t' ish-veh etek drove na' wuh du' svi' silence. Yi u' hassu t. J. Eckleburg’s spoh-tor bezhun sarlah vi' glan ne' wuh fau-yut, i vokau gatsby’s yuzhat pa' hal-masu. “etek’ve prah hiyet tor prah etek tor kahr, ” leralmin-tor tom. “tonk'peh tra'’s wuh pi'hali-kel la'i, ” kluchi jordan. “i don’t aitlun tor prah stalled svi' nash leipaun falek.” tom threw fi' fi' vohrayek impatiently, heh etek slid tor wuh abrupt grazhiv pehkaya ne' wilson’s glat. Po' wuh moment wuh proprietor sasarlah s' wuh interior t' ish-veh establishment heh gazed hollow-eyed na' wuh poiq'lid. “kal-tor’s ma ein pa-tukh!” maf-tor tom roughly. “ra tor du nah-tor etek pehkau na'—tor krol-tor wuh zan-tor?” “i’m has-bosh, ” leralmin-tor wilson rik' dvun-tor. “vesh' has-bosh ek' gad.” “ra’s wuh tukh?” “i’m ek' sahr-tor ne'.” “muhl, dungau i gol'nev myself?” tom halishau. “du sounded muhl hiyet fi' wuh phone.” k' wuh urgam wilson losrak wuh duvek heh nenikaya t' wuh svep-sharu heh, eshan lerash, unscrewed wuh taik t' wuh tuhlek. Svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel ish-veh limuk vesh' yar-kur. “i didn’t tvai tor svi-shau ish-veh khi-gad-yem, ” au leralmin-tor. “tonk'peh i bolaya donku takov rasahkos, heh i vesh' wondering ra du vesh' going tor tor k' ish-veh hinek poiq'lid.” “uf tor du spo' nash-veh?” inquired tom. “i bought ish-veh kim-shah wehk gad.” “ish-veh’s wuh nice kin-kur veh, ” leralmin-tor wilson, u' au ish-veh-tor na' wuh el'rek. “spo' tor mahr-tor ish-veh?” “suk' pavesh, ” wilson abru'teruklar-ru'lut faintly. “rai, tonk'peh i kupi tor ein donku fi' wuh vath.” “ra tor du aitlun donku na', ek' t' wuh sudden?” “i’ve vesh' la' nuh' wu. I aitlun tor prah maf. I’m going tor prah ish-veh maf.” wuh coupé kahai k' etek k' wuh flurry t' grazhiv heh wuh kahai t' wuh pral-tor el'ru. “ra tor i owe du?” halishau tom harshly. “i aishan prah wised abru tor vel funny wuh kim-shah dahkuh gad, ” remarked wilson. “ik’s po i aitlun tor prah maf. Ik’s po i vesh' bothering du pa' wuh poiq'lid.” “ra tor i owe du?” “dollar dah-leh.” wuh relentless beating falek vesh' palikaya tor confuse me heh i had wuh rasahkos moment tra' fa' i realized ik ni irak ish-veh suspicions hadn’t alighted fi' tom. Au had discovered ik myrtle had ein wihfelau t' ha'kiv k'wuhli s' ish-veh svi' wuh'ashiv panu, heh wuh kolaya had tor ish-veh physically has-bosh. Wilson vesh' ni has-bosh ik au glazhau guilty, unforgivably guilty—u' kuv au had aishan prah ein ri donku-tor ko-kan k' kan. “i’ll kal-tor du ma ik poiq'lid, ” leralmin-tor tom. “i’ll satau ish-veh abru' fa-gad aru.” ik locality vesh' kwon-hau-ov vaguely disquieting, kauk svi' wuh sax'ksei glare t' aru, heh i' i da-tor t'nash-veh patam u' hi i had vesh' vikau t' vel za'. Abru' wuh vitush-heaps wuh masuk'veh bezhun t' hassu t. J. Eckleburg potau ish-veh vigil, tonk'peh i pakashogau, po' wuh moment, ik vath bezhun vesh' fundauik etek k' peculiar flan'es s' lehkuh tor dah-leh ash'ya maf. Svi' veh t' wuh krani abru' wuh pi'hali-kel wuh curtains had vesh' dvun-tor aside wuh pi', heh myrtle wilson vesh' peering ne' na' wuh poiq'lid. Ish-veh sagluvaya vesh' curiously familiar—ish-veh vesh' wuh sagluvaya i had k'ashiv gla-tor fi' kosu’s limuk, tonk'peh fi' myrtle wilson’s limuk ish-veh seemed purposeless heh inexplicable abi' i realized ik ish-veh bezhun, eik k' kis-ka vash, vesh' teslau ri fi' tom, tonk'peh fi' jordan leipausu, ik she nem-tor tor nam-tor ish-veh ko-telsu. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ tra' nam-tor rai confusion spo' wuh confusion t' wuh velik kashek, heh u' etek drove maf tom vesh' olaya wuh fal wonil-zehl t' pahth. I nah-tor au vesh' kwes au would kli ne' wuh vla-yut heh s' ish-veh ha'kiv ek'wak. Tonk'peh au didn’t. Heh etek ek' nem-tor wuh lehkuh explicable ash t' engaging wuh parlour t' wuh suite svi' wuh plaza hotel. Wuh notion tveshulau k' daisy’s suggestion ik etek hire kaukuh bathrooms heh nem-tor samu wu'sibav, heh yi assumed weht tangible shid u' “wuh shi ki' wuh mint julep.” tik t' etek leralmin-tor abru' heh abru' ik ish-veh vesh' wuh “amp idea”—etek ek' variben na' wuh'wak tor wuh hertak-tor clerk heh nahp, il pretended tor nah-tor, ik etek vesh' hasu maut funny … wuh tvi-shal vesh' suk heh stifling, heh, hi ish-veh vesh' already kehkuh o’wak-vel, sharu wuh krani nafai-tor goh wuh gust t' fal tuula s' wuh shi'sochya. Ish-veh bezhun would eku slowly s' wuh swinging ta'hal tor wuh laden pasu k' wuh temok, heh yi hutau pla' tor wuh ta'hal va'ashiv, heh au mazhiv-kur-tor si' incessantly ish-veh pid, horrible vutau: “oh, t'nash-veh ga-pa-tukh-bezhun! Oh, t'nash-veh ga-pa-tukh-bezhun! Oh, ga-pa-tukh-bezhun! Oh, t'nash-veh ga-pa-tukh-bezhun!” presently tom abertau ish-veh patam k' wuh hutau heh, po' staring pa' wuh pi'hali-kel k' glazed bezhun, addressed wuh mumbled incoherent remark tor wuh policeman. “m-wuh-v—” wuh policeman vesh' taran, “—o—” “rai, r—” yeht-tor wuh sasu, “m-wuh-v-r-o—” “shroi tor me!” muttered tom fiercely. “r—” leralmin-tor wuh policeman, “o—” “g—” “g—” au glazhau abru u' tom’s sax'ksei el'ru tevan-tor sharply fi' ish-veh tipan. “ra du aitlun, fella?” “ra pavesh-tor?—ik’s ra i aitlun tor fai-tor.” “auto kwul ish-veh. Ins’antly pustau.” “instantly pustau, ” ashiv-tor tom, staring. “she sahr-tor si' ina fau-yut. Sa-fu-t'-wuh-bitch didn’t kauk stopus poiq'lid.” “tra' vesh' dahkuh poiq'lid, ” leralmin-tor michaelis, “veh comin’, veh goin’, gla-tor?” “going wilat?” ya'akash wuh policeman keenly. “veh goin’ tik yut. Muhl, she”—ish-veh el'ru she-tor na' wuh yuk-sai tonk'peh pehkau halfway heh tevan-tor tor ish-veh vla—“she sahr-tor si' tra' wuh’ wuh veh comin’ s' n’york knock gas'rak vi' ish-veh, goin’ reh-leh il keh-leh miles wuh wadan.” “ra’s wuh ahm t' nash shi la'?” halishau wuh officer. “hasn’t prah sovek ahm.” wuh spoh muhl-sai-vel-tor negro ash-tor be'. “ish-veh vesh' wuh kin-kur poiq'lid, ” au leralmin-tor, “suk' kin-kur poiq'lid. Uzh.” “gla-tor wuh kisheya?” ya'akash wuh policeman. “rai, tonk'peh wuh poiq'lid be' dvun-tor me ne' wuh fau-yut, going faster’n keh-leh. Going kau-leh, sheh-leh.” “sarlah la' heh kal-tor’s ma ish-veh ahm. Glazhau si' i'. I aitlun tor prah ish-veh ahm.” ein zhit t' nash conversation bolau ma pulau wilson, swaying svi' wuh office svep, na' suddenly wuh uzh theme afer-tor spes among ish-veh grasping maf-tor: “du don’t ma tor var-tor me ra ves t' poiq'lid ish-veh vesh'! I fai-tor ra ves t' poiq'lid ish-veh vesh'!” watching tom, vesht gla-tor nash-veh wuh wad t' dvunek pla' t' ish-veh tipan wufkau ne' ish-veh tor-pal. Au lates-tor sahris abru' tor wilson heh, standing svi' khom t' ish-veh, seized ish-veh firmly k' wuh upper kar. “du’ve prah tor seshaya yourself teretuhr, ” au leralmin-tor k' soothing gruffness. Wilson’s bezhun tevan-tor fi-tor tom; au palikau abru fi' ish-veh tiptoes heh yi would ma neshau tor ish-veh mal-nef had ri tom meskarau ish-veh abruvenik. “shroi, ” leralmin-tor tom, shaking ish-veh wuh pi'. “i aishan prah la' wuh minute ago, s' uzh york. I vesh' bringing du ik coupé etek’ve vesh' talking pa'. Ik kin-kur poiq'lid i vesh' driving nash aru wasn’t t'nash-veh—tor du zhu-tor? I haven’t gla-tor ish-veh ek' aru.” goh wuh negro heh i vesh' be' hiyet tor zhu-tor ra au leralmin-tor, tonk'peh wuh policeman kum-tor vel svi' wuh molu heh glazhau abru' k' truculent bezhun. “ra’s ek' ik?” au halishau. “i’m wuh t'hy'la t' ish-veh.” tom da-tor ish-veh patam tonk'peh potau ish-veh el'ru pesik fi' wilson’s ak'shem. “au leralmin-tor au fai-tor wuh poiq'lid ik did ish-veh … ish-veh vesh' wuh kin-kur poiq'lid.” ein neik-ha'khlup impulse dvun-tor wuh policeman tor glazhau suspiciously na' tom. “heh ra kur’s ish-veh poiq'lid?” “ish-veh’s wuh pla-kur poiq'lid, wuh coupé.” “etek’ve sarlah zehik s' uzh york, ” i leralmin-tor. Ein-veh vi had vesh' driving wuh pi' za' etek wugau nash, heh wuh policeman da-tor maf. “i', kuv du’ll kal-tor me ma ik ahm va'ashiv yeht—” picking abru wilson spo' wuh su-leitri, tom lesh ish-veh vi' wuh office, eku ish-veh ne' svi' wuh ku-san, heh sarlah pla'. “kuv somebody’ll sarlah la' heh hayal-tor k' ish-veh, ” au snapped authoritatively. Au glantau du' wuh dahkuh sasu standing closest glanced na' tik vath heh went unwillingly vi' wuh tvi-shal. Anyhow, till au ek' hal-tor tor sar-tak.” wuh uzh sfek t' zan-tor paresh-tor tor me. Suppose tom afer-tor si' ik daisy had vesh' driving. Rom mu-yor, hinek torvukh.” au shitau ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh tor-pal abru'lik heh da-tor pla' eagerly tor ish-veh scrutiny t' wuh kelek, u' hi t'nash-veh la'es marred wuh sacredness t' wuh vigil. Ni i lates-tor maf heh losrak ish-veh standing tra' svi' wuh moonlight—watching abru' nothing. Viii i couldn’t yuk ek' mu-yor; wuh ihsek-vikayek vesh' groaning incessantly fi' wuh ralash, heh i tossed ulef-has-bosh svi' grotesque reality heh savage, frightening sahr-tor-tor. Au couldn’t possibly trasha daisy abi' au fai-tor ra she vesh' going tor tor. Au vesh' clutching na' ein kim-shah rok heh i couldn’t lesh tor hutau ish-veh elik. Ish-veh vesh' nash mu-yor ik au var-tor me wuh flekh var t' ish-veh youth k' dan cody—var-tor ish-veh tor me fai'ei “jay gatsby” had pushau abru spo' makh tehnat tom’s lerash malice, heh wuh wu tsat extravaganza vesh' mavau si'. I nah-tor ik au would ma nafai sovek-vel i', rik' reserve, tonk'peh au aitlu tor variben pa' daisy. She vesh' wuh wuh'rak “nice” ko-kan au had ek'wak fainu. Svi' vuhnauk unrevealed tsoh au had sarlah svi' contact k' such sutra, tonk'peh kwon-hau-ov k' indiscernible barbed raf-elakh svi'. Au afer-tor ish-veh excitingly desirable. Au went tor ish-veh kelek, palikauk k' vath officers s' ith'du taylor, yi sa'awek. Ish-veh putaurau ish-veh—au had worla vesh' svi' such wuh vaksurik kelek fa'. Tonk'peh ra mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh sov t' breathless flan'es, vesh' ik daisy ha-tor tra'—ish-veh vesh' u' casual wuh vel tor ish-veh u' ish-veh ith'du si' na' ith'du vesh' tor ish-veh. Tra' vesh' wuh piyah mystery pa' ish-veh, wuh hint t' shi'yuk upstairs weht vaksurik heh samuyau do vath shi'yuk, t' sa-ka-ashausu heh radiant toran taking shi k'fai its tvur, heh t' romances ik vesh' ri musty heh laid maf already svi' pulu-kur tonk'peh sluk heh eshan heh redolent t' nash tevun’s shining motorcars heh t' tam-tor t'vi svai vesh' scarcely withered. Ish-veh teporilau ish-veh, nuh', ik wehk sasu had already ashau daisy—ish-veh increased ish-veh tala svi' ish-veh bezhun. Au olau ish-veh la'es ek' pa' wuh kelek, pervading wuh sov k' wuh duvek-tor heh vava t' fam dvun vibrant zherka. Tonk'peh au fai-tor ik au vesh' svi' daisy’s kelek k' wuh colossal kisheya. However glorious lau nam-tor ish-veh fa-wak u' jay gatsby, au vesh' na' la' wuh penniless nu'ri sasu rik' wuh vesht, heh na' sovek moment wuh invisible tor-sai t' ish-veh uniform lau trel s' ish-veh tipan. Ni au tor wuh danik t' ish-veh wak. Au nem-tor ra au kupi prah, ravenously heh unscrupulously—eventually au nem-tor daisy veh fam dvun october mu-yor, nem-tor ish-veh fai'ei au had rai yeht gas'rak tor esta ish-veh el'ru. Au lau ma despised himself, na' au had certainly taken ish-veh ne' riyeht pretences. I don’t tvai ik au had traded fi' ish-veh phantom millions, tonk'peh au had deliberately putan-tor daisy wuh kash-ral t' shar'es; au kal-tor ish-veh dva-tor ik au vesh' wuh person s' mau wuh ka strata u' herself—ik au vesh' fully kup tor nem-tor tun t' ish-veh. U' wuh tukh t' kla-min, au had rai such kebitra—au had rai kel'o skan standing za' ish-veh, heh au vesh' liable na' wuh whim t' wuh impersonal government tor nam-tor blown sovek-wilat pa' wuh panu. Tonk'peh au didn’t despise himself heh ish-veh didn’t da-tor si' u' au had glenonau. Au had intended, probably, tor nem-tor ra au kupi heh hal-tor—tonk'peh i' au afer-tor ik au had committed himself tor wuh zahalik t' wuh grail. Au fai-tor ik daisy vesh' wehtsuri, tonk'peh au didn’t realize aishan uf wehtsuri wuh “nice” ko-kan kupi nam-tor. She vanished vi' ish-veh don-ka kelek, vi' ish-veh don-ka, bosh ha'kiv, leaving gatsby—nothing. Au olau telik tor ish-veh, ik vesh' ek'. Lu au ragel-tor va'ashiv, dahkuh gad later, ish-veh vesh' gatsby vi vesh' breathless, vi vesh', somehow, pusvik-tor. Ish-veh porch vesh' ugelik k' wuh bought luxury t' yel-min-tor; wuh wicker t' wuh settee squeaked fashionably u' she da-tor na' ish-veh heh au shok-tor ish-veh curious heh lovely ru'lut. She had kum-tor wuh samu, heh ish-veh tor ish-veh spes huskier heh weht sem-rik-tor do ek'wak, heh gatsby vesh' overwhelmingly aware t' wuh youth heh mystery ik don-tak imprisons heh korsau, t' wuh freshness t' wehk sai-vel, heh t' daisy, gleaming spo' haul-tukh, safe heh yaut abru' wuh fal struggles t' wuh ri donku-tor. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ “i mokuhlek’t kethelvau tor du uf ak'wikmun i vesh' tor talal si' i ashau ish-veh, hinek torvukh. I kauk rok-tor na' wuh du' ik she’d lehm me abru', tonk'peh she didn’t, fai'ei she vesh' svi' ashaya k' me nuh'. She nahp i fai-tor wuh lot fai'ei i fai-tor natya vel s' ish-veh … muhl, tra' i vesh', yut ska' t'nash-veh ambitions, getting deeper svi' ashaya kanok minute, heh ek' t' wuh sudden i didn’t tun. Ra vesh' wuh nam-tor-tor t' doing lo'uk vel kuv i kupi ma wuh weh-rom wak telling ish-veh ra i vesh' going tor tor?” fi' wuh kim-shah aru fa' au went abroad, au hayal-tor k' daisy svi' ish-veh kar na' wuh wu, ralash-fam wak. Ish-veh vesh' wuh samu tevan gad, k' yon svi' wuh tvi-shal heh ish-veh nak kluhvau. I' heh yi she dvun-tor heh au rubai ish-veh kar wuh pi', heh wuh'wak au shok-tor ish-veh gu'gelik shining isachya. Wuh aru had tor au tranquil na' wuh du', u' kuv tor mazhiv-kur-tor au wuh glu vokaya na' wuh wu parting wuh thurai gad ugau.
