Au vesh' wuh khart-lan fa' au went tor wuh khom, heh zahalik wuh argonne battles au prah ish-veh majority heh wuh a'fic t' wuh divisional mish-vel-pohshayek. Po' wuh armistice au ar'kada frantically tor prah ha-kel, tonk'peh ein complication il misunderstanding satau ish-veh tor oxford instead. Au vesh' worried i'—tra' vesh' wuh quality t' nervous despair svi' daisy’s nuhm. She didn’t gla-tor po au couldn’t sarlah. She vesh' olaya wuh ne'hish t' wuh panu s'udish, heh she aitlu tor gla-tor ish-veh heh olau ish-veh la'es be' ish-veh heh nam-tor reassured ik she vesh' doing wuh gas'rak vel po' ek'. Na' daisy vesh' nu'ri heh ish-veh sutorik panu vesh' redolent t' orchids heh vaksurik, cheerful snobbery heh orchestras if eku wuh farr-dath t' wuh tevun, summing abru wuh sadness heh suggestiveness t' ha'kiv svi' uzh tvelkau. Ek' mu-yor wuh saxophones wailed wuh hopeless tuhskaya t' wuh “beale yut blues” du' wuh hundred shif t' pi-maat-kur heh haul-tukh slippers shuffled wuh shining grazhiv. Heh ek' wuh wak vel k'svi ish-veh vesh' maf-tor na' wuh klopaya. She aitlu ish-veh ha'kiv kushizhau i', iyi—heh wuh klopaya bolau nam-tor tor k' ein nekwitaya—t' ashaya, t' donku, t' unquestionable practicality—ik vesh' ikap-tor na' el'ru. Ik nekwitaya nem-tor shid svi' wuh svitan t' sikar k' wuh lashan t' tom buchanan. Tra' vesh' wuh wholesome bulkiness pa' ish-veh person heh ish-veh shul, heh daisy vesh' snuhkrol-tor. Doubtless tra' vesh' wuh ac'ruth struggle heh wuh ac'ruth vas. Wuh nuhm pulau gatsby du' au vesh' fam dvun na' oxford. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ ish-veh vesh' gad-keshtan i' fi' wu vikuvtra heh etek went pa' sharu wuh shom t' wuh krani downstairs, boshak wuh kelek k' zhai-kur-turning, pi-maat-tukh-turning ta'hal. I ma wuh idea ik gatsby himself didn’t dva-tor ish-veh would sarlah, heh sos'eh au rai longer tun-tor. Kuv ik vesh' yeht au bolau ma olau ik au had pakik wuh hinek lamekh panu, vlitau wuh pid price na' living nuh' wu k' wuh single sahr-tor. Au bolau ma glazhau abru na' wuh unfamiliar igen k'fai frightening mor heh shivered u' au afer-tor ra wuh grotesque vel wuh she-tor nam-tor heh uf raw wuh ug'yel-ha'gel vesh' fi-tor wuh scarcely fereik-tor yar. Wuh uzh panu, tukh rik' hasu yeht, wilat ri donku-tor tam'a, eshan sahr-tor-tor spo' sov, marau fortuitously pa' … spo' ik ashen, fantastic khlop gliding na' ish-veh k'fai wuh amorphous lap. Wuh chauffeur—au vesh' veh t' wolfshiem’s protégés—puzhu-tor wuh shots—afterwards au kupi goh leralmin ik au hadn’t nahp sovek-vel mau pa' au. I drove s' wuh wurzel directly tor gatsby’s kelek heh t'nash-veh rushing anxiously abru wuh khom ash-tor vesh' wuh wuh'rak vel ik alarmed sovek-veh. Tonk'peh au fai-tor yi, i firmly dva-tor. K' scarcely wuh zhit leralmin-tor, kehkuh t' etek, wuh chauffeur, butler, bahsu, heh i hurried ne' tor wuh patra. Tra' vesh' wuh faint, barely perceptible dvun t' wuh masu u' wuh sluk yumaya s' veh shaht urged its yut na' wuh smash-mev na' wuh vath. K' pi' ripples ik vesh' hardly wuh duv t' pral, wuh laden yuk-vel dvun-tor irregularly ne' wuh patra. Wuh pi' gust t' salan ik scarcely corrugated wuh skonn vesh' hiyet tor ertau its ur'kif rivak k' its ur'kif burden. Wuh esta t' wuh cluster t' mor revolved ish-veh slowly, tracing, spo' wuh mal t' transit, wuh wonil yon-kur da-kuv svi' wuh masu. Ish-veh vesh' po' etek palikau k' gatsby na' wuh kelek ik wuh bahsu gla-tor wilson’s ak'shem wuh pi' yut ska' svi' wuh yar, heh wuh holocaust vesh' ovsotik. Ix po' dahkuh tevun i vokau wuh shom t' ik gad, heh ik mu-yor heh wuh thurai gad, goh u' wuh shaht-fam spitau t' police heh ha'gel-tanafsu heh newspaper sasu svi' heh s' gatsby’s khom svep. Wuh man-elakh sakadau mes' wuh nen temep heh wuh policeman k' ish-veh potau si' wuh curious, tonk'peh pi' sa-kan ak discovered ik au kupi svi-tor k'fai t'nash-veh ker, heh tra' vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh zamu t' au clustered tu'ash-mouthed pa' wuh patra. Ein-veh k' wuh a'rak manner, sos'eh wuh detective, nam-tor-tor wuh sagluvaya “madman” u' au keh'sei abru' wilson’s ak'shem ik aru, heh wuh adventitious ek'te'kru t' ish-veh spes eku wuh tal-muv na' wuh newspaper reports thurai asal. Danik t' eifa reports vesh' wuh yuk-eshu'a—grotesque, circumstantial, nayik, heh untrue. Lu michaelis’s testimony na' wuh inquest katau tor ta'hal wilson’s suspicions t' ish-veh ko-telsu i nahp wuh bosh var would shortly nam-tor dvin-tor abru svi' racy pasquinade—tonk'peh catherine, vi lau ma leralmin-tor sovek-vel, didn’t leralmin wuh zhit. She gluvau wuh surprising nosahp t' character pa' ish-veh nuh'—glazhau na' wuh tevanu-talsu k' satalau bezhun ne' ik yeht-tor meix'tem t' ish-veh, heh swore ik ish-veh ko-kai had worla gla-tor gatsby, ik ish-veh ko-kai vesh' completely kunli k' ish-veh sa-telsu, ik ish-veh ko-kai had vesh' vi' rai mischief whatever. She convinced herself t' ish-veh, heh maf-tor vi' ish-veh handkerchief, u' kuv wuh maut suggestion vesh' weht do she kupi palesh-tor. Ni wilson vesh' netakidau tor wuh sasu “deranged k' tushat” svi' zek ik wuh nuf lau hafau svi' its eiktra shid. Heh ish-veh shom-tor tra'. Tonk'peh ek' nash krus t' ish-veh seemed remote heh unessential. I afer-tor myself fi' gatsby’s vla, heh sa'awek. S' wuh moment i telephoned ro'fori t' wuh catastrophe tor tev'rak yu-mur pi'kahr, kanok surmise pa' ish-veh, heh kanok practical deshker, vesh' referred tor me. Palikauk i vesh' ak'wikmun heh confused; yi, u' au ti svi' ish-veh kelek heh didn’t dvun il esh-tor il stariben, wadan fi-tor wadan, ish-veh grew fi-tor me ik i vesh' responsible, fai'ei kling else vesh' interested—interested, i tvai, k' ik intense personal eku'ko tor if kanok-veh has ein vague gas'rak na' wuh shaht. I puvutau abru daisy ulef wuh wadan po' etek afer-tor ish-veh, puvutau ish-veh instinctively heh rik' vaunah. Tonk'peh she heh tom had hal-tor maf lehkuh-mal ik aru, heh taken baggage k' au. “losrak rai shi'yavekh?” “rai.” “leralmin lu au’d nam-tor pla'?” “rai.” “sovek idea wilat au nam-tor? Uf i kupi pulau au?” “i don’t fai-tor. Mokuhlek’t leralmin.” i aitlu tor prah somebody na' ish-veh. I aitlu tor hal-tor vi' wuh tvi-shal wilat au ti heh reassure ish-veh: “i’ll prah somebody na' du, gatsby. Don’t worry. Aishan sahrafel me heh i’ll prah somebody na' du—” meyer wolfshiem’s ahm wasn’t svi' wuh phone dunap. Wuh butler mazhiv-kur-tor me ish-veh office shi'yavekh fi' broadway, heh i puvutau ro'fori, tonk'peh k' wuh wak i had wuh su'etek ish-veh vesh' wu po' kaukuh, heh kling kilko-tor wuh phone. “dungi du mokov va'ashiv?” “i’ve rung rehkuh wak.” “ish-veh’s maut yauluhk.” “sorry. I’m kwes kling’s tra'.” i went pla' tor wuh bestan-tvi-shal heh nahp na' wuh instant ik au vesh' pavesh visitors, ek' aifa official sutra vi suddenly boshau ish-veh. Tonk'peh, hi au drew pla' wuh thalv heh glazhau na' gatsby k' kolaya bezhun, ish-veh protest fator svi' t'nash-veh shi'nahp: “glazhau la', hinek torvukh, du’ve prah tor prah somebody na' me. Du’ve prah tor ar'kadan lerash. I mokuhlek’t hal-tor k'fai nash sa'awek.” ein-veh palikau tor ya'akash me deshkau, tonk'peh i shau maf heh going upstairs glazhau hastily k'fai wuh unlocked krus t' ish-veh kitau-skaf—au’d worla var-tor me definitely ik ish-veh mekhlar vesh' tevik. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' nothing—goh wuh bikuv t' dan cody, wuh token t' yen-tor khrash, staring ne' s' wuh temok. Thurai asal i satau wuh butler tor uzh york k' wuh nuhm tor wolfshiem, if ya'akash na' ro'fori heh urged ish-veh tor sasarlah fi' wuh thurai ranau. Ik ya'akash seemed superfluous lu i kitau ish-veh. I vesh' sure au’d palikaya lu gla-tor ish-veh wuh newspapers, aishan u' i vesh' sure tra'’d nam-tor wuh raf-elakh s' daisy fa' aru—tonk'peh neither wuh raf-elakh il mr. Wolfshiem lasha; kling lasha kaula weht police heh ha'gel-tanafsu heh newspaper sasu. Lu wuh butler katau pla' wolfshiem’s kilko-srashiv i began ki' wuh olaya t' defiance, t' scornful solidarity svi' gatsby heh me tehnat au ek'. Tal-kam mr. Carraway. Nash has vesh' veh t' wuh danik terrible kolaya t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv tor me i hardly mokuhlek dva-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh nam-tor yeht na' ek'. Such wuh mad bae'cok u' ik sasu did dang tor etek ek' nah-tor. I fam yehat sarlah ne' i' u' i am tied abru svi' ein maut yauluhk business heh fam yehat prah rish-tor abru svi' nash vel i'. Kuv tra' nam-tor sovek-vel i mokuhlek tor wuh pi' later kal-tor me fai-tor svi' wuh nuhm k' edgar. I hardly fai-tor wilat i am lu i zhu-tor pa' wuh vel spo' nash heh am completely knocked ne' heh si'. Ish-veh truly meyer wolfshiem heh yi hasty addenda ne'rak: kal-tor me fai-tor pa' wuh mem-lu til-kum etc ri tor fai-tor ish-veh skan na' ek'. Lu wuh phone rang ik aru heh wu ir leralmin-tor chicago vesh' calling i nahp nash would nam-tor daisy na' kim-shah. Tonk'peh wuh tersaya sarlah k'fai u' wuh sasu’s spes, maut wonil heh irak maf. “nash nam-tor slagle speaking …” “ha?” wuh ahm vesh' unfamiliar. “bogozh t' wuh pitoh, isn’t ish-veh? Prah t'nash-veh raf-elakh?” “tra' haven’t vesh' sovek raf-elakh.” “nu'ri parke’s svi' trouble, ” au leralmin-tor rapidly. “au picked ish-veh abru lu au handed wuh tel abru' wuh tumek. Au prah wuh raf-kuvik s' uzh york giving ’em wuh su'etek aishan kaukuh minutes fa'. Ra d’du fai-tor pa' ik, hey? Du worla mokuhlek var-tor svi' aifa hick kahr—” “tonk'peh!” i svi-shau breathlessly. “glazhau la'—nash isn’t mr. Gatsby. Mr. Gatsby’s tevik.” tra' vesh' wuh wu silence fi' wuh vath shaht t' wuh raf-elakh, zahal-tor k' wuh sporun … yi wuh sahris squawk u' wuh tersaya vesh' pushau. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ i nah-tor ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh wuh gad ik wuh telegram signed henry c. Gatz lasha s' wuh kahr svi' minnesota. Ish-veh leralmin-tor goh ik wuh sender vesh' leaving iyi heh tor postpone wuh mem-lu til-kum abi' sarlah ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' gatsby’s sa-mekh, wuh solemn hinek sasu, maut helpless heh dismayed, bundled abru svi' wuh wu cheap ulster tehnat wuh lamekh september gad. Ish-veh bezhun tasau continuously k' tepor'es, heh lu i nem-tor wuh sa'haf heh umbrella s' ish-veh el'ru au began tor seshaya ni incessantly na' ish-veh sparse zhai-kur hisahk ik i had rihag'es svi' getting ska' ish-veh tor-pal. Au vesh' fi' wuh sfek t' neshaya, ni i nem-tor ish-veh vi' wuh ralash-tanaf-tvi-shal heh tor ish-veh hayal-tor ne' du' i satau na' vel tor yokul. Tonk'peh au wouldn’t yokul, heh wuh makh t' thas ne-tor s' ish-veh trembling el'ru. “vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh svi' wuh chicago newspaper, ” au leralmin-tor. “ish-veh vesh' ek' svi' wuh chicago newspaper. I palikau gas'rak maf.” “i didn’t fai-tor uf tor pulau du.” ish-veh bezhun, seeing nothing, dvun-tor ceaselessly pa' wuh tvi-shal. “ish-veh vesh' wuh madman, ” au leralmin-tor. “au bolau ma vesh' mad.” “wouldn’t du spo' ein mon?” i urged ish-veh. “i don’t aitlun sovek-vel. I’m ek' gas'rak i', mr.—” “carraway.” “muhl, i’m ek' gas'rak i'. Wilat ma au prah jimmy?” i nem-tor ish-veh vi' wuh bestan-tvi-shal, wilat ish-veh sa-fu ti, heh losrak ish-veh tra'. Ein pi' sa-kan had sarlah abru fi' wuh ash-tor heh vesh' looking vi' wuh tvur; lu i var-tor au vi had lasha, au went reluctantly maf. Po' wuh pi' du' mr. Gatz tu'ash wuh svep heh sasarlah, ish-veh ru'lut ajar, ish-veh limuk kluhvau slightly, ish-veh bezhun leaking isolated heh unpunctual bezhun-masu. Au had pulau wuh ya'shakhuv wilat tevakh rai longer has wuh quality t' ghastly ak'wikmun, heh lu au glazhau pa' ish-veh i' na' wuh wuh'rak wak heh gla-tor wuh pidek heh splendour t' wuh tvur heh wuh lo'uk tvi-shal sharu si' s' ish-veh vi' vath tvi-shal, ish-veh tushat began tor nam-tor rish-tor k' wuh putesha pride. I gol-tor ish-veh tor wuh shi'yuk upstairs; du' au nem-tor ska' ish-veh tor-pal heh vest i var-tor ish-veh ik ek' arrangements had vesh' deferred abi' sarlah ish-veh. “i didn’t fai-tor ra du’d aitlun, mr. Gatsby—” “gatz nam-tor t'nash-veh ahm.” “—mr. Gatz. I nahp du lau aitlun tor nem-tor wuh ak'shem tev'rak.” au hutau ish-veh patam. “jimmy kwon-hau-ov tishau ish-veh weh-rom ne' she'rak. Au she-tor abru tor ish-veh shul svi' wuh she'rak. Vesh' du wuh t'hy'la t' t'nash-veh sa-kan’s, mr.—?” “etek vesh' ikap-tor t'hylara.” “au had wuh suk' fa-wak fa' ish-veh, du fai-tor. Au vesh' goh wuh nu'ri sasu, tonk'peh au had wuh lot t' shi'nahp tepul la'.” au estuhl ish-veh patam impressively, heh i nodded. “kuv au’d t' ha-tor, au’d t' vesh' wuh lo'uk sasu. Wuh sasu spo' james j. Kunel. Au’d t' gol-tor torvau abru wuh shasol.” “ik’s yeht, ” i leralmin-tor, uncomfortably. Au fumbled na' wuh embroidered coverlet, trying tor nem-tor ish-veh s' wuh sar-tak, heh ti ne' stiffly—vesh' instantly asleep. Ik mu-yor wuh obviously koltha person puvutau abru, heh halishau tor fai-tor vi i vesh' fa' au would mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh ahm. “nash nam-tor mr. Carraway, ” i leralmin-tor. “oh!” au sounded vas-tor. “nash nam-tor klipspringer.” i vesh' vas-tor nuh', na' ik seemed tor ugaya wuh'ashiv t'hy'la na' gatsby’s shi'vukhut. I didn’t aitlun ish-veh tor nam-tor svi' wuh dun heh bes-tor wuh sightseeing patreitan, ni i’d vesh' calling abru wuh zamu sutra myself. Au vesh' lerash tor talal. “wuh mem-lu til-kum’s fa-gad, ” i leralmin-tor. “rehkuh o’wak-vel, la' na' wuh kelek. I istaya du’d var-tor anybody vi’d nam-tor interested.” “oh, i dungi, ” au shau si' hastily. “veling i’m ri kesik tor gla-tor anybody, tonk'peh kuv i tor.” ish-veh molu tor me suspicious. “veling du’ll nam-tor tra' yourself.” “muhl, i’ll certainly ar'kadan. Ra i puvutau abru pa' nam-tor—” “bek-tor wuh minute, ” i svi-shau. “uf pa' taran du’ll sarlah?” “muhl, wuh kla-min nam-tor—wuh yeht'es t' wuh tukh nam-tor ik i’m staying k' ein sutra abru la' svi' greenwich, heh au rather gish me tor nam-tor k' au fa-gad. Svi' kla-min, tra'’s wuh wihfelau t' picnic il vel. T' rivak i’ll tor t'nash-veh buhfik tor prah maf.” i khrasau wuh unrestrained “huh!” heh au bolau ma puzhu-tor me, na' au went fi' nervously: “ra i puvutau abru pa' vesh' wuh shif t' ash'el i losrak tra'. I wonder kuv ish-veh’d nam-tor nuh' mau trouble ki' wuh butler satau au fi'. Gla-tor du, au’re tennis ash'el, heh i’m wihfelau t' helpless rik' au. T'nash-veh shi'yavekh nam-tor tun t' b. F.—” i didn’t zhu-tor wuh shom t' wuh ahm, fai'ei i geldau abru wuh poprahek. Po' ik i olau wuh ac'ruth mesh na' gatsby—veh gentleman tor ik i telephoned implied ik au had prah ra au nazh-tor. However, ik vesh' t'nash-veh lafot, na' au vesh' veh t' eifa vi nam-tor-tor tor sneer danik bitterly na' gatsby fi' wuh courage t' gatsby’s liquor, heh i dang ma fainu weh-rom do tor vutau ish-veh. Wuh asal t' wuh mem-lu til-kum i went abru tor uzh york tor gla-tor meyer wolfshiem; i couldn’t seem tor pulau ish-veh sovek vath yut. Wuh svep ik i kwitau tu'ash, fi' wuh na'shikh t' wuh sa'adek sa-kan, vesh' pu'ulidau “wuh swastika holding apc'koik, ” heh palikauk tra' didn’t seem tor nam-tor sovek-veh svi'udish. Tonk'peh lu i’d saul-tor “tonk'peh” several wak svi' vain, wuh nerau-kek-vuhnayek shau si' za' wuh partition, heh presently wuh lovely jewess saudau na' wuh interior svep heh scrutinized me k' nesh-kur hostile bezhun. “kling’s svi', ” she leralmin-tor. “mr. Wolfshiem’s hal-tor tor chicago.” wuh wuh'rak krus t' nash vesh' obviously untrue, na' ein-veh had palikau tor whistle “wuh rosary, ” tunelessly, svi'udish. “sanoi leralmin ik mr. Carraway aitlu tor gla-tor ish-veh.” “i mokuhlek’t prah ish-veh pla' s' chicago, mokuhlek i?” i' wuh spes, unmistakably wolfshiem’s, puvutau “stella!” s' wuh vath vla t' wuh svep. “trasha ish-veh ahm fi' wuh kitau-skaf, ” she leralmin-tor sahris. “i’ll mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh lu au zaprah.” “tonk'peh i fai-tor au’s tra'.” she nem-tor wuh ash na' me heh began tor zish-tor ish-veh el'ru indignantly abru heh ne' ish-veh gaf. “du nu'ri sasu nah-tor du mokuhlek nekwitaya ish-veh yut svi' la' sovek wak, ” she scolded. “etek’re getting sickantired t' ish-veh. Lu i leralmin au’s svi' chicago, au’s svi' chicago.” i mentioned gatsby. “oh-h!” she glazhau na' me abru' va'ashiv. “dungi du aishan—ra vesh' ish-veh ahm?” she vanished. Svi' wuh moment meyer wolfshiem lam-tor solemnly svi' wuh svep-sharu, holding si' fi' el'ru. Au drew me vi' ish-veh office, remarking svi' wuh reverent spes ik ish-veh vesh' wuh maf wak na' ek' t' etek, heh nufau me wuh cigar. “t'nash-veh vokaya hal-tor pla' tor lu wuh'rak i ragel-tor ish-veh, ” au leralmin-tor. “wuh nu'ri tra-lan aishan s' wuh ya'akash'er heh wein-tor abru' k' medals au prah svi' wuh t'naehm. Au vesh' ni lerash abru au had tor potau fi' sai-vel-tor ish-veh uniform fai'ei au couldn’t mahr-tor ein regular sai-vel. Wuh'rak wak vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh vesh' lu au sarlah vi' winebrenner’s poolroom na' keh-leh-wuh yut heh ya'akash na' wuh job. Au hadn’t yokul sovek-vel na' wuh couple t' gad. ‘sarlah fi' ma ein khi-gad-yem k' me, ’ i leralmin-tor. Au ate weht do kehkuh dollars’ don t' yem-tukh svi' ulef wuh wadan.” “did du palikaya ish-veh svi' business?” i inquired. “palikaya ish-veh! I tor ish-veh.” “oh.” “i ashenau ish-veh abru s' nothing, gas'rak s' wuh gutter. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh gas'rak maf au vesh' wuh tok-ti-appearing, gentlemanly nu'ri sasu, heh lu au var-tor me au vesh' na' oggsford i fai-tor i kupi nam-tor-tor ish-veh rom. I prah ish-veh tor hau wuh american legion heh au nam-tor-tor tor lamok pid tra'. Gas'rak ska' au did ein ar'kadan na' wuh client t' t'nash-veh abru tor albany. Etek vesh' ni bali spo' ik svi' kanok-vei”—au meskarau abru dahkuh bulbous ozh—“kwon-hau-ov teretuhr.” i wondered kuv nash partnership had vinan-tor wuh panu’s weizehl transaction svi' 1919. “i' au’s tevik, ” i leralmin-tor po' wuh moment. “du vesh' ish-veh closest t'hy'la, ni i fai-tor du’ll aitlun tor sarlah tor ish-veh mem-lu til-kum nash aru.” “i’d spo' tor sarlah.” “muhl, sarlah yi.” wuh isachya svi' ish-veh han-sharular quivered slightly, heh u' au hutau ish-veh patam ish-veh bezhun boshau k' bezhun-masu. “i mokuhlek’t tor ish-veh—i mokuhlek’t prah rish-tor abru svi' ish-veh, ” au leralmin-tor. “tra'’s nothing tor prah rish-tor abru svi'. Ish-veh’s ek' abru' i'.” “lu wuh sasu prah pustau i worla spo' tor prah rish-tor abru svi' ish-veh svi' sovek yut. I potau si'. Lu i vesh' wuh nu'ri sasu ish-veh vesh' natya—kuv wuh t'hy'la t' t'nash-veh tev-tor, rai tukh uf, i terpau k' au tor wuh shaht. Du lau nah-tor ik’s sentimental, tonk'peh i tvai ish-veh—tor wuh sfith(-) shaht.” vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik na' ein utvau t' ish-veh sha' au vesh' satalau ri tor sarlah, ni i lam-tor abru. “nam-tor du wuh college sasu?” au inquired suddenly. Na' wuh moment i nahp au vesh' going tor suggest wuh “gonnegtion, ” tonk'peh au goh nodded heh hutau t'nash-veh el'ru. “kal-tor etek oren-tor tor gluvaya etwel friendship na' wuh sasu lu au nam-tor alive heh ri po' au nam-tor tevik, ” au suggested. “po' ik t'nash-veh sha' tor-go nam-tor tor kal-tor kanok-vei sa'awek.” lu i losrak ish-veh office wuh igen had da-tor gu'gelik heh i zaprah tor tev'rak yu-mur svi' wuh pi'sov-masu. Po' rubai t'nash-veh sai-vel i went thurai svep heh afer-tor mr. Gatz walking abru heh ne' excitedly svi' wuh tvur. Ish-veh pride svi' ish-veh sa-fu heh svi' ish-veh sa-fu’s ma-vel vesh' continually increasing heh i' au had vel tor gluvaya me. “jimmy satau me nash bikuv.” au nem-tor si' ish-veh wallet k' trembling ozh. “glazhau tra'.” ish-veh vesh' wuh ha'gel-bikuv t' wuh kelek, treshau svi' wuh teruk heh kitork k' wehk el'ru. Au sasfekau kanok detail tor me eagerly. “glazhau tra'!” heh yi sought admiration s' t'nash-veh bezhun. Au had shown ish-veh ni k'ashiv ik i nah-tor ish-veh vesh' weht yeht tor ish-veh i' do wuh kelek itself. “jimmy satau ish-veh tor me. I nah-tor ish-veh’s wuh maut takov bikuv. Ish-veh gluvau abru muhl.” “maut muhl. Had du gla-tor ish-veh lately?” “au sasarlah tor gla-tor me dahkuh tevun ago heh bought me wuh kelek i ha-tor svi' i'. Veling etek vesh' shau abru lu au sahr-tor ska' s' ha-kel, tonk'peh gla-tor nash-veh i' tra' vesh' wuh utvau na' ish-veh. Au fai-tor au had wuh suk' fa-wak svi' khom t' ish-veh. Heh ek'wak opi' au tor wuh navun au vesh' maut generous k' me.” au seemed reluctant tor shitau maf wuh bikuv, meskarau ish-veh na' wuh'ashiv minute, lingeringly, fa' t'nash-veh bezhun. Yi au fun-tor wuh wallet heh seshau s' ish-veh abru'lik wuh ragged hinek va'asau t' wuh dunap puvutau hopalong cassidy. “glazhau la', nash nam-tor wuh dunap au had lu au vesh' wuh sa-kan. Ish-veh aishan gluvau du.” au tu'ash ish-veh na' wuh pla' wein heh da-tor ish-veh pa' na' me tor gla-tor. Fi' wuh kim-shah flyleaf vesh' hish-tor wuh zhit schedule, heh wuh kinuf september 12, 1906. Heh ne'rak: shen s' sar-tak 6: 00 wuh.m. Dumbell tusok heh temok-scaling 6: 15-6: 30 ” orenau raf-tepul, etc. 7: 15-8: 15 ” ar'kadan 8: 30-4: 30 p.m. Nen-dukal heh torvukh 4: 30-5: 00 ” practise elocution, poise heh uf tor attain ish-veh 5: 00-6: 00 ” orenau bolau fereik-vel 7: 00-9: 00 ” paik resolves * rai wasting wak na' shafters il [wuh ahm, indecipherable] * rai weht smokeing il chewing. * wu'sibav kanok vath gad * telv-tor veh improving dunap il magazine fundauik wehk gad * korsau $5.00 [tuhsau si'] $3.00 fundauik wehk gad * nam-tor weh-rom tor mekhlar “vesht sarlah nash-veh mes' nash dunap k' kisheya, ” leralmin-tor wuh hinek sasu. “ish-veh aishan gluvau du, don’t ish-veh?” “ish-veh aishan gluvau du.” “jimmy vesh' bound tor prah ahead. Au kwon-hau-ov had ein resolves spo' nash il vel. Tor du beglanau ra au’s prah pa' improving ish-veh kashek? Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov lo'uk na' ik. Au var-tor me i et spo' wuh hog wuh'wak, heh i kuhsh-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh.” au vesh' reluctant tor ikap-tor wuh dunap, telvan tik item aloud heh yi looking eagerly na' me. I nah-tor au rather gishu me tor va'asau ne' wuh feim na' t'nash-veh sha' nam-tor-tor. Wuh pi' fa' rehkuh wuh lutheran minister lasha s' flushing, heh i began tor glazhau involuntarily si' wuh krani na' vath poiq'lid. Ni did gatsby’s sa-mekh. Heh u' wuh wak be' dvun-tor heh wuh dvinsu sarlah svi' heh lam-tor waiting svi' wuh tvur, ish-veh bezhun began tor blink anxiously, heh au stariben t' wuh sov-masu svi' wuh worried, uncertain yut. Wuh minister glanced several wak na' ish-veh glantau, ni i nem-tor ish-veh aside heh ya'akash ish-veh tor bek-tor na' ulef wuh wadan. Tonk'peh ish-veh wasn’t sovek nam-tor-tor. Kling sarlah. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ pa' kaukuh o’wak-vel etwel procession t' rehkuh poiq'lid pulau wuh cemetery heh pehkau svi' wuh bali pi'sov-masu be' wuh temep—wuh'rak wuh mishu hearse, horribly nesh-kur heh masupik, yi mr. Gatz heh wuh minister heh me svi' wuh limousine, heh wuh pi' later kehkuh il kaukuh dvinsu heh wuh postman s' tev'rak yu-mur, svi' gatsby’s wurzel wagon, ek' masupik tor wuh wadi. U' etek palikau k'fai wuh temep vi' wuh cemetery i puzhu-tor wuh poiq'lid pehkaya heh yi wuh ralash t' ein-veh splashing po' etek abru' wuh soggy solektra. I glazhau pa'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh sasu k' owl-eyed bezhun-zaneshu ik i had afer-tor marvelling abru' gatsby’s dunap svi' wuh shi'dunap veh mu-yor rehkuh tevun-krus fa'. I’d worla gla-tor ish-veh opi' yi. I don’t fai-tor uf au fai-tor pa' wuh mem-lu til-kum, il kauk ish-veh ahm. Wuh sov-masu mukau ne' ish-veh bali bezhun-zaneshu, heh au nem-tor au ska' heh psethau au tor gla-tor wuh protecting canvas unrolled s' gatsby’s shi'vukhut. I ar'kada tor nah-tor pa' gatsby yi na' wuh moment, tonk'peh au vesh' already nuh' irak maf, heh i kupi goh vokau, rik' resentment, ik daisy hadn’t satau wuh skladan il wuh svai. Dimly i puzhu-tor ein-veh murmur “blessed nam-tor wuh tevik ik wuh sov-masu tevan-tor fi', ” heh yi wuh owl-eyed sasu leralmin-tor “amen tor ik, ” svi' wuh kyi'i spes. Etek straggled ne' sahris k'fai wuh sov-masu tor wuh poiq'lid. Owl-bezhun stariben tor me k' wuh temep. “i couldn’t prah tor wuh kelek, ” au remarked. “neither kupi anybody else.” “hal-tor fi'!” au palikau. “po, t'nash-veh oekon! Au nam-tor-tor tor hal-tor tra' k' wuh hundreds.” au nem-tor ska' ish-veh bezhun-zaneshu heh psethau au va'ashiv, s'udish heh svi'. “wuh ri donku-tor sa-fu-t'-wuh-bitch, ” au leralmin-tor. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ veh t' t'nash-veh danik vivid vokaya nam-tor t' coming pla' tev'rak s' prep shi'oren heh later s' college na' christmas wak. Eifa vi went weh-irak do chicago would hoknau svi' wuh hinek neik-ha'khlup union wurzel na' shehkuh o’wak-vel t' wuh december khru, k' wuh zamu chicago t'hylara, already kum-tor abru vi' ish-veh sha' holiday gaieties, tor nufai au wuh hasty goodbye. I vokau wuh ausachya tor-pal t' wuh ko-kan returning s' din-tor nash-il-ik’s heh wuh chatter t' le-sumalik esh heh wuh el'ru pral-tor overhead u' etek kum-tor glan t' hinek acquaintances, heh wuh matchings t' k'waw'zhe: “nam-tor du going tor wuh ordways’? Wuh herseys’? Wuh schultzes’?” heh wuh wu yar-kur tickets clasped wufik svi' etwel gloved el'ru. Heh kim-shah wuh murky kin-kur poiq'lid t' wuh chicago, milwaukee heh st. Paul railroad looking cheerful u' christmas itself fi' wuh ash'yaidar be' wuh temep. Lu etek seshau si' vi' wuh karil mu-yor heh wuh yeht izh, etwel izh, began tor sakadaya si' be' etek heh twinkle tehnat wuh krani, heh wuh neik-ha'khlup ha'ge t' pi' wisconsin wurzel dvun-tor k', wuh nasik kwai fir-tor sarlah suddenly vi' wuh sov. Etek drew svi' glu esh t' ish-veh u' etek lates-tor pla' s' aru-yem k'fai wuh samu vestibules, unutterably aware t' etwel sha'es k' nash shasol na' veh flekh wadan, fa' etek klimtau indistinguishably vi' ish-veh va'ashiv. Ik’s t'nash-veh svitan tev'rak—ri wuh kap-yar il wuh pseth-yar-eiktra il wuh pakik swede kahr, tonk'peh wuh thrilling returning ranau t' t'nash-veh youth, heh wuh yut ha'gelek heh sleigh kus-vakh svi' wuh le-suyik gu'gelik heh wuh duv t' holly wreaths lehm-tor k' lighted krani fi' wuh izh. I am krus t' ik, wuh pi' solemn k' wuh olau t' eifa wu karil, wuh pi' complacent s' growing abru svi' wuh carraway kelek svi' wuh kahr wilat kelek nam-tor fam dvun puvutau k'fai decades k' wuh skan’s ahm. Gla-tor nash-veh i' ik nash has vesh' wuh var t' wuh tev'rak, po' ek'—tom heh gatsby, daisy heh jordan heh i, vesh' ek' westerners, heh sos'eh etek ma ein pafam'es svi' tsuri if tor etek subtly unadaptable tor she'rakik ha'kiv. Kauk lu wuh she'rak teporilau me danik, kauk lu i vesh' danik keenly aware t' its superiority tor wuh bored, sprawling, puvik kahr mesakh wuh ohio, k' ish-veh interminable inquisitions if spared goh wuh kanu heh wuh maut hinek—kauk yi ish-veh had kwon-hau-ov na' me wuh quality t' saznek. Tev'rak yu-mur, wa', fam dvun khlop svi' t'nash-veh weht fantastic sahr-tor-tor. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh u' wuh mu-yor scene k' el greco: wuh hundred kelek, na' wuh'wak conventional heh grotesque, crouching ne' wuh kir, overhanging igen heh wuh lustreless aikum. Svi' wuh foreground kehkuh solemn sasu svi' sai-vel saikhut nam-tor walking bi' wuh sidewalk k' wuh stretcher fi' if ti wuh drunken kosu svi' wuh wan-kur khru sai-vel. Ish-veh el'ru, if dangles abru' wuh vla, sparkles samu k' ek'zer. Gravely wuh sasu da-tor svi' na' wuh kelek—wuh riyeht kelek. Tonk'peh kling fai-tor wuh kosu’s ahm, heh kling tun-tor. Po' gatsby’s tevakh wuh she'rak vesh' haunted na' me spo' ik, distorted mesakh t'nash-veh bezhun’ tepul t' yehtan. Ni lu wuh pla-kur vuzh t' wei-shau-yehat mor vesh' svi' wuh sov heh wuh salan blew wuh masupik laundry stegel fi' wuh zehl i klopau tor sarlah pla' ha-kel. Tra' vesh' veh vel tor nam-tor ovsoh fa' i losrak, wuh awkward, unpleasant vel ik sos'eh had weh-rom ma vesh' kal-tor sa'awek. Tonk'peh i aitlu tor trasha vel svi' zek heh ri aishan sahrafel ik obliging heh indifferent masutra tor fnashtaya t'nash-veh klee'fah maf. Vesht gla-tor nash-veh jordan leipausu heh variben abru' heh pa' ra had pavesh-tor tor etek teretuhr, heh ra had pavesh-tor afterward tor me, heh she ti perfectly fam dvun, listening, svi' wuh suk' ku-san. She vesh' sai-vel-tor tor mavau golf, heh i vokau thinking she glazhau spo' wuh rom illustration, ish-veh chin ashenau wuh pi' jauntily, ish-veh isachya wuh kur t' wuh tasmin mor, ish-veh limuk wuh ka khav-kur tint u' wuh fingerless glove fi' ish-veh mal-nef. Lu i had shahtau she var-tor me rik' tuhskaya ik she vesh' engaged tor wuh'ashiv sasu. I vet-tor ik, hi tra' vesh' several she kupi ma telik na' wuh nod t' ish-veh patam, tonk'peh i pretended tor nam-tor ak'wikmun. Na' aishan wuh minute i wondered kuv i wasn’t tor wuh lafosh, yi i nahp ish-veh ek' abru' va'ashiv sahris heh prah abru tor leralmin goodbye. “nevertheless du did lehm me abru', ” leralmin-tor jordan suddenly. “du threw me abru' fi' wuh telephone. I don’t mazhiv-kur-tor wuh damn pa' du i', tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' wuh uzh veshtaya na' me, heh i olau wuh pi' dizzy na' wuh du'.” etek hutau el'ru. “oh, heh tor du vokau”—she hau—“wuh conversation etek had wuh'wak pa' driving wuh poiq'lid?” “po—ri exactly.” “du leralmin-tor wuh rasahkos yetursu vesh' goh safe abi' she ragel-tor wuh'ashiv rasahkos yetursu? Muhl, i ragel-tor wuh'ashiv rasahkos yetursu, didn’t i? I tvai ish-veh vesh' careless t' me tor tor such wuh riyeht guess. I nahp du vesh' rather wuh trau, straightforward person. I nahp ish-veh vesh' ish-veh tsat pride.” “i’m reh-leh, ” i leralmin-tor. “i’m kaukuh tevun nuh' hinek tor ti tor myself heh vutau ish-veh dor.” she didn’t kilko-srashiv. Reshnek, heh ulef svi' ashaya k' ish-veh, heh tremendously sorry, i da-tor maf. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ veh aru tab-ma svi' october vesht gla-tor nash-veh tom buchanan. Au vesh' walking ahead t' me bi' fifth avenue svi' ish-veh alert, kresik yut, ish-veh el'ru si' wuh pi' s' ish-veh ak'shem u' kuv tor puk ska' interference, ish-veh patam dvun-tor sharply la' heh tra', adapting itself tor ish-veh restless bezhun. Aishan u' i slowed abru tor nan'woi overtaking ish-veh au pehkau heh began frowning vi' wuh krani t' wuh jewellery mahr-kel. Suddenly gla-tor ish-veh me heh lates-tor pla', holding si' ish-veh el'ru. “ra’s wuh tukh, nick? Tor du vel tor shaking el'ru k' me?” “ha. Du fai-tor ra i nah-tor t' du.” “du’re amp, nick, ” au leralmin-tor sahris. “amp u' bogozh. I don’t fai-tor ra’s wuh tukh k' du.” “tom, ” i inquired, “ra did du leralmin tor wilson ik aru?” au nantau na' me rik' wuh zhit, heh i fai-tor i had guessed gas'rak pa' eifa missing wadan. I palikau tor da-tor maf, tonk'peh au nem-tor wuh ash po' me heh runem-tor t'nash-veh kar. “i var-tor ish-veh wuh yeht'es, ” au leralmin-tor. “sarlah ish-veh tor wuh svep du' etek vesh' getting pok tor trasha, heh lu i satau ne' zhit ik etek weren’t svi' au ar'kada tor nekwitaya ish-veh yut upstairs. Au vesh' amp hiyet tor stau me kuv i hadn’t var-tor ish-veh vi puma wuh poiq'lid. Ish-veh el'ru vesh' fi' wuh revolver svi' ish-veh abru'lik kanok minute au vesh' svi' wuh kelek—” au shau ska' defiantly. “ra kuv i did var-tor ish-veh? Ik katravahsu had ish-veh coming tor ish-veh. Au threw grazhiv vi' ish-veh bezhun aishan spo' au did svi' daisy’s, tonk'peh au vesh' wuh dulai veh. Au sahr-tor abru' myrtle spo' du’d sahr-tor abru' wuh dog heh worla kauk pehkau ish-veh poiq'lid.” tra' vesh' nothing i kupi leralmin, kaula wuh veh unutterable kla-min ik ish-veh wasn’t yeht. “heh kuv du nah-tor i didn’t ma t'nash-veh thresh t' suffering—glazhau la', lu i went tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru ik pa'ash heh gla-tor ik damn natuhn t' dog kreyla sitting tra' fi' wuh sideboard, i hayal-tor ne' heh maf-tor spo' wuh kan-bu. K' oekon ish-veh vesh' awful—” i couldn’t forgive ish-veh il spo' ish-veh, tonk'peh vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik ra au had ovsoh vesh', tor ish-veh, entirely justified. Ish-veh vesh' ek' maut careless heh confused. Au vesh' careless sutra, tom heh daisy—au smashed abru vel heh creatures heh yi retreated pla' vi' ish-veh donku il ish-veh vast carelessness, il whatever ish-veh vesh' ik potau au teretuhr, heh kal-tor vath sutra sok'i abru wuh mess au had tor … i hutau el'ru k' ish-veh; ish-veh seemed silly ri tor, na' i olau suddenly u' hi i vesh' talking tor wuh kan. Yi au went vi' wuh jewellery mahr-kel tor mahr-tor wuh pearl necklace—il sos'eh goh wuh shif t' cuff gonaf—rid t' t'nash-veh provincial squeamishness ek'wak. ------------------------------------------------------------------------ gatsby’s kelek vesh' fam dvun herbosh lu i losrak—wuh yar fi' ish-veh yartra had grown u' wu u' t'nash-veh. Veh t' wuh taxi yetursu svi' wuh pi'kahr worla nem-tor wuh panavau vesht wuh entrance temep rik' stopping na' wuh minute heh pointing svi'udish; sos'eh ish-veh vesh' au vi drove daisy heh gatsby abru' tor she'rak yu-mur wuh mu-yor t' wuh kisheya, heh sos'eh au had tor wuh var pa' ish-veh ek' ish-veh sha'. I didn’t aitlun tor zhu-tor ish-veh heh i nan'woi ish-veh lu i prah ska' wuh ranau. I spent t'nash-veh gad mu-yor svi' uzh york fai'ei eifa gleaming, dazzling parties t' ish-veh vesh' k' me ni vividly ik i kupi fam dvun zhu-tor wuh ralash-tanaf heh wuh laughter, faint heh incessant, s' ish-veh bah-ker, heh wuh poiq'lid going abru heh ne' ish-veh yetur. Veh mu-yor i did zhu-tor wuh tukh poiq'lid tra', heh gla-tor its ha'ge pehkaya na' ish-veh khom ash-tor. Tonk'peh i didn’t sasu-hil-tor. Probably ish-veh vesh' ein kim-shah be'hai'la vi had vesh' maf na' wuh shahtau t' wuh terra heh didn’t fai-tor ik wuh party vesh' abru'. Fi' wuh kim-shah mu-yor, k' t'nash-veh lap-fek sa'haf-tor heh t'nash-veh poiq'lid makau tor wuh grocer, i went abru' heh glazhau na' ik masuk' incoherent vravshaya t' wuh kelek wuh'wak weht. Fi' wuh wan-kur ash-tor wuh obscene zhit, scrawled k' ein sa-kan k' wuh krus t' dok, lam-tor si' clearly svi' wuh moonlight, heh i snishau ish-veh, bestan t'nash-veh ash'el raspingly bi' wuh kov. Yi i czar-tor ne' tor wuh shahov heh sprawled si' fi' wuh mazhiv. Danik t' wuh suk' gef shitau vesh' a'ing i' heh tra' vesh' hardly sovek ha'ge kaula wuh shadowy, dvun-tor min t' wuh mes-masu-hali mes' wuh ralash. Heh u' wuh aikum she-tor higher wuh inessential kelek began tor klimtau maf abi' gradually i became aware t' wuh hinek vikuvtra la' ik svai-tor wuh'wak na' dutch masusu’ bezhun—wuh sluk, yar-kur thasek t' wuh uzh panu. Its vanished lap, wuh lap ik had tor yut na' gatsby’s kelek, had wuh'wak pandered svi' zhal-tor tor wuh kim-shah heh greatest t' ek' komihn sahr-tor-tor; na' wuh transitory enchanted moment sasu bolau ma meskarau ish-veh esh svi' wuh la'es t' nash ek'kovtra, compelled vi' wuh aesthetic contemplation au neither ken-tor il aitlu, limuk tor limuk na' wuh kim-shah wak svi' vesht-var k' vel commensurate tor ish-veh tsoh na' wonder. Heh u' i hayal-tor tra' brooding fi' wuh hinek, ri-fainu panu, i nahp t' gatsby’s wonder lu au wuh'rak picked si' wuh yar-kur ta'hal na' wuh shaht t' daisy’s kif. Au had sarlah wuh wu yut tor nash pla-kur yartra, heh ish-veh sahr-tor bolau ma seemed ni ikap-tor ik au kupi hardly vravshau tor ruskaraya ish-veh. Au did ri fai-tor ik ish-veh vesh' already za' ish-veh, ein-wilat pla' svi' ik vast obscurity mesakh wuh kahr, wilat wuh gu'gelik vunai t' wuh republic padukau fi' ne' wuh mu-yor. Gatsby pudva-tor svi' wuh yar-kur ta'hal, wuh orgastic fa-wak ik tevun k' tevun satrasha fa' etek. Ish-veh savlau etek yi, tonk'peh ik’s rai tukh—fa-gad etek dungi sahr-tor faster, sakadaya si' etwel kar further … heh veh tok-ti asal— ni etek kuhsh-tor fi', masu-hali tehnat wuh current, borne pla' ceaselessly vi' wuh vesht.
